### [1] [Giant Magnetocrystalline Anisotropy in Honeycomb Iridate NiIrO3 with Large Coercive Field Exceeding 17 T](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04491)
*Chuanhui Zhu,Pengfei Tan,Xiao-Sheng Ni,Jingchun Gao,Yuting Chang,Mei-Huan Zhao,Zheng Deng,Shuang Zhao,Tao Xia,Jinjin Yang,Changqing Jin,Junfeng Wang,Chengliang Lu,Yisheng Chai,Dao-Xin Yao,Man-Rong Li*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究报道了首个具有耦合3d-5d磁性亚晶格的蜂窝状铱酸盐NiIrO3的合成与发现，该材料表现出长程亚铁磁序、超大磁晶各向异性能（32.2 meV/f.u.）和巨矫顽场（>17.3 T），为研究低维和受挫量子自旋系统提供了新平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在受挫和自旋轨道耦合材料中实现非常规量子相是量子材料研究的前沿。本研究旨在探索具有耦合3d-5d磁性亚晶格的蜂窝状铱酸盐体系，以发现新的量子相和物理特性。

Method: 通过软拓扑化学反应（soft topotactic reaction）合成NiIrO3，结合结构分析、综合磁性和电输运测量，以及实验与理论相结合的研究方法。结构分析揭示了具有Kitaev几何的钛铁矿型堆叠结构。

Result: NiIrO3在213 K以下表现出长程亚铁磁序（ferrimagnetic order），与已知蜂窝状铱酸盐的主要反铁磁序形成鲜明对比。该化合物显示出32.2 meV/f.u.的异常大磁晶各向异性能（magnetocrystalline anisotropy energy）和超过17.3 T的巨矫顽场（coercive field），均为铱酸盐中观测到的最高值之一。

Conclusion: NiIrO3的异常各向异性和矫顽性源于耦合3d-5d蜂窝晶格网络中的强晶格受挫（lattice frustration）与Ir4+（Jeff = 1/2）态的强自旋轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）之间的协同效应。该工作将NiIrO3定位为研究低维和受挫量子自旋系统的有前景平台，并突显了通过定向工程化3d-5d相互作用在自旋电子学（spintronic）应用中的潜力。

Abstract: The realization of unconventional quantum phases in frustrated and spin-orbit coupled materials remains at the forefront of quantum materials research. Here we report the synthesis and discovery of NiIrO3, the first honeycomb iridate with coupled 3d-5d magnetic sublattices, through a soft topotactic reaction. Structural analysis reveals an ilmenite-type stacking of edge-sharing NiO6 and IrO6 octahedral honeycomb sublattices in a Kitaev geometry. Comprehensive magnetic and electrical transport measurements unveil its long-range ferrimagnetic order below 213 K, which is in sharp contrast to the predominantly antiferromagnetic order in the known honeycomb iridates. Notably, the titled compound displays an exceptionally large magnetocrystalline anisotropy energy of 32.2 meV/f.u. and a giant coercivity with coercive field exceeding 17.3 T below 4.2 K, both ranking among the highest observed in iridates to date. Combined experimental and theoretical investigations indicate that the exceptional anisotropy and coercivity originate from the synergistic effect between strong lattice frustration in the coupled 3d-5d honeycomb lattice network and the robust spin-orbit coupling of the Ir4+ (Jeff = 1/2) state. This work positions NiIrO3 as a promising platform to investigate low-dimensional and frustrated quantum spin systems, and highlights its potential for spintronic applications through the targeted engineering of 3d-5d interactions.

</details>


### [2] [Thermodynamics of the ultrafast phase transition of vanadium dioxide](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04600)
*Shreya Bagchi,Ernest Pastor,José Santiso,Allan S. Johnson,Simon E. Wall*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究开发了一种基于温度依赖超快泵浦-探测测量的热力学框架，用于识别相变驱动机制，揭示了全热声子谱（特别是高频氧模式）的占据对于稳定金属相的必要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超快光激发是选择性控制相变的新兴途径，但难以确定哪些模式主导相变以及光激发如何有效靶向这些模式。以二氧化钒为例，其从单斜绝缘体到金红石金属的相变机制存在长期争议，涉及电子驱动与结构驱动、相干与非相干等核心问题。

Method: 研究开发了基于温度依赖超快泵浦-探测（temperature-dependent ultrafast pump-probe）测量的简单热力学框架，并与无微观细节建模进行对比，以识别相变的驱动机制。

Result: 分析揭示全热声子谱（full thermal phonon spectrum）的占据，特别是高频氧模式（high-frequency oxygen modes），对于稳定金属相是必要的。该方法能够确定相变本质，无需复杂多信使实验。

Conclusion: 该热力学框架可广泛应用于确定其他光诱导相变的本质，无需复杂多信使实验，并能指导新的控制策略，即使对于非相干相变也适用。

Abstract: Ultrafast photoexcitation is an emerging route to selective control of phase transitions. However, it is difficult to determine which modes govern the transformation and how effectively they are targeted by photoexcitation. This is exemplified in vanadium dioxide, which transitions from a monoclinic insulator to a rutile metal upon heating or photoexcitation. There is a long-standing debate about whether this transition is electronically or structurally driven and whether the structural component is coherent, driven by a single structural mode or thermal in nature. In this work, we develop a simple thermodynamic framework based on temperature-dependent ultrafast pump-probe measurements and contrast it to microscopic-detail-free modelling to identify the driving mechanism of the transition, revealing that population of the full thermal phonon spectrum, especially high-frequency oxygen modes, is necessary to stabilize the metallic phase. Our approach can straightforwardly be applied to determine the nature of other photoinduced phase transitions without the need for complex multi-messenger experiments and can guide new control strategies, even for incoherent transitions.

</details>


### [3] [Successive single-q and double-q orders in an anisotropic XY model on the diamond structure: a model for quadrupole ordering in PrIr$_2$Zn$_{20}$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04702)
*Kaito Sasa,Kazumasa Hattori*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究通过经典蒙特卡洛模拟分析了PrIr$_2$Zn$_{20}$在磁场下的四极矩有序，揭示了磁场与四极矩各向异性竞争导致的丰富相图，包括单-q态与双-q态之间的转换。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在分析PrIr$_2$Zn$_{20}$在磁场下的四极矩有序行为，特别是理解磁场与四极矩各向异性之间的竞争如何影响系统的相图拓扑结构。

Method: 采用基于金刚石结构上有效$Γ_3$四极矩模型的经典蒙特卡洛模拟，分析磁场平行于[001]方向时系统的相行为。

Result: 研究发现磁场与四极矩各向异性竞争导致丰富的相图，包括单-q态与双-q态之间的转换；同时揭示对称性允许的双二次型位点间相互作用（对应十六极矩相互作用）对再现实验观测的弱场拓扑结构至关重要。

Conclusion: 该研究成功解释了PrIr$_2$Zn$_{20}$在磁场下的复杂相行为，强调了十六极矩相互作用在决定系统弱场拓扑结构中的关键作用。

Abstract: Quadrupole ordering with the ordering wavevector at the L points in PrIr$_2$Zn$_{20}$ under magnetic fields is analyzed using classical Monte Carlo simulations based on an effective $Γ_3$ quadrupole model on the diamond structure. We demonstrate that competition between the magnetic field and quadrupole anisotropy leads to a rich phase diagram for magnetic fields applied parallel to [001], which includes switching between a single-q state and a double-q state. We also show that a symmetry-allowed biquadratic intersite interaction, corresponding to a hexadecapole interaction, is crucial for reproducing the weak-field topology observed in experiments.

</details>


### [4] [Orbital-Selective Spin-Orbit Mott Insulator in Fractional Valence Iridate La$_3$Ir$_3$O$_{11}$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04739)
*Kai Wang,Jun Yang,Chaoyang Kang,Weikang Wu,Wenka Zhu,Jianzhou Zhao,Yaomin Dai,Bing Xu*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 通过红外光谱和理论计算，揭示了La₃Ir₃O₁₁中强健的莫特绝缘态（Mott insulating state）的微观机制，该绝缘态源于结构畸变、自旋轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）和库仑相互作用（Coulomb interactions）的协同作用，导致在Jeff = 1/2能带中发生轨道选择性莫特转变（orbital-selective Mott transition）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 5d铱酸盐（iridates）因其强自旋轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）与库仑相互作用（Coulomb interactions）的结合，成为实现新奇关联电子态（correlated electronic states）的独特平台。研究旨在理解La₃Ir₃O₁₁这一1/3空穴自掺杂系统中非常规绝缘基态的起源。

Method: 采用红外光谱（infrared spectroscopy）实验手段，观察到Drude响应的崩溃和跨越莫特能隙（Mott gap）的尖锐激发。结合理论计算，分析了结构畸变、自旋轨道耦合和库仑相互作用对电子结构的协同影响。

Result: 实验证实La₃Ir₃O₁₁中存在强健的莫特绝缘态。理论计算表明，八面体畸变（octahedral distortion）和Ir-Ir二聚化（dimerization）分裂了t₂g轨道，使Jeff = 1/2能带趋向半填充（half-filling），而Jeff = 3/2能带远离半填充。库仑相互作用在Jeff = 1/2能带中诱导了轨道选择性莫特转变，同时在Jeff = 3/2能带中形成了带绝缘能隙（band-insulating gap）。

Conclusion: La₃Ir₃O₁₁中的非常规绝缘态是由结构畸变、自旋轨道耦合和电子关联（electron correlations）协同作用稳定形成的。该发现为设计和理解自旋轨道耦合铱酸盐的绝缘基态提供了新的见解。

Abstract: The combination of strong spin-orbit coupling and Coulomb interactions makes the $5d$ iridates a unique platform for realizing novel correlated electronic states. Here, utilizing infrared spectroscopy, we demonstrate that a robust Mott insulating state persists in the $1/3$-hole self-doped system La$_3$Ir$_3$O$_{11}$, evidenced by the collapse of the Drude response and the emergence of sharp excitations across the Mott gap. Our theoretical calculations reveal that the insulating behavior arises from the cooperative interplay of structural distortions, spin-orbit coupling, and Coulomb interactions. Specifically, octahedral distortion and Ir-Ir dimerization split the $t_{2g}$ orbitals, driving the $J_{\mathrm{eff}} = 1/2$ bands toward half-filling while keeping the $J_{\mathrm{eff}} = 3/2$ bands away from it. Consequently, electron correlations induce an orbital-selective Mott transition in the $J_{\mathrm{eff}} = 1/2$ bands, whereas a band-insulating gap develops in the $J_{\mathrm{eff}} = 3/2$ bands, thereby stabilizing the unconventional insulating state in La$_3$Ir$_3$O$_{11}$. These findings provide new insights into the design and understanding of the insulating ground state of spin-orbit-coupled iridates.

</details>


### [5] [Crystal growth and magnetic properties of spin-$1/2$ distorted triangular lattice antiferromagnet CuLa$_2$Ge$_2$O$_8$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05126)
*S. Thamban,C. Aguilar-Maldonado,S. Chillal,R. Feyerherm,K. Prokeš,A. J. Studer,D. Abou-Ras,K. Karmakar,A. T. M. N. Islam,B. Lake*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究合成了高质量CuLa₂Ge₂O₈单晶，表征其形成扭曲三角晶格的量子自旋-1/2 Cu²⁺离子体系，发现弱磁阻挫和低于1.14 K的长程磁有序，其磁结构为非共线反铁磁序而非传统120°序。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究CuLa₂Ge₂O₈这一形成扭曲三角晶格的量子自旋-1/2 Cu²⁺离子体系，旨在探索其晶体生长方法并表征其磁性质，特别是磁阻挫（magnetic frustration）行为和磁有序结构。

Method: 采用移动溶剂浮区法（traveling-solvent floating zone technique）生长大尺寸单晶，通过粉末X射线衍射（powder X-ray diffraction）、能量色散X射线分析（energy dispersive X-ray analysis）和劳厄衍射（Laue diffraction）表征相纯度和结晶质量，利用直流磁化率（dc-susceptibility）、磁化强度和热容测量研究磁性质，并通过中子粉末衍射（neutron powder diffraction）确定磁结构。

Result: 成功合成了高质量大尺寸单晶（4 mm×4 mm×10 mm），磁测量显示存在弱磁阻挫，长程磁有序发生在TN=1.14(1) K以下，中子衍射确定的磁结构为共格非共线反铁磁序（commensurate, noncollinear antiferromagnetic），不同于等边三角反铁磁体的120°序，有序矩位于bc平面，总有序矩为0.89(6) μB/Cu²⁺。

Conclusion: CuLa₂Ge₂O₈在扭曲三角晶格中表现出弱磁阻挫和独特的非共线反铁磁有序，其磁结构偏离传统三角反铁磁体的120°序，为研究几何阻挫（geometric frustration）系统中的磁有序提供了新案例。

Abstract: CuLa$_2$Ge$_2$O$_8$ forms a distorted triangular lattice of quantum spin-1/2 Cu$^{2+}$ ions. A crystal growth method was developed using the traveling-solvent floating zone technique resulting in the synthesis of a large single crystal (4 mm$\times$4 mm$\times$10 mm). The crystal was characterized with regard to phase purity and crystallinity using powder X-ray diffraction, energy dispersive X-ray analysis and Laue diffraction, and found to be of excellent quality. The magnetic properties were characterized using dc-susceptibility, magnetization, and heat capacity measurements which revealed weak magnetic frustration with long-range magnetic order occurring below $T_N=1.14(1)$~K. The magnetic structure determined using neutron powder diffraction is a commensurate, noncollinear antiferromagnetic, different from the 120$^{\circ}$ order of an equilateral triangular antiferromagnet. The ordered moments lie in the {\bf bc}-plane, with components $m_b=0.50(3)$~$μ_{B}$ and $m_c= 0.73(5)$~$μ_{B}$ along the {\bf b}- and {\bf c}-axes respectively, giving a total ordered moment of $M_{total}$= 0.89(6)$μ_{B}/$Cu$^{2+}$ at 20~mK.

</details>


### [6] [Higher harmonics in Mott-Hubbard insulators as sensors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05254)
*Abdelrahman Azab,Friedemann Queisser,Gulloo Lal Prajapati,Jan-Christoph Deinert,Ralf Schützhold*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究利用强耦合含时微扰理论分析Mott绝缘体和电荷转移绝缘体在振荡电场中的响应，推导高阶谐波电流的解析表达式，并证明这些谐波可编码自旋序和微观跃迁路径信息。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探索强关联材料在振荡电场下的响应特性，特别是高阶谐波电流如何反映材料的微观物理性质，为强关联材料表征提供新探针。

Method: 采用强耦合含时微扰理论（strong-coupling time-dependent perturbation theory），分析Mott绝缘体和电荷转移绝缘体（charge-transfer insulators）在振荡电场中的响应行为。

Result: 推导出高阶谐波电流（higher-harmonic currents）的解析表达式，证明这些谐波编码了自旋序（spin order）和微观跃迁路径（microscopic hopping pathways）的信息。

Conclusion: 高阶谐波可作为强关联材料（correlated materials）的有效探针，同时也能作为外加驱动场的传感器，为材料表征提供新手段。

Abstract: Using strong-coupling time-dependent perturbation theory, we study the response of Mott and charge-transfer insulators to an oscillating electric field. We derive analytical expressions for the resulting higher-harmonic currents and show that they encode information about spin order and microscopic hopping pathways. The results demonstrate that higher harmonics can serve as probes of correlated materials and as sensors of the applied driving field.

</details>

# hep-lat [[Back]](#toc)

### [7] [Constrained Symplectic Quantization: Disclosing the Deterministic Framework Behind Quantum Mechanics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05072)
*Martina Giachello,Francesco Scardino,Giacomo Gradenigo*

Main category: hep-lat

TL;DR: 本文介绍了约束辛量子化（constrained symplectic quantization）方法，解决了原始辛量子化框架的两个结构性问题，并通过量子谐振子模型验证了该方法能够有效采样实时量子可观测量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 原始辛量子化（symplectic quantization）框架存在两个结构限制：非相互作用极限定义不明确，以及其关联函数与费曼路径积分（Feynman path integral）生成的关联函数缺乏直接对应关系。需要解决这些问题以建立更完善的实时量子场论采样方法。

Method: 引入约束辛量子化，这是一种全纯重构（holomorphic reformulation）方法，其中场和作用量被解析延拓，并对本征时间哈密顿流（intrinsic time Hamiltonian flow）施加约束。这些约束选择稳定的确定性轨迹，并为相应的微正则测度（microcanonical measure）定义收敛的全纯积分回路。

Result: 在连续极限下，该方法在生成泛函层面与费曼路径积分建立了精确等价性，从而在本征时间关联函数（intrinsic time correlators）和实时格林函数（real-time Green functions）之间提供了直接联系。通过量子谐振子模型测试，数值结果与精确解在一、二点函数上一致，并重建了振荡传播子、离散能隙谱和本征态概率密度演化等实时特征。

Conclusion: 约束辛量子化能够采样实时量子可观测量，为超越欧几里得时间重要性采样（Euclidean-time importance sampling）提供了实用途径。数值测试为该方法的有效性提供了证据。

Abstract: Symplectic quantization is a functional approach to quantum field theory that allows sampling of quantum fluctuations directly in Minkowski space time by means of a generalized Hamiltonian dynamics in an extra time variable $τ$ which, at large times, samples a microcanonical ensemble. In a previous work we showed that, for an interacting scalar theory in 1+1 dimensions, this framework captures genuine real time features that are inaccessible to Euclidean simulations. That original formulation suffers from two structural limitations, an ill defined non interacting limit and the lack of a direct correspondence between its correlation functions and those generated by the Feynman path integral. To solve these problems we introduced constrained symplectic quantization, a holomorphic reformulation in which fields and action are analytically continued and constraints are imposed on the intrinsic time Hamiltonian flow. The constraints select stable deterministic trajectories and they define convergent holomorphic integration cycles for the corresponding microcanonical measure. In the continuum limit we establish exact equivalence with the Feynman path integral at the level of the generating functional, thus providing a direct link between intrinsic time correlators and real time Green functions. In this contribution, we apply the method to the quantum harmonic oscillator on a real-time 1-dimensional lattice. Testing various observables, we find agreement between numerical and exact results for one- and two-point functions, and we reconstruct characteristic real-time features such as an oscillatory propagator, the discrete energy-gap spectrum, and the evolution of eigenstate probability densities. These tests provide numerical evidence that constrained symplectic quantization can sample real-time quantum observables and offers a practical route beyond Euclidean-time importance sampling.

</details>


### [8] [Intrinsic Width of the flux tube in 2+1 dimensional Yang-Mills theories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05323)
*Lorenzo Verzichelli,Michele Caselle,Elia Cellini,Alessandro Nada,Dario Panfalone*

Main category: hep-lat

TL;DR: 该研究更新了(2+1)维SU(2)规范群杨-米尔斯理论中通量管（flux tube）本征宽度的结果，发现低温下宽度恒定，接近解禁闭温度（deconfinement temperature）时呈现增长趋势。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在确定(2+1)维SU(2)杨-米尔斯理论中通量管的本征宽度（intrinsic width），特别是探索其随温度变化的特性，以理解通量管结构的物理本质。

Method: 将本征宽度定义为通量管轮廓指数衰减尾部的特征长度尺度，通过检查宽温度范围内的数据，验证该长度与通量管长度无关，并利用Svetitsky-Yaffe映射（Svetitsky-Yaffe mapping）理解相变普适类（universality class）。

Result: 本征宽度在低温下保持恒定值，接近解禁闭温度时呈现增长趋势，这一行为可通过Svetitsky-Yaffe映射从相变普适类角度理解。

Conclusion: 通量管的本征宽度在低温区恒定，接近解禁闭相变时增长，其温度依赖特性可通过Svetitsky-Yaffe映射与相变普适类相关联，深化了对(2+1)维SU(2)杨-米尔斯理论中通量管结构的理解。

Abstract: We present our updated results on the intrinsic width of the profile of the flux tube in (2+1)-dimensional Yang-Mills theory with SU(2) gauge group. We identify the intrinsic width as the characteristic length scale of the exponentially decaying tails of the profile of the flux tube. Inspecting a broad range of temperature, we check that this length does not depend on the length of the flux tube. Our estimations of the intrinsic width show a constant value at low temperature and a growing trend approaching the deconfinement temperature that can be understood from the universality class of the phase transition via the Svetitsky-Yaffe mapping.

</details>

### [9] [The Inverse Micromechanics Problem given Dielectric Constants for Isotropic Composites with Spherical Inclusions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05460)
*Athindra Pavan,Swaroop Darbha,Bjorn Birgisson*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 本文提出使用凸优化（convex optimization）方法研究基于Eshelby模型的逆微力学（inverse micromechanics）问题，重点关注通过复合材料及其各组分介电常数确定微观结构信息。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索凸优化作为研究Eshelby基逆微力学问题的有效工具。传统正问题（forward problem）关注给定组分性质和微观结构信息时确定复合材料有效性质，而逆问题则关注给定复合材料及其所有组分性质时确定微观结构信息。

Method: 采用Eshelby-Mori-Tanaka模型处理各向同性复合材料中的球形夹杂物（spherical inclusions）。将逆问题表述为线性规划（Linear Programming）问题，并通过凸优化视角分析该问题及其重要变体。

Result: 成功解决了通过复合材料及其组分性质确定组分体积分数（volume fractions）的逆问题。展示了关于色散材料（dispersive materials）、测量噪声与获得体积分割质量之间关系的积极结果。

Conclusion: 凸优化为研究Eshelby基逆微力学问题提供了有前景的工具。论文讨论了凸优化在逆微力学中的应用范围，验证了该方法在确定复合材料微观结构信息方面的有效性。

Abstract: In this article, convex optimization is introduced as a promising tool to study Eshelby based inverse micromechanics problems. The focus is on inverse micromechanics using the Eshelby-Mori-Tanaka model given the dielectric constants of the composite material and of all of its components. The model is exactly the same for the conductivity properties as well. This choice of model is made since the model is fairly simple and has a closed form analytical solution for the case of spheroidal inclusions as well. The forward or direct micromechanics problem deals with the determination of effective properties of a composite material given the properties of its components and microstructural information. The focus is on isotropic composites and the distribution of inclusions is assumed to be such that this holds. The inverse micromechanics problem considered in this paper deals with the determination of microstructural information given the properties of the composite material and all of its components. Since in this paper, isotropy of the composite and only spherical inclusions are considered, the goal is to determine just volume fractions of the components of the composite material. The inverse problem is formulated as a Linear Programming problem and is solved. Before this, the inverse problem and certain important variants of it are examined through the lens of convex optimization. Lastly, promising results regarding the relationship between dispersive materials, noise in measurements, and quality of obtained volumetric splits are showcased. The scope of the use of convex optimization in inverse micromechanics is discussed.

### [10] [Evidence for Vortex Rings with Multiquantum Circulation in He II](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05387)
*Yiming Xing,Yousef Alihosseini,Sosuke Inui,Wei Guo*

Main category: cond-mat.other

TL;DR: 通过粒子追踪测速技术，在超流氦-4中发现了罕见的多量子涡旋环（multiquantum vortex rings）事件，这些事件挑战了多量子涡旋寿命短暂的传统认知。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统理论认为超流氦-4中的涡旋动力学已确立：环流量（circulation）以κ=h/m₄为单位量子化，多量子涡旋会迅速分裂为单量子细丝，涡旋环（vortex rings）在热准粒子散射耗散下加速收缩。然而，实验观测到的罕见事件与这一标准图景不符。

Method: 采用冻结氘示踪粒子的粒子追踪测速技术（particle tracking velocimetry），识别出与涡旋结合的粒子事件。通过测量运动学参数，并与涡旋细丝模拟（vortex-filament simulations）结果对比，分析观测现象的可能物理机制。

Result: 观测到一类具有收缩驱动涡旋环运动特征加速行为的事件，其运动学数据无法用单量子环解释，需要有效环流量nκ（n>1）。模拟表明紧密排列的单量子环束会迅速分散，而观测到的高速度下粒子持续陷获现象暗示了更深的核心陷获势阱，仅与真正的多量子核心一致。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明存在异常长寿命的多量子环（anomalously long-lived multiquantum rings），这一发现构成了显著的理论难题，需要超越现有范式进行专门审视。

Abstract: Quantized vortex dynamics in superfluid $^4$He (He~II) are widely regarded as well established: circulation is quantized in units of $κ=h/m_4$, vortices carrying more than one quantum are expected to split into singly quantized filaments, and vortex rings shrink while accelerating due to dissipation from thermal-quasiparticle scattering. Using particle tracking velocimetry with frozen deuterium tracers, we uncover rare vortex-bound particle events that disrupt this canonical picture. In a class of events exhibiting the acceleration characteristic of shrinkage driven vortex ring motion, the measured kinematics cannot be reconciled with a singly quantized ring. Instead, they require an effective circulation $nκ$ with $n>1$, directly challenging the standard expectation that multiquantum vortices are short lived. A more prosaic possibility is that the inferred $nκ$ arises from a bundle of closely spaced singly quantized rings, which could generate similar large-scale motion. However, this scenario is disfavored by vortex-filament simulations that show rapid bundle dispersion. Furthermore, the persistence of particle trapping at the observed high speeds suggests a much deeper core trapping potential, consistent only with a truly multiquantum core. Together, these results point to anomalously long-lived multiquantum rings, a striking puzzle that calls for dedicated scrutiny beyond the prevailing paradigm.

</details>

### [11] [Necessary conditions for the Markovian Mpemba effect](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04567)
*Ido Avitan,Roee Factor,David Gelbwaser-Klimovsky*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究为姆潘巴效应（Mpemba effect）建立了马尔可夫三能级系统的简单必要判据，并将其推广至N能级系统，揭示了该热力学异常现象的内在机制与系统谱特性要求。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 姆潘巴效应作为一种热力学异常现象，在多种系统中被实验观测到，但确定何种系统会展现此效应仍是一个开放性问题。研究旨在建立普适性判据以理解其机制并指导应用。

Method: 研究推导了马尔可夫三能级系统中姆潘巴效应的简单必要条件，这些条件基于跃迁速率，并可推广至N能级系统分析。通过多时间尺度热化过程解释该效应。

Result: 研究建立了判断系统是否展现姆潘巴效应的协议，基于最大熵原理排除了亚欧姆（sub-Ohmic）和欧姆（Ohmic）谱系统，这些系统广泛存在于物理化学现象中但不会出现该效应。

Conclusion: 该协议为确定姆潘巴效应的最小物理要求提供了清晰路径，有助于理解其内在机制，并可为实验、数值模拟及多样化应用识别相关参数。

Abstract: The Mpemba effect is a thermodynamic anomaly in which a system farther away in temperature from equilibrium thermalizes before one that is initially closer. The effect has been experimentally observed across a wide range of systems, including water, colloids, and trapped ions. It has recently been the focus of numerous studies aimed at understanding its mechanisms and developing multiple applications. Despite extensive work in the field, clearly determining which types of systems exhibit the Mpemba effect remains an open question. To address this, we derive simple necessary conditions on the transition rates for the Mpemba effect in a Markovian 3-level system and show that they can be applied to study the Mpemba effect in an N-level system. Multiple time scales govern thermalization in these systems. This allows the evolution to occur more quickly across larger temperature differences, explaining the Mpemba effect. We apply our protocol to evaluate which types of systems exhibit the Mpemba effect and, in doing so, explain why the Mpemba effect in Markovian systems remains a thermodynamic anomaly. In particular, due to the maximum entropy principle, our conditions allow us to discard the sub-Ohmic and Ohmic spectra. The latter describes a wide range of physical and chemical phenomena, which will not exhibit the Mpemba effect. Moreover, our results provide a clear path to determine the minimal physical requirements for the Mpemba effect, and we apply them to understand its underlying mechanisms better. Finally, our protocol could help identify relevant parameters for experiments, numerical simulations and diverse applications.

</details>


### [12] [Resolving Spurious Multifractality in Discrete Systems: A Finite-Size Scaling Protocol for MFDFA in the 2D Ising Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04609)
*Sebastian Jaroszewicz,Nahuel Mendez,Maria P. Beccar-Varela,Maria Cristina Mariani*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文解决了离散自旋模型中使用MFDFA方法时出现的"虚假多重分形"争议，通过建立严格的分析协议，证明二维伊辛模型的宽奇异性谱是有限尺寸效应，而随机键伊辛模型则展现出真正的多重分形行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多重分形去趋势波动分析（MFDFA）已成为表征复杂系统尺度不变性的标准工具，但其在离散自旋模型中的应用常因"虚假多重分形"报告而受到质疑，这些报告与已有理论相矛盾。本研究旨在解决这一争议。

Method: 通过建立严格的离散晶格快照分析协议，以二维伊辛模型为基准，将分析限制在正矩区域并进行系统性的有限尺寸标度（FSS）分析。同时对比随机键伊辛模型（RBIM）以验证方法的区分能力。

Result: 先前报道的宽奇异性谱是负矩区域（q<0）中由晶格离散效应主导的有限尺寸伪影。在热力学极限下，谱宽坍缩为零（Δα→0），准确恢复了伊辛普适类的单分形指数（α≈H≈0.875）。随机键伊辛模型则展现出真正的宽多重分形谱（Δα≈0.23）。

Conclusion: MFDFA多项式去趋势可作为唯象重整化群（renormalization group）滤波器，抑制解析背景场（无关算子）以分离奇异临界行为。这些结果定义了区分有限系统中清洁临界性和无序主导临界性的稳健方法。

Abstract: Multifractal Detrended Fluctuation Analysis (MFDFA) has emerged as a standard tool for characterizing scale invariance in complex systems, yet its application to discrete spin models is frequently marred by reports of ``spurious multifractality'' that contradict established theory. In this work, we resolve this controversy by establishing a rigorous protocol for the analysis of discrete lattice snapshots. Using the 2D Ising model as a benchmark, we demonstrate that the previously reported broad singularity spectra \cite{Ludescher2011} are finite-size artifacts dominated by lattice discreteness effects in the negative moment regime ($q<0$). By restricting the analysis to positive moments and performing a systematic Finite-Size Scaling (FSS) analysis, we show that the spectral width collapses to zero ($Δα\to 0$) in the thermodynamic limit. The method accurately recovers the monofractal exponent of the Ising universality class ($α\approx H \approx 0.875$), consistent with Conformal Field Theory. To validate the discriminatory power of this protocol, we contrast these findings with the Random Bond Ising Model (RBIM), showing that quenched disorder induces a genuine, broad multifractal spectrum ($Δα\approx 0.23$) that survives scaling. Furthermore, we propose a theoretical interpretation where the MFDFA polynomial detrending functions as a phenomenological Renormalization Group filter, suppressing analytic background fields (irrelevant operators) to isolate the singular critical behavior. These results define a robust methodology for distinguishing between clean and disorder-dominated criticality in finite systems.

</details>


### [13] [Dissipation-Reliability Tradeoff for Stochastic CMOS Bits in Series](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04658)
*Cathryn Murphy,Schuyler Nicholson,Nahuel Freitas,Emanuele Penocchio,Todd Gingrich*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种通过耦合多个CMOS单元形成链式结构来抑制比特翻转错误的技术，利用单元间相关性实现自然纠错，并通过张量网络方法量化了可靠性-功耗权衡关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: CMOS技术实现的比特易受热噪声影响而产生比特翻转错误（bit-flip errors）。虽然传统方法通过高偏置电压（bias voltage）可靠抑制这些错误，但植入式生物医学设备（implantable biomedical devices）的小型化和电路设计需求促使研究者寻求替代的低电压错误抑制策略。

Method: 研究提出将多个CMOS单元耦合形成链式结构（CMOS chains），利用单元间相关性实现自然纠错。采用张量网络（tensor networks）数值求解CMOS链的随机主方程（stochastic master equation），量化了传统稀疏矩阵方法难以处理的大规模系统的可靠性-功耗权衡。

Result: 计算结果表明，比特翻转错误的典型时间随偏置电压呈指数增长，但随链长呈亚指数增长。在固定低偏置电压下，CMOS链比单个CMOS单元具有更高的稳定性；然而，提高偏置电压是实现同等稳定性的更低功耗途径。

Conclusion: CMOS链结构在低电压下能有效提升比特稳定性，但通过增加偏置电压实现相同稳定性是更节能的方案。该研究为植入式设备等低功耗应用提供了错误抑制策略的量化分析框架。

Abstract: Physical instantiations of a bit of information are subject to thermal noise that can trigger unintended bit-flip errors. Bits implemented with CMOS technology typically operate in regimes that reliably suppress these errors with a large bias voltage, but miniaturization and circuit design for implantable biomedical devices motivate error suppression via alternative low-voltage strategies. We present and analyze an error-suppression technique that involves coupling multiple CMOS units into chains, introducing a natural error correction arising from inter-unit correlations. Using tensor networks to numerically solve a stochastic master equation for the CMOS chain, we quantify the reliability-dissipation tradeoff across system sizes that would be intractable with conventional sparse-matrix methods. The calculations show that the typical time for bit-flip errors scales exponentially with the bias voltage but subexponentially with the chain length. While a CMOS chain adds stability compared to a single CMOS unit for a fixed low bias voltage, increasing the bias voltage is a lower-dissipation route to equivalent stability.

</details>


### [14] [Disorder effects in Ising metamagnetic phase transition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04732)
*A. B. Acharyya,M. Acharyya*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 通过蒙特卡洛模拟研究随机淬火无序伊辛超磁体的热力学性质，分析非磁性杂质浓度和均匀分布淬火随机磁场对反铁磁相变的影响，发现相变温度随无序度增加而降低，并呈现特定的标度行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究随机淬火无序（randomly quenched disordered）伊辛超磁体（Ising metamagnet）的热力学性质，特别关注非磁性杂质（nonmagnetic impurity）和均匀分布淬火随机磁场（uniformly distributed quenched random magnetic field）对反铁磁相变（antiferromagnetic phase transition）的影响。

Method: 采用蒙特卡洛模拟（Monte Carlo simulations）方法，通过引入非磁性杂质或均匀分布淬火随机磁场实现无序，研究交错磁化强度（staggered magnetisation）和交错磁化率（staggered susceptibility）随温度的变化关系。

Result: 反铁磁相变温度随非磁性杂质浓度增加而线性降低，交错磁化强度呈现标度行为 $M_sp^b \sim (T-T_c)p^a$；相变温度也随随机磁场宽度增加而非线性降低，外推至零无序极限恢复三维纯伊辛反铁磁体的奈尔温度（Neel temperature）。

Conclusion: 无序（杂质浓度和随机磁场）显著抑制反铁磁相变，降低相变温度；系统在零无序极限下恢复纯系统的行为，验证了模拟方法的可靠性。

Abstract: The thermodynamics of randomly quenched disordered Ising metamagnet has been studied by Monte Carlo simulations. The disorder has been implemented either by inserting nonmagnetic impurity or by uniformly distributed quenched random magnetic field. The staggered magnetisation ($M_s$) (calculated from the sublattice magnetisation) and the corresponding staggered susceptibility ($χ$) are studied as functions of the temperature ($T$). The antiferromagnetic phase transition has been found while cooling the system from the high temperature paramagnetic phase. The transition temperature(or pseudocritical temperature ($T_c$)) has been found to decrease as the concentration ($p$) of nonmagnetic impurity increased. The nonmagnetic impurity dependent staggered magnetisation has been found to show the scaling behaviour $M_sp^b \sim (T-T_c)p^a$ (with $a \cong -0.95$, $b \cong 0.09$ and $T_c \cong 4.45$) obtained through the data collapse. The zero temperature staggered magnetisation ($M_s(0)$) has been found to decrease linearly. The critical temperature($T_c$) is showing a linear ($T_c=mp+c$) dependence with the concentration ($p$) of nonmagnetic impurity. The antiferromagnetic phase transition has been found to take place at lower temperature for the higher value of the width ($s$) of the uniformly distributed quenched random field. The critical temperature ($T_c$) has been found to show the nonlinear dependence ($T_c=a+bs+cs^2$) on the width ($s$) of the uniformly distributed random magnetic field. The extrapolation (both for $p \to 0$ and $s \to 0$) restores the Neel temperature of three dimensional pure Ising antiferromagnet.

</details>


### [15] [The Statistical Mechanics of Indistinguishable Energy States and the Glass Transition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04823)
*Shimul Akhanjee*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究探索了占据不可区分能态的粒子的统计力学，通过组合计数方法推导了高简并度下经典和量子粒子的精确分布函数，发现经典粒子表现出类似过冷液体的玻璃化转变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统统计力学通常将能级或态视为可区分的，通过独特的量子数或空间位置进行区分。本研究旨在探索占据不可区分能态的粒子的统计力学，填补这一理论空白。

Method: 采用组合计数问题的结果，推导了高简并度（high degeneracy levels）下经典和量子粒子的精确分布函数。该方法与传统统计力学在微观态处理上存在数学差异。

Result: 经典粒子表现出明确的玻璃化转变（glass transition），类似于过冷液体（supercooled liquids），在有限温度$T_K$以下构型熵（configurational entropy）消失。同时获得了量子粒子的相应分布函数。

Conclusion: 通过重新审视微观态的数学处理，本研究为不可区分能态系统的统计力学提供了新的理论框架，揭示了经典粒子系统中的玻璃化转变行为。

Abstract: The statistical mechanics of particles that populate indistinguishable energy states is explored. In particular, the mathematical treatment of the microstates differs from conventional statistical mechanics where the energy levels or states are universally treated as distinguishable, and differentiated by unique quantum numbers, or addressed by distinct spatial locations. Results from combinatorial counting problems are adapted to derive exact distribution functions for both classical and quantum particles at high degeneracy levels. Classical particles exhibit a definitive glass transition, similar to supercooled liquids where where the configurational entropy vanishes below a finite temperature $T_K$.

### [16] [A minimal electrostatic theory for the Seebeck coefficient in liquids](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04835)
*Wataru Kobayashi*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一个基于溶剂化熵的最小静电理论，用于解释液体中高达mV/K量级的塞贝克系数（Seebeck coefficient），并通过扩展玻恩方程（extended Born equation）定量重现实验观测值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 液体中的塞贝克系数常达到mV/K量级，但其微观起源因电解质系统的复杂性而尚不明确。需要建立简化的理论框架来揭示其物理机制。

Method: 提出了一个关注溶剂化熵（solvation entropy）的最小静电理论（minimal electrostatic theory）。使用包含温度依赖介电常数（temperature-dependent dielectric constant）的扩展玻恩方程（extended Born equation）进行分析。

Result: 该理论定量重现了实验观测到的塞贝克系数幅值。明确了增强液体塞贝克响应的关键因素：高电荷数（large valence）、小阳离子半径（small cationic radius）、低介电常数（small dielectric constant）以及大的dε/dT。

Conclusion: 基于溶剂化熵的静电理论成功解释了液体中大塞贝克系数的微观起源，并识别出影响其大小的关键物理参数，为理解和设计热电液体材料提供了理论指导。

Abstract: The Seebeck coefficient in liquids often reaches the mV/K range, yet its microscopic origin remains unclear due to the complexity of electrolyte systems. Here we propose a minimal electrostatic theory focusing on solvation entropy. Using the extended Born equation with temperature ($T$)-dependent dielectric constant ($\varepsilon$), we quantitatively reproduce the experimentally observed magnitude. The theory clarifies that large valence, small cationic radius, small dielectric constant, and large $\frac{d\varepsilon}{dT}$ are key factors for enhanced liquid Seebeck response.

### [17] [Diffusion disorder in the contact process](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04844)
*Valentin Anfray,Manisha Dhayal,Hong-Yan Shih,Thomas Vojta*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文研究了空间非均匀扩散对接触过程非平衡相变的影响，发现扩散无序会破坏清洁定向渗透临界点，使相变归属于与感染或治愈率无序相同的无限随机普适类。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究空间非均匀扩散对接触过程非平衡相变的影响。已知接触过程中的定向渗透临界点对均匀扩散项具有稳定性，但扩散率的淬火无序性影响尚不明确。

Method: 采用场论中的幂次计数分析扩散无序的相关性，并进行大规模蒙特卡洛模拟验证。同时开发了具有无限扩散率的有效模型，分析扩散无序如何转化为治愈率的有效无序。

Result: 扩散无序通过幂次计数在场论中显示为无关变量，但蒙特卡洛模拟表明其会破坏清洁定向渗透临界点。相变归属于与感染或治愈率无序相同的无限随机普适类。扩散无序在重整化下会生成标准的随机质量无序。

Conclusion: 扩散无序通过生成治愈率的有效无序而破坏清洁定向渗透临界点，这一机制在重整化群描述中表现为扩散无序生成随机质量无序。该机制可能适用于其他吸收态相变和非平衡相变。

Abstract: We study the effects of spatially inhomogeneous diffusion on the non-equilibrium phase transition in the contact process. The directed-percolation critical point in the contact process is known to be stable against the addition of a spatially uniform diffusion term. Correspondingly, we find quenched randomness in the diffusion rates to be irrelevant by power counting in the field-theory of the contact process. However, large-scale Monte Carlo simulations demonstrate that such diffusion disorder destabilizes the clean directed percolation critical point. Instead, the transition belongs to the same infinite-randomness universality class as the contact process with disorder in the infection or healing rates. To explain these results, we develop an effective model with an infinite diffusion rate; it shows that diffusion disorder generates an effective disorder in the healing rates. The same mechanism also appears in the field-theoretic description: Whereas diffusion disorder is irrelevant by power-counting, it generates standard random-mass disorder under renormalization. We discuss the validity of this mechanism for other absorbing state transitions and non-equilibrium phase transitions in general.

</details>


### [18] [Fluctuation-induced quadrupole order in magneto-electric materials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04987)
*Finja Tietjen,R. Matthias Geilhufe*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种基于复合序（composite order）的新视角来解释磁电材料中的四极矩有序（quadrupolar ordering），取代传统的竞争序（competing orders）解释框架，并推导了四极矩转变温度、临界各向异性及其与机械应变的耦合关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 磁电材料中观察到的超越偶极有序（dipolar ordering）进入多极有序（multipolar ordering）的相变现象，传统上使用竞争序和精确微观相互作用来解释。然而，本文旨在提出一种基于复合序的新解释框架。

Method: 提出从母相（parent phase）中涌现的复合序方法来解释磁或电偶极有序之上的四极矩有序。该方法包含了热涨落（thermal fluctuations）和对称性的影响，并分析了它们对四极矩序出现的作用。

Result: 推导出四极矩转变温度（quadrupolar transition temperature）和临界各向异性（critical anisotropy）的解析表达式，解释了四极矩序与机械应变（mechanical strain）的耦合关系，这些结果与实验观测一致。

Conclusion: 从竞争序到复合序的视角转变具有普适性，可扩展到其他类型的多极有序。这种方法为理解相关相变的可调谐性和材料特异性预测提供了可能性，无需明确的微观机制知识。

Abstract: Phases that go beyond dipolar ordering and into multipolar ordering have recently been observed in magneto-electric materials. The resulting phase diagram is commonly explained using the concept of competing orders and exact microscopic interactions. In contrast, we propose an approach based on composite order emerging from a parent phase to explain quadrupoling above magnetic or electric dipolar orders. We include thermal fluctuations and symmetry and show their influence on the emergence of quadrupolar order. We find an analytical expression for the quadrupolar transition temperature, the critical anisotropy and explain the coupling of the quadrupolar order to mechanical strain, in agreement with experiments. The shift in perspective on quadrupolar ordering from competing to composite order is universal and can be extended to other types of multipolar ordering. This offers the possibility of understanding tunability and material-specific predictions of the related phase transitions without explicit knowledge of the microscopic mechanisms.

</details>


### [19] [Fokker-Planck description of an active Brownian particle with rotational inertia](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05074)
*Lingyi Wang,Ziluo Zhang,Zhongqiang Xiong,Zhanglin Hou,Linli He,Shigeyuki Komura*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究开发了一种微扰框架来计算具有有限转动惯量的活性布朗粒子（ABPs）的均方位移（MSD）。通过傅里叶变换和厄米多项式展开，系统性地推导出MSD的解析表达式，并与数值模拟结果进行了验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于建立计算具有有限转动惯量的活性布朗粒子（active Brownian particles, ABPs）均方位移（mean-squared displacement, MSD）的理论框架。现有方法通常忽略转动惯量的影响，而本研究旨在系统性地处理这一物理参数。

Method: 方法基于相应的福克-普朗克方程（Fokker-Planck equation），采用空间坐标的傅里叶变换（Fourier transform）和角速度的厄米多项式（Hermite polynomials）作为本征函数。通过微扰展开（perturbative expansion）在拉普拉斯空间（Laplace space）中对级数进行重整化（resumming），并进行逆变换得到MSD的解析表达式。

Result: 研究获得了均方位移（MSD）作为转动惯量函数的显式解析表达式。通过将理论结果与数值模拟（numerical simulations）进行比较，验证了该微扰框架的准确性和有效性。

Conclusion: 该研究成功开发了计算具有有限转动惯量的活性布朗粒子（ABPs）均方位移（MSD）的微扰框架。该方法提供了系统性的理论处理手段，并通过数值验证证实了其可靠性，为相关活性物质系统的动力学研究提供了新的分析工具。

Abstract: We develop a perturbative framework to calculate the mean-squared displacement (MSD) of active Brownian particles (ABPs) with a finite moment of inertia. Starting from the corresponding Fokker-Planck equation, we employ a Fourier transform for the spatial coordinates and Hermite polynomials as eigenfunctions for the angular velocity, which enables a systematic perturbative expansion of the MSD order by order. By resumming the resulting series in Laplace space and performing the inverse transform, we obtain an explicit expression for the MSD as a function of the moment of inertia. The analytical results are further validated by comparison with numerical simulations.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究采用基于可逆变换的生成模型（Boltzmann Generators），该模型能够直接从玻尔兹曼分布（Boltzmann distribution）中采样平衡构型。研究聚焦于Lennard-Jones流体的液-气临界点（liquid-gas critical point），评估模型在临界区域及邻近相图状态的表现。

Result: Boltzmann Generators能够捕捉临界行为（critical behavior）的基本特征，在临界点或临界点附近训练时保持可靠性能，并能外推到相图的邻近状态。一个有趣的观察是模型的效率指标紧密追踪底层相边界，暗示生成性能与热力学之间存在联系。然而，方法受限于当前可访问的小系统尺寸，这些尺寸抑制了表征临界现象的大涨落。

Conclusion: 研究结果界定了Boltzmann Generators在相空间挑战性区域的当前能力和边界，同时指出了未来在慢动力学主导问题（如玻璃形成和成核）中的应用方向。尽管模型在临界区域表现出潜力，但系统尺寸限制仍是当前主要制约因素。

Abstract: Generative models based on invertible transformations provide a physics-aware route to sample equilibrium configurations directly from the Boltzmann distribution, enabling efficient exploration of complex thermodynamic landscapes. Here, we evaluate their applicability in regions where conventional simulations suffer from severe dynamical bottlenecks, focusing on the liquid-gas critical point of a Lennard-Jones fluid. We show that Boltzmann Generators capture essential signatures of critical behavior, retain reliable performance when trained at or near criticality, and extrapolate across neighboring states of the phase diagram. An intriguing observation is that the model's efficiency metric closely traces the underlying phase boundaries, hinting at a connection between generative performance and thermodynamics. However, the approach remains limited by the small system sizes currently accessible, which suppress the large fluctuations that characterize critical phenomena. Our results delineate the current capabilities and boundaries of Boltzmann Generators in challenging regions of phase space, while pointing toward future applications in problems dominated by slow dynamics, such as glass formation and nucleation.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了一种新颖的估计器，仅依赖于检测单个粒子在连续空间中离开或进入区域，或穿越流形的事件。该估计器基于此类事件之间转换的频率和持续时间，通过引入两种空间离散化（discretization of space）方法推导得出。

Conclusion: 该方法为连续系统中有限分辨率观测下的熵产生估计提供了新途径，克服了现有方法对马尔可夫事件检测或离散动力学假设的依赖。通过空间离散化策略，建立了基于粒子穿越事件的实际可观测量的估计框架。

Abstract: Estimating entropy production in continuous systems that can only be observed with a limited resolution remains an open problem in stochastic thermodynamics. Extant estimators based on the measurement of waiting-time distributions require either the detection of Markovian events, which uniquely determine the state of the system, or assume a discrete underlying dynamics. We present a novel estimator that relies solely on the detection of a single particle leaving or entering regions, or crossing manifolds, in continuous space. This estimator is based on the frequency and the duration of transitions between such events. We derive this bound by introducing two kinds of discretization of space. Finally, we compare our novel bound to the TUR using simulations of a Brownian vortex and discuss its relation to other lower bounds to entropy production.

### [22] [The bliss of dimensionality: how an unsupervised criterion identifies optimal low-resolution representations of high-dimensional datasets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05214)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高维数据离散化中分辨率选择是一个核心问题，特别是在无监督设置下底层分布未知时。需要验证相关性-分辨率（Relevance-Resolution, Res-Rel）框架的信息论权衡方法是否与基于真实分布的最优离散化一致。

Method: 研究通过比较Res-Rel框架的两个特征最优准则——最大相关性（maximum relevance）和-1斜率点（-1 slope point），与基于已知或物理动机真实分布的Kullback-Leibler（KL）散度最小化离散化。测试数据集包括非结构化和结构化合成数据、MNIST的高斯克隆以及丙氨酸二肽（alanine dipeptide）的分子动力学模拟。

Conclusion: 研究确立了无监督信息论选择与基于分布的最优性之间的定量一致性，为高维数据离散化中分辨率选择提供了理论验证。

Abstract: Selecting the optimal resolution for discretizing high-dimensional data is a central problem in physics and data analysis, particularly in unsupervised settings where the underlying distribution is unknown. The Relevance-Resolution (Res-Rel) framework addresses this issue through an information-theoretic trade-off between descriptive detail and statistical reliability. Here we provide a systematic validation of this approach by comparing its characteristic optima--maximum relevance and the -1 slope (information-theoretic) point--with the discretization that minimizes the Kullback-Leibler divergence from a known or physically motivated ground truth distribution. Across unstructured and structured synthetic datasets, Gaussian clones of MNIST, and molecular dynamics simulations of the alanine dipeptide, we find that as the dimensionality or informative content increases the KL-optimal discretization consistently lies within the Res-Rel optimality region. Furthermore, in high-dimensional regimes the -1 slope criterion closely matches the KL divergence minimum. These results establish the quantitative consistency of unsupervised information-theoretic selection with distribution-based optimality.

### [23] [Dynamical quantum phase transitions through the lens of mode dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05284)
*Akash Mitra,Shashi C. L. Srivastava*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在理解动量空间中突然淬火协议下一般二次费米子哈密顿量的模式动力学特性，特别是探索零能模式与动力学量子相变（dynamical quantum phase transition, DQPT）之间的关系。

Method: 采用动量空间中的突然淬火（sudden quench）协议，研究一般二次费米子哈密顿量的模式动力学。重点关注任意时间t的零能模式，特别是其中自旋翻转对称性（spin-flip symmetry）恢复的特定零能模式。

Result: 研究发现，零能模式的出现是动力学量子相变（DQPT）的必要但不充分条件。特定零能模式中的自旋翻转对称性恢复定义了DQPT，且这种对称性恢复的条件与速率函数发散和动力学拓扑序参量的整数跃迁条件相同。

Conclusion: 自旋翻转对称性恢复为动力学量子相变（DQPT）提供了新的定义视角，统一了传统DQPT标识符（速率函数发散和拓扑序参量整数跃迁）。该视角还能自然解释DQPT和基态量子相变（ground-state quantum phase transitions）的发生条件。

Abstract: We study the mode dynamics of a generic quadratic fermionic Hamiltonian under a sudden quench protocol in momentum space. Modes with zero energy at any given time, $t$, are referred to as dynamical critical modes. Among all zero-energy modes, spin-flip symmetry is restored in the eigenvector corresponding to selected zero-energy modes. This symmetry restoration is used to define the dynamical quantum phase transition (DQPT). This shows that the occurrence of these dynamical critical modes is necessary but not sufficient for a DQPT. We show that the conditions on the quench protocol and time for such dynamical symmetry restoration are the same as the divergence of the rate function and integer jump in the dynamical topological order parameter, which have been the traditional identifiers of a DQPT. This perspective also naturally explains when one or both of DQPT and ground-state quantum phase transitions will occur.

### [24] [Finite-size scaling in quasi-3D stick percolation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05374)
*Ryan K. Daniels*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本研究将连续渗流（continuum percolation）的普适有限尺寸标度（universal finite-size scaling）框架从二维（2D）扩展到准三维（Q3D）棒状系统，通过蒙特卡洛模拟（Monte Carlo simulation）确定了各向同性Q3D棒状系统的渗流阈值（percolation threshold），并证明其与二维连续渗流和晶格渗流（lattice percolation）遵循相同的普适标度函数（universal scaling function）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于将连续渗流的普适有限尺寸标度框架从二维系统扩展到准三维棒状系统，其中有限直径的导线（wires）在平坦基底上垂直堆叠。这有助于理解三维几何结构对渗流行为的影响。

Method: 采用蒙特卡洛模拟方法，研究准三维棒状系统中顺序沉积（sequentially deposited）的导线。通过模拟确定各向同性Q3D棒状系统的渗流阈值，并分析导线直径与长度比（d/l）对阈值的影响。

Result: 模拟结果显示，Q3D棒状系统的渗流阈值为$N_c l^2 = 6.850923 \pm 0.00014$，比已建立的二维值$5.6373$高出约$21.5\%$。阈值与导线直径长度比$d/l$无关，反映了顺序沉积下接触拓扑（contact topology）的尺度不变性（scale invariance）。

Conclusion: 通过引入非普适度量因子（nonuniversal metric factor），Q3D棒状渗流在具有自由边界条件（free boundary conditions）的方形系统中的跨越概率（spanning probability）与二维连续渗流和晶格渗流落在相同的普适标度函数上。这为Q3D棒状渗流与二维棒状渗流和晶格渗流遵循相同普适标度函数提供了实证证据。

Abstract: This work extends the universal finite-size scaling framework for continuum percolation from two-dimensional (2D) to quasi-three-dimensional (Q3D) stick systems, in which sequentially deposited wires of finite diameter stack vertically on a flat substrate. Using Monte Carlo simulation, the percolation threshold is determined for isotropic Q3D stick systems as $N_c l^2 = 6.850923 \pm 0.00014$, approximately $21.5\%$ above the established 2D value of $5.6373$. The threshold is shown to be independent of the wire diameter-to-length ratio $d/l$, reflecting the scale invariance of the contact topology under sequential deposition. Simulation results indicate that, as with 2D networks, by introducing a nonuniversal metric factor, the spanning probability of Q3D stick percolation on square systems with free boundary conditions falls on the same universal scaling function as that for 2D continuum and lattice percolation. This provides substantiating evidence that Q3D stick percolation falls on the same universal scaling function as that for 2D stick percolation and lattice percolation.

### [25] [Extreme Values of Infinite-Measure Processes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05390)
*Talia Baravi,Eli Barkai*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了在无限遍历理论（infinite ergodic theory）框架下，非平稳但循环系统的极值统计特性。研究发现，这类系统的极值统计由返回指数（return exponent）α和无限不变测度（infinite invariant measure）控制，偏离了经典的Fréchet、Gumbel和Weibull普适性类别。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于理解非平稳但循环系统的极值统计特性，这类系统在长时间极限下由非归一化的无限不变密度（infinite invariant density）描述。传统极值统计理论无法直接应用于此类系统，需要新的理论框架。

Method: 研究方法基于无限遍历理论，在观测时间t很长且变量数量N很大的联合极限下分析极值统计。理论框架通过返回指数α和无限不变测度来描述极值分布，并在三个具体系统中进行验证：弱混沌间歇映射（weakly chaotic intermittent maps）、渐近平坦势中的过阻尼扩散（overdamped diffusion in an asymptotically flat potential）以及亚反冲激光冷却的随机模型（stochastic model of sub-recoil laser cooling）。

Result: 研究结果表明，无限遍历系统中的极值统计由返回指数α和无限不变测度控制，显著偏离了经典的Fréchet、Gumbel和Weibull普适性类别。极值测量可用于推断系统的无限密度结构，为理解这类非平稳系统的统计特性提供了新方法。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了无限遍历系统中极值统计的新理论框架，证明了极值统计特性由返回指数和无限不变测度决定，而非经典普适性分布。极值测量可作为探测无限密度结构的有效工具，为研究非平稳循环系统的统计特性开辟了新途径。

Abstract: We study the statistics of the maximum and minimum of a set of $N$ random variables whose dynamical and statistical properties fall within the scope of infinite ergodic theory. These non-stationary yet recurrent systems are described, in the long-time limit, by a non-normalizable infinite invariant density. Extreme events in such systems emerge in a joint limit where the observation time $t$ is long and the number of variables $N$ is large. We show that the resulting extreme value statistics are controlled by the return exponent $α$ and the infinite invariant measure, and therefore depart from the classical Fréchet, Gumbel, and Weibull universality classes. We illustrate the theory for weakly chaotic intermittent maps, overdamped diffusion in an asymptotically flat potential, and a stochastic model of sub-recoil laser cooling, and show how measurements of extremes can be used to infer the infinite-density structure.

</details>

### [26] [Reheating after Starobinsky Inflation in the Jordan Frame](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04497)
*Gláuber C. Dorsch,Luiz Carlos Miranda,Nelson Yokomizo*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了Jordan框架下Starobinsky模型中的引力再加热（gravitational reheating），其中暴胀由$R^2$引力修正驱动而无显式暴胀子场。研究表明，Ricci标量振荡通过引力粒子产生实现再加热，最终温度约为$2\times10^9$ GeV。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究Starobinsky模型中引力再加热的机制，特别是在Jordan框架下，暴胀由$R^2$引力修正驱动而无显式暴胀子场的情况。探讨引力粒子产生作为再加热机制的可行性及其与经典等效框架的差异。

Method: 在Jordan框架下分析暴胀后背景演化，显示修正引力动力学产生的有效流体在振荡阶段表现为无压物质。通过求解耦合的背景方程和Boltzmann方程，并考虑产生粒子的反作用（backreaction），研究Ricci标量振荡的指数阻尼效应。

Result: 发现Ricci标量振荡获得指数阻尼，一致地终止粒子产生。通过求解耦合方程得到再加热温度$T_{\mathrm{reh}} \sim 2 \times 10^{9}$ GeV。比较Jordan和Einstein框架描述，发现尽管经典等效，但考虑量子效应时可能导致不同的微观物理解释和定量预测。

Conclusion: Starobinsky模型在Jordan框架下可通过纯引力机制实现再加热，无需引入显式暴胀子场。Ricci标量振荡驱动的引力粒子产生能有效实现再加热，温度达$10^9$ GeV量级。不同框架的经典等效性在考虑量子效应时可能被破坏，导致不同的物理预测。

Abstract: We investigate gravitational reheating in the Starobinsky model in the Jordan frame, where inflation is driven by an $R^2$ modification of gravity with no explicit inflaton field. In this description, reheating proceeds exclusively through gravitational particle production triggered by the oscillations of the Ricci scalar after the end of inflation. We analyze the post-inflationary background evolution and show that an effective fluid emerging from the modified gravitational dynamics behaves as pressureless matter during the oscillatory phase. Including the backreaction of the produced particles, we demonstrate that the Ricci scalar oscillations acquire an exponential damping, consistently terminating particle production. Solving the coupled background and Boltzmann equations, we obtain a reheating temperature $T_{\mathrm{reh}} \sim 2 \times 10^{9}$ GeV. We finally compare the Jordan and Einstein frame descriptions and argue that, although classically equivalent, they can lead to distinct microphysical interpretations and quantitative predictions for reheating once quantum effects are taken into account.

</details>


### [27] [Nonlinear Dynamics in General Relativity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04501)
*Vitor Cardoso,Jaime Redondo-Yuste,Ulrich Sperhake,Furkan Tuncer*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了广义相对论中新的非线性效应，包括高阶谐波产生、频谱展宽和聚焦现象，这些效应有助于解释黑洞合并的平滑行为，但也警示对引力波波形的简化解释需谨慎。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 黑洞和引力波是爱因斯坦方程非线性特性的结果，但广义相对论的显著性质暗示存在其他效应。本研究旨在揭示引力理论中新的非线性方面。

Method: 研究在爱因斯坦-克莱因-戈登（Einstein-Klein-Gordon）系统中建立了高阶谐波产生、频谱展宽和聚焦现象。在真空中，证明了单色波在二次阶散射中对频率的弱敏感性，特别是在大波长条件下。

Result: 发现了引力理论中新的非线性效应，包括高阶谐波产生（higher harmonic generation）、频谱展宽（spectral broadening）和聚焦（focusing）。这些效应表明在二次阶散射中，大波长单色波的散射对频率变化不敏感。

Conclusion: 这些新发现的非线性效应既能解释黑洞合并看似平滑的行为，也警示我们避免对引力波波形（waveforms）进行过于简化的解释。研究强调了引力理论中复杂非线性相互作用的重要性。

Abstract: Black holes and gravitational waves are consequences of the nonlinear character of the Einstein equations. Yet, the remarkable properties of General Relativity point to the existence of other effects. Here we uncover new nonlinear facets of gravity. We establish higher harmonic generation, spectral broadening and focusing in the Einstein Klein-Gordon system. In vacuum, we show that scattering of monochromatic waves at quadratic order is weakly sensitive to frequency, at large wavelengths. These aspects can both explain the seemingly smooth behavior of mergers, but also caution us against too simplistic an interpretation of waveforms.

</details>

Result: 提供了关于狭义相对论（Special Relativity）数学方面的全面论述，特别是洛伦兹群（Lorentz group）的详细数学处理。手稿包含已出版书籍的内容，并增加了附录以补充或扩展相关主题。

Conclusion: 该专著为狭义相对论（Special Relativity）的数学基础提供了系统而严谨的阐述，特别强调洛伦兹群（Lorentz group）的核心作用。通过整合力学和电动力学（electrodynamics）中的相对论变换（relativistic transformations），建立了完整的数学框架。

### [29] [Cosmological black holes in the inflationary epoch](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04590)
*Ertola Urtubey Milos,Daniela Pérez*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了暴胀时期黑洞的演化，假设它们通过广义McVittie几何与宇宙背景动态耦合，使得引力质量随宇宙尺度因子变化。采用Starobinsky的$\mathcal{R}^2$暴胀模型，分析了宇宙耦合、霍金蒸发和辐射吸积在暴胀、辐射、物质和暗能量时期的综合效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机是探索暴胀时期形成的黑洞在宇宙演化过程中的命运，特别是考虑它们通过广义McVittie几何与宇宙背景动态耦合的情况。这种耦合使得黑洞的引力质量随宇宙尺度因子变化，从而影响其在后续宇宙时期的演化。

Method: 采用Starobinsky的$\mathcal{R}^2$暴胀模型，分析黑洞在暴胀、辐射、物质和暗能量时期的演化。通过要求黑洞事件视界始终小于粒子视界来获得质量参数的上限，同时考虑辐射吸积和霍金蒸发效应来约束参数空间。

Result: 研究发现，辐射时期的辐射吸积进一步约束了参数空间以防止失控增长，而霍金蒸发设定了初始质量的下限以确保黑洞能存活过暴胀期。只有暴胀时期形成的、初始质量处于狭窄范围内的黑洞才能持续存在至今，最大质量可达$M(t_0) \simeq 1.043\times10^{-3} M_\odot$。

Conclusion: 结论表明，在广义McVittie几何框架下，暴胀时期形成的黑洞只有在特定初始质量范围内才能存活至今，这为早期宇宙黑洞的观测提供了理论约束。最大质量约为$1.043\times10^{-3}$太阳质量的黑洞可能存在于当前宇宙中。

Abstract: We investigate the evolution of black holes present during the inflationary epoch, assuming they are dynamically coupled to the cosmological background through a generalized McVittie geometry, such that their gravitational mass scales with the cosmic scale factor. Adopting Starobinsky's $\mathcal{R}^2$ inflation model, we analyse the combined effects of cosmological coupling, Hawking evaporation and radiation accretion during the subsequent cosmic eras: inflation, radiation, matter, and dark energy. Requiring the black hole event horizon to remain smaller than the particle horizon at all times yields an upper bound on the mass parameter. Radiation accretion during the radiation era further constrains the parameter space to prevent runaway growth. Hawking evaporation sets a lower bound on the initial mass to ensure survival through inflation. We find that only black holes formed within a narrow initial mass range during inflation can persist to the present day, reaching a maximum mass of $M(t_0) \simeq 1.043\times10^{-3} M_\odot$.

### [30] [Junction Conditions for General Gravitational Theories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04645)
*José M. M. Senovilla*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文基于分布形式主义（distributional formalism）推导了依赖于曲率标量不变量（包括微分不变量）任意函数的广义引力理论的连接条件（junction conditions）。研究获得了薄壳（thin shells）存在时的壳能量-动量一般表达式，并推导了广义Israel条件以及无壳时的适当匹配条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于建立基于曲率标量不变量任意函数的广义引力理论的连接条件。这些理论包括依赖于曲率标量不变量（包括微分不变量）的拉格朗日密度，需要系统性地推导其匹配条件以理解薄壳和引力双层的存在条件。

Method: 研究方法采用分布形式主义（distributional formalism）来处理广义引力理论中的不连续性。该方法系统地处理拉格朗日密度中出现的最高阶导数，从而推导出连接条件和壳能量-动量表达式。

Result: 主要结果包括：(i) 当黎曼张量的m阶协变导数在匹配超曲面连续时出现薄壳，其中m是拉格朗日密度中出现的最高阶；(ii) 无薄壳的适当连接需要(m+1)阶导数也连续；(iii) m=0且曲率标量不变量二次的理论是特殊的，允许黎曼张量不连续性导致薄壳和引力双层（gravitational double layers）；(iv) 广义相对论和F(R)理论是特殊的，允许曲率壳（即脉冲引力波）。

Conclusion: 结论表明广义引力理论的连接条件强烈依赖于拉格朗日密度中的最高导数阶数。研究推导了薄壳存在的一般条件，并识别了允许曲率不连续性的特殊理论类别，包括广义相对论和F(R)理论。所有结果基于与物质的最小耦合推导，但方法可推广到更一般的耦合情形。

Abstract: The junction conditions for general theories of gravity based on actions that depend on arbitrary functions of the curvature scalar invariants (including differential invariants) are obtained using the distributional formalism. In case of the existence of thin shells, a general expression for the shell energy-momentum is presented. The generalized Israel conditions are also obtained. The conditions for a proper matching, without shells, are also derived. The main results are: (i) shells arise if the $m$th-covariant derivative of the Riemann tensor is continuous at the matching hypersurface, where $m$ is the maximum order appearing in the Lagrangian density; (ii) a proper junction without thin shells requires further that the $(m+1)$-th derivative be also continuous, (iii) theories with $m=0$ that are quadratic in the scalar curvature invariants are special and unique for they allow for discontinuities of the Riemann tensor resulting in the existence of {\em thin shells and gravitational double layers} and (iv) General Relativity and $F(R)$ theories are extraordinary theories that admit shells of curvature (i.e. impulsive gravitational waves) because other theories require the absence of jumps of the second fundamental form across the matching hypersurface. All results are derived for a minimal coupling with the matter, but the strategy would be analogous for more general couplings.

</details>


### [31] [Going into a tailspin near the abyss: analytic solutions for spinning particles on near equatorial, plunging orbits in Kerr spacetime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04682)
*Gabriel Andres Piovano*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 首次提出克尔时空（Kerr spacetime）中近赤道自旋测试粒子（spinning test-particle）坠入运动的解析解，涵盖所有能量E<1的坠入轨道类型，为自旋力（self-force）方法和黑洞微扰理论（black hole perturbation theory）的波形建模提供工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为自旋力方法和黑洞微扰理论中的旋近-合并-环降（inspiral-merger-ringdown）波形建模提供解析工具，解决克尔时空中自旋测试粒子坠入运动的解析描述问题。

Method: 在粒子自旋的小参数一阶近似下求解运动方程，提出新颖的类开普勒参数化（Keplerian-like parametrization）方法，并推导轨道平面进动（precession）的解析表达式。

Result: 首次获得所有能量E<1的坠入轨道（plunging orbits）的解析解，包含粒子自旋引起的轨道平面进动效应，并以闭合形式给出了最内束缚圆轨道（innermost bound circular orbit）半径的修正。

Conclusion: 提出的解析解和参数化方法将有效支持自旋力方法和黑洞微扰理论中的波形建模，为研究克尔黑洞附近自旋粒子的动力学行为提供了新的解析工具。

Abstract: This work presents, the first time, analytic solutions for the nearly equatorial, plunging motion of a spinning test-particle in Kerr spacetime. The equations of motion are solved at first-order in the small-body spin for all classes of plunging orbits with energy $E < 1$. The solutions incorporate the small precession of the orbital plane caused by the precession of the particle's spin. Additionally, we present the correction to the radius of the innermost bound circular orbit in closed form, and introduce a novel, Keplerian-like parametrization for generic plunging orbits. Our solutions will be useful in the modelling of inspiral-merger-ringdown waveforms with self-force methods and black hole perturbation theory.

### [32] [Inflation in fractional Newtonian cosmology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04712)
*S. M. M. Rasouli*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在分数阶牛顿宇宙学框架下研究早期宇宙演化，通过构建合适的分数阶势能，展示宇宙演化可从非奇异暴胀前状态自然产生，并发现暴胀相作为稳定动力学吸引子出现，同时解决了视界问题并实现了优雅退出。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索分数阶牛顿宇宙学（fractional Newtonian cosmology）框架下早期宇宙的演化过程，特别是如何从非奇异暴胀前状态自然过渡到暴胀相，并解决相关的宇宙学问题。

Method: 方法包括构建合适的分数阶势能（fractional potential），分析宇宙演化动力学，特别关注过渡时间附近的动力学行为，并确定力零点与暴胀结束点之间的微小分离。

Result: 研究发现存在自然过渡时间分隔暴胀前和暴胀状态，暴胀相作为稳定动力学吸引子出现；分数阶力在暴胀结束点附近消失并改变符号；建立了e-折叠数（e-folds）与分数阶参数α之间的有意义关系，确保了与观测的一致性并解决了视界问题（horizon problem）。

Conclusion: 结论表明该框架不仅实现了从暴胀的优雅退出（graceful exit），而且随后得到了具有标准时间依赖性和α相关归一化的精确辐射主导解，为早期宇宙演化提供了自洽的理论描述。

Abstract: In this paper, we investigate the evolution of the early universe within the framework of fractional Newtonian cosmology. By constructing a suitable fractional potential, we show that the cosmological evolution can naturally originate from a non-singular pre-inflationary regime. We find a natural transition time, separating the pre-inflationary and inflationary regimes, characterized by the balance of the corresponding forces. By analyzing the dynamics near the transition time, we show that the inflationary phase emerges as a stable dynamical attractor. We show that the fractional force vanishes and undergoes a sign change at a point very close to the end of inflation. We then determine the small separation between the force zero point and the end of inflation, and show that it leads to a meaningful relation between the number of $e$-folds and the fractional parameter $α$, ensuring consistency with observations and resolving the horizon problem. Moreover, our results demonstrate the existence of a graceful exit from inflation, followed by an exact radiation-dominated solution with the standard time dependence and an $α$-dependent normalization.

</details>


### [33] [Search for continuous gravitational waves from neutron stars in five globular clusters in the first part of the fourth LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA observing run](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04792)
*Damon H. T. Cheung,Keith Riles,Rafel Amengual,Preet Baxi,Alicia Calafat,Anamaria Effler,Tabata Aira Ferreira,Evan Goetz,Tom Kimpson,David Keitel,Alan M. Knee,Joan-Rene Merou,Quynh Lan Nguyen,Joseph O'Leary,Ornella J. Piccinni,Alicia M. Sintes,Karl Wette*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究对五个银河系球状星团中的未知中子星进行了连续引力波定向搜索，使用LIGO第四轮观测运行前八个月的数据，未在20-475 Hz频段内检测到信号，但对NGC 6397在282 Hz附近获得了迄今最严格的95%置信水平上限约4.2×10⁻²⁶。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探测银河系球状星团中未知中子星发出的连续引力波（continuous gravitational waves），这些信号可能来自非轴对称旋转的中子星，为理解致密天体物理提供新途径。

Method: 使用WEAVE半相干程序（semi-coherent program）对LIGO第四轮观测运行（fourth LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA observing run）前八个月的数据进行分析，通过将匹配滤波检测统计量（matched-filter detection-statistic）在观测期间多个时间片段上求和来增强灵敏度。

Result: 在20-475 Hz搜索频段内，对源年龄大于300年的假设下未检测到引力波信号；通过数据中注入模拟信号验证，在大部分参数空间获得了迄今最敏感的探测结果，对NGC 6397在282 Hz附近的中值95%置信水平上限达到约4.2×10⁻²⁶。

Conclusion: 尽管未发现连续引力波信号，但研究建立了对球状星团中子星引力波辐射的新约束，为未来更高灵敏度的观测奠定了基础，并展示了WEAVE程序在参数空间搜索中的有效性。

Abstract: We present the results of directed searches for continuous gravitational waves from unknown neutron stars in five Milky Way globular clusters. We carry out the searches in the LIGO data from the first eight months of the fourth LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA observing run using the WEAVE semi-coherent program, which sums matched-filter detection-statistic values over many time segments spanning the observation period. No gravitational wave signal is detected in the search band of 20-475 Hz for assumed source ages greater than 300 years. Injections of simulated continuous wave signals in the data indicate that we achieve the most sensitive results to date across most of the explored parameter space volume, obtaining median 95% confidence level upper limits as low as $\sim 4.2 \times 10^{-26}$ near 282 Hz for NGC 6397.

### [34] [Dyonic hairy black holes in $U(1)$ gauge-invariant scalar-vector-tensor theories : Cubic and quartic interactions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04884)
*Masaki Kitagawa,Naoki Tsukamoto,Ryotaro Kase*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究在U(1)规范不变的标量-矢量-张量理论中构建并分类了具有电、磁荷的渐近平坦静态球对称有毛黑洞解，系统纳入了立方和四次相互作用项，揭示了磁荷在激活特定相互作用项中的关键作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于超越先前二次相互作用的研究，系统性地在磁荷存在下纳入更高阶的相互作用项，探索U(1)规范不变的标量-矢量-张量理论中具有电、磁荷的有毛黑洞解。

Method: 方法包括构造渐近平坦、静态、球对称的有毛黑洞解，系统纳入立方和四次相互作用项，推导消除磁荷诱导的高阶导数项的一致性条件，基于对称性对解进行分类，并通过解析展开与数值积分验证解的全局正则性。

Result: 结果表明：平移对称耦合产生由诺特电流（Noether current）支配的次级毛，而φ依赖相互作用产生初级毛；磁荷在激活特定相互作用项如立方耦合$\tilde{f}_3$中起关键作用，该项在纯电构型中不出现；识别出本质依赖于磁荷的解分支，这些解在磁单极极限消失时不存在；标量毛的渐近衰减率随相互作用类型而变化。

Conclusion: 研究成功构建并分类了U(1)规范不变的标量-矢量-张量理论中具有电、磁荷的有毛黑洞解，揭示了磁荷在激活特定相互作用项中的关键作用，并验证了这些解的全局正则性，为观测特征的可能变化提供了理论基础。

Abstract: We construct and classify asymptotically flat, static, spherically symmetric hairy black hole solutions in $U(1)$ gauge-invariant scalar-vector-tensor (SVT) theories carrying both electric and magnetic charges. Extending previous studies beyond the quadratic sector, we systematically incorporate cubic and quartic interaction terms in the presence of the magnetic charge. We derive a consistency condition for the quartic interaction that eliminates higher-order derivative terms induced by the magnetic charge, ensuring the theory remains second-order. We classify the obtained solutions based on their symmetry properties: shift-symmetric couplings yield secondary hair governed by the Noether current, whereas $φ$-dependent interactions generate primary hair. Crucially, our analysis reveals that the magnetic charge plays a key role in activating specific interaction sectors such as the cubic coupling $\tilde{f}_3$, which does not appear in the field equations in purely electric configurations. We identify solution branches that are intrinsic to the magnetic charge, as they cease to exist in the vanishing monopole limit ($P\to 0$). Furthermore, we demonstrate that the scalar hair exhibits distinct asymptotic decay rates depending on the interaction type, suggesting possible variations in observational signatures. Finally, we verify the global regularity of these solutions by connecting analytic expansions with numerical integration.

</details>


### [35] [A loop quantization of the marginally bound Lemaître-Tolman-Bondi dust model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04995)
*Luca Cafaro,Farshid Soltani*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文对边际束缚的Lemaître-Tolman-Bondi（LTB）模型进行了圈量子化（loop quantization），描述了球对称无压尘埃的引力坍缩。研究显示单壳演化是非奇异的，初始坍缩的波包在普朗克能量密度处发生反弹，随后遵循经典膨胀轨迹，从而解决了经典中心曲率奇点问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究的动机在于对描述球对称无压尘埃引力坍缩的边际束缚Lemaître-Tolman-Bondi（LTB）模型进行量子化处理，以解决经典理论中的中心曲率奇点问题。

Method: 方法是将完整的量子LTB模型构建为一系列非相互作用壳层的集合，每个壳层由独立的单壳圈量子动力学（single-shell loop quantum dynamics）控制。研究还比较了圈量子理论与同一模型的Wheeler-DeWitt量子化，并评估了圈量子引力有效理论在再现完整量子动力学方面的准确性。

Result: 结果显示单壳演化是非奇异的，初始坍缩轨迹上达到峰值的波包在普朗克能量密度处发生反弹，随后遵循膨胀的经典轨迹，从而解决了经典中心曲率奇点。研究发现初始坍缩的波包通常在反弹处产生干涉图案，这抑制了有效理论在尘埃云中心附近的准确性。

Conclusion: 研究表明圈量子化能够成功解决LTB模型中的经典奇点问题，但同时也揭示了有效理论在描述量子动力学方面的局限性，特别是在反弹区域附近的有效性受到干涉效应的抑制。

Abstract: We present a loop quantization of the marginally bound Lemaître-Tolman-Bondi (LTB) model, describing the gravitational collapse of pressureless dust in spherical symmetry. The full quantum LTB model is constructed as a collection of non-interacting shells, each governed by an individual single-shell loop quantum dynamics. We show that the single-shell evolution is non-singular and that wave packets initially peaked on a collapsing trajectory undergo a bounce at Planckian energy densities and subsequently follow an expanding classical trajectory, resolving the classical central curvature singularity. We also compare the loop quantum theory with the Wheeler-DeWitt quantization of the same model and assess the accuracy of the loop quantum gravity effective theory in reproducing the full quantum dynamics. Specifically, we find that initially collapsing wave packets generically develop an interference pattern at the bounce, which suppresses the accuracy of the effective theory near the center of the dust cloud.

### [36] [Observational and Thermodynamic aspects of one-dimensional Dark Energy EoS parametrization models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05009)
*Anirban Chatterjee,Yungui Gong*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 使用贝叶斯推断结合信息准则诊断，约束两种一维参数化模型（GZ-Type I和GZ-Type II）。观测数据包括Ia型超新星（Union3、Pantheon+SH0ES、DES-SN5YR）、DESI重子声学振荡和宇宙计时器测量的H(z)。同时引入构型熵作为结构形成的热力学探针。

Conclusion: Gong-Zhang框架被确立为ΛCDM的物理透明且观测一致的扩展，构型熵为晚期宇宙加速提供了补充诊断工具。该研究为理解动力学暗能量对宇宙演化的影响提供了新的分析视角。

Abstract: We examine the observational viability and physical implications of the Gong-Zhang (GZ) dark--energy equation-of-state parametrizations using exclusively late-time cosmological probes. Bayesian inference combined with information-criteria diagnostics shows that both parametrizations provide competitive alternatives to $Λ$CDM, while the GZ-Type~II model is consistently favored, exhibiting reduced parameter degeneracy and stronger Jeffreys-scale support. Beyond background expansion tests, we employ configuration entropy as a thermodynamically motivated probe of structure formation. We demonstrate that the entropy-production rate sensitively traces the impact of dynamical dark energy on late-time gravitational clustering while preserving standard early-time behavior. Our results establish the Gong-Zhang framework as a physically transparent and observationally consistent extension of $Λ$CDM, with configuration entropy providing a complementary diagnostic of late-time cosmic acceleration.

### [37] [Strong breaking of black-hole uniqueness from coexisting scalarization mechanisms](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05064)
*Astrid Eichhorn,Pedro G. S. Fernandes,Lidia Marino*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文发现了一个超越广义相对论的理论，其中克尔黑洞解存在非线性不稳定性，导致多个黑洞解分支共存，破坏了黑洞唯一性定理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 黑洞唯一性（black-hole uniqueness）定理在广义相对论中成立，但预期在超越广义相对论的理论中会被破坏。本研究旨在探索这种破坏可能达到的强烈形式，即多个超越克尔解的黑洞解分支共存的情况。

Method: 研究采用了一个包含标量场与高斯-博内不变量（Gauss-Bonnet invariant）立方耦合的理论框架。该理论通过克尔解的非线性不稳定性触发黑洞标量化（black-hole scalarization）。

Result: 研究发现，在大自旋条件下，曲率诱导和自旋诱导的标量化机制在固定耦合符号下相互竞争。这导致了丰富的黑洞解相结构，以及不同黑洞分支之间的连续和不连续相变。

Conclusion: 该理论展示了黑洞唯一性定理的强烈破坏形式，其中多个黑洞解分支共存，为超越广义相对论的黑洞物理提供了重要案例研究。

Abstract: Black-hole uniqueness, i.e., the statement that all stationary vacuum black holes in the universe are described by the Kerr solution, is expected to break in theories beyond General Relativity. This breaking can take a particularly strong form, if several branches of black-hole solutions beyond the Kerr solution coexist. We find an example of a theory that exhibits such strong breaking. In this theory, a cubic coupling of a scalar field to the Gauss-Bonnet invariant triggers black-hole scalarization through a non-linear instability of the Kerr solution. At large spin, curvature-induced and spin-induced scalarization mechanisms compete at fixed sign of the coupling. This results in a rich phase structure of black-hole solutions and continuous as well as discontinuous transitions between the different branches of black holes.

### [38] [External magnetic field influence on massive binary black hole inspiral gravitational waves and its similarity with environmental effects](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05084)
*Xulong Yuan,Xiangdong Zhang*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了Bertotti-Robinson和Bonnor-Melvin黑洞外部磁场对参数化后爱因斯坦（ppE）引力波波形的印记，旨在区分磁场效应与星系中心大质量黑洞的环境影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 磁场是天体物理研究的关键组成部分，为解释星系尺度的高能天体物理活动提供基础。本研究旨在区分黑洞外部磁场效应与环境影响因素，特别是针对位于星系中心的大质量黑洞。

Method: 首先计算了小质量黑洞向大质量Kerr-Bertotti-Robinson（KBR）黑洞旋进时的ppE频域波形，该黑洞对应于嵌入外部磁场中的Kerr黑洞。进一步研究了旋转的Kerr-Bonnor-Melvin（KBM）黑洞效应。

Result: KBR黑洞磁场的主要阶修正出现在相对于四极矩项的-2后牛顿（PN）阶，而次主要阶修正出现在-1.5 PN阶，源于黑洞自旋。KBM黑洞的主要阶磁场修正出现在-3 PN阶，自旋诱导修正同样在-1.5 PN阶。

Conclusion: KBR和KBM黑洞的主要阶ppE修正与任何修正引力理论效应不简并，但分别类似于指数γ=1和γ=0的幂律分布额外物质的引力贡献。未来引力波观测检测到-3或-2 PN阶修正时，将推断其源于磁场效应或物质环境影响。

Abstract: Magnetic fields represent a critical component of astrophysical research, laying the foundation for interpreting high-energy astrophysical activity across galactic scales. In this work, we investigate the parametrized post-Einsteinian (ppE) waveform imprints induced by the external magnetic fields of Bertotti-Robinson and Bonnor-Melvin black holes, with the aim of distinguishing such magnetic effects from environmental influences--particularly for massive black holes posited to reside at galactic centers. We first compute the ppE frequency-domain waveform for a small black hole inspiraling into a massive Kerr-Bertotti-Robinson (KBR) black hole, which corresponds to a Kerr black hole embedded in an external magnetic field. We find that the leading-order correction arising from the magnetic field is at the $-2$ post-Newtonian (PN) order relative to the quadrupole term, while the next-leading-order correction is at $-1.5$ PN, originating from the spin of the black hole. We further examine the effects of a spinning Kerr-Bonnor-Melvin (KBM) black hole, whose leading-order magnetic correction is at $-3$ PN (consistent with the preceding result), whereas its spin-induced correction is also at $-1.5$ PN. The leading-order ppE corrections for both KBR and KBM black holes do not appear degenerate with any modified theory of gravity effects; nonetheless, we demonstrate that they resemble the gravitational pull contributions from additional matter with power-law distributions of index $γ=1$ and $γ=0$, respectively. As a result, future gravitational wave (GW) observations detecting $-3$ or $-2$ PN order corrections will infer their origin as either magnetic field effects or matter environmental influences.

</details>

*Jiawei Li,Ka-Di Zhu*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种利用光悬浮纳米球和光学腔来约束对称子（symmetron）相互作用的实验方案，通过测量光力学共振谱的分裂来探测暗能量候选粒子，预计可将现有实验室约束提高数个数量级。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了一种光力学（optomechanical）方案，利用光学腔内两个光悬浮纳米球（optically levitated nanospheres）来约束对称子相互作用。对称子介导的相互作用（symmetron-mediated interaction）会产生有效耦合，导致光力学共振谱（optomechanical resonance spectrum）出现可测量的分裂。

Result: 该方法可在μ∼10⁻²eV-10⁻⁴ eV参数范围内提供约束，相比现有实验室界限（laboratory bounds）可提高数个数量级。这证明了光力学光谱学（optomechanical spectroscopy）对屏蔽第五力（screened fifth forces）的高灵敏度。

Conclusion: 光力学方案为探测对称子相互作用提供了有前景的实验途径，其灵敏度显著优于现有实验室方法，有望在暗能量候选粒子的实验探测方面取得重要进展。

Abstract: Screened scalar fields such as the symmetron provide a viable description of dark energy yet their laboratory detection remains challenging. We propose an optomechanical scheme to constrain symmetron interactions using two optically levitated nanospheres inside a cavity. The symmetron-mediated interaction induces an effective coupling which leads to a measurable splitting in the optomechanical resonance spectrum. We forecast constraints in the regime $μ\sim 10^{-2}$eV-$10^{-4}$ eV, which shows that this approach can improve existing laboratory bounds by up to several orders of magnitude, demonstrating the sensitivity of optomechanical spectroscopy to screened fifth forces.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用精确的新方案运行牛顿耦合常数，通过标准插值适当距离函数实现尺度识别，平滑连接紫外和红外区域，构建重整化群改进的类史瓦西黑洞几何。

Conclusion: 重整化群改进成功正则化了黑洞中心奇点，量子修正导致热力学性质的显著变化，同时渐近安全效应改变了相结构临界点但保持了拓扑不变性。

Abstract: We construct a renormalization-group improved Schwarzschild-like black hole geometry using the exact new scheme running for the Newton coupling. The scale identification is implemented via a standard interpolating proper-distance function that smoothly connects the ultraviolet and infrared regimes. We present the resulting coordinate-dependent coupling and the improved metric function, analyzing its asymptotic expansions. The large-distance limit is shown to recover the classical Schwarzschild solution, while the short-distance behavior exhibits a regular de Sitter-like core, demonstrating the regularization of the central singularity. We also analyze the thermodynamic properties of the solution, showing that quantum corrections significantly modify the small-radius behavior, leading to a remnant configuration and a nontrivial phase structure. Finally, we perform a topological classification of the thermodynamic phase space and demonstrate that asymptotically safe effects shift the critical point while preserving the global topological number of the Schwarzschild solution.

### [41] [Accretion Disk Perturbations and Their Effects on Kerr Black Hole Superradiance and Gravitational Atom Evolution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05182)
*Ruiheng Li,Zhong-hao Luo,Zehong Wang,Fa Peng Huang*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了吸积盘引力对克尔黑洞超辐射（Kerr black hole superradiance）的影响，发现吸积盘扰动会改变引力原子的能级和态混合，从而显著影响超辐射增长和玻色子云演化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在现实系统中，吸积盘引力会改变引力原子的能级并混合不同态，从而修正有效的超辐射增长。这为评估超轻玻色子在真实天体物理环境中的可探测性提供了更可靠的理论基础。

Method: 将吸积盘建模为弱外部扰动，通过多极展开（multipole expansion）推导出弱耦合区域下$n=2$子空间$\{\ket{211},\ket{210},\ket{21-1}\}$的有效三能级哈密顿量（three-level Hamiltonian）。

Result: 主导的吸积盘效应是四极矩（quadrupolar）潮汐场，其对称性决定了选择定则：轴对称性仅产生对角能移，赤道非轴对称性激活$Δm=\pm2$混合，而破坏赤道反射对称性则开启涉及$\ket{210}$的$Δm=\pm1$耦合。

Conclusion: 吸积盘扰动是决定黑洞超辐射动力学和玻色子云演化的关键环境因素，为评估超轻玻色子在真实天体物理环境中的可探测性提供了更可靠的理论基础。

Abstract: Kerr black hole (BH) superradiance can form gravitational atoms and produce characteristic gravitational-wave signals, providing a probe of ultralight bosons and dark matter. In realistic systems, accretion-disk gravity can shift energy levels and mix states, modifying the effective superradiant growth. We model the disk as a weak external perturbation via a multipole expansion and derive an effective three-level Hamiltonian for the $n=2$ subspace $\{\ket{211},\ket{210},\ket{21-1}\}$ in the weak-coupling regime. The leading disk effect is the quadrupolar ($\ell_d=2$) tidal field, whose symmetries fix the selection rules: axisymmetry gives only diagonal shifts, equatorial nonaxisymmetry activates $Δm=\pm2$ mixing ($\ket{211}\leftrightarrow\ket{21-1}$), and breaking equatorial reflection opens $Δm=\pm1$ couplings involving $\ket{210}$. As illustrations, a transient equatorial $m=2$ spiral wave drives the resulting two-level system and can suppress or quench superradiance by populating a decaying mode, while a quasi-static warp produces full three-level mixing and can generate narrow ``growth gaps'' near accidental near-degeneracies, with the same static reshuffling also allowing enhancement when weight shifts toward the growing mode. These findings demonstrate that accretion disk perturbations are a crucial environmental factor in determining the dynamics of BH superradiance and the evolution of boson clouds, thereby providing a more reliable theoretical basis for assessing the detectability of ultralight bosons in realistic astrophysical settings.

### [42] [Can Light Cross a Singularity? Exact Solutions from Analogue Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05285)

Result: 研究发现即使在奇点存在的情况下，电磁场方程仍存在精确的正则解（regular solutions）。某些解能够维持穿越奇点的正则且有界的功率通量（power flux）。

We find exact solutions to the full set of electrostatic and electrodynamic equations that remain regular even in the presence of the singularity. Moreover, certain solutions sustain a regular and bounded power flux across the singularity, suggesting that electromagnetic energy may be transmitted through it.

### [43] [Emergence of the geometric contribution to the superfluid density in the inner crust of neutron stars](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05179)
*Giorgio Almirante*

Main category: nucl-th

TL;DR: 该研究阐明了中子星内壳层中超流密度几何贡献（geometric contribution）在能带理论框架下的产生机制，特别关注了多能带穿越费米能级时超流密度对配对能隙（pairing gap）的依赖关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究中子星内壳层超流密度的几何贡献具有重要意义，需要澄清其在能带理论（band theory）框架下的产生机制，特别是当系统存在多个能带穿越费米能级（Fermi energy）时的物理图像。

Method: 采用能带理论分析中子超流系统，在微扰理论（perturbation theory）框架下推导超流密度对配对能隙大小的依赖关系，并系统比较了不同阶修正对几何贡献的影响。

Result: 研究发现，要获得完整的几何贡献，必须同时考虑对（Bogoliubov）准粒子态（quasi-particle states）的修正；若仅考虑对（Hartree-Fock）单粒子态（single-particle states）的修正，则只能得到常规贡献（conventional contribution）。

Conclusion: 该工作明确了中子星内壳层超流密度几何贡献的微观起源，揭示了在能带理论框架下，准粒子态修正在获得几何贡献中的关键作用，为理解该复杂系统的超流性质提供了理论依据。

Abstract: The geometric contribution to the superfluid density has been found to be of great importance in the inner crust of neutron stars. In this work we clarify how this contribution arises in the context of a band theory for neutrons. Specifically, we derive the dependence of the superfluid density on the magnitude of the pairing gap when the system has many bands cutting the Fermi energy, as it is the case for the neutrons in the inner crust. Also, in the perturbation theory framework, we find that it is essential to account for the corrections to the (Bogoliubov) quasi-particle states in order to get the geometric contribution. Accounting only for the corrections to the (Hartree-Fock) single-particle states leads to the conventional contribution only.

</details>
