### [44] [Coherent Biexciton Transport in the Presence of Exciton-Exciton Annihilation in Molecular Aggregates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04483)
*Rajesh Dutta,Chern Chuang*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一个分子聚集体中双激子（biexciton）动力学的理论框架，通过扩展弱耦合极限之外的动力学描述，捕捉激子离域和激子-激子湮灭的影响，同时保持计算可行性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有激子动力学描述通常局限于弱耦合极限，无法充分处理激子离域和激子-激子湮灭等非线性过程。需要建立一个能够明确处理不同激发流形间布居和相干性的理论框架，以解释非线性光学实验中的复杂动力学行为。

Method: 采用约化密度矩阵形式（reduced density-matrix formalism），在马尔可夫环境弛豫描述下构建理论框架。该方法扩展了弱耦合极限之外的动力学描述，同时保持计算可行性，能够处理激子离域和激子-激子湮灭过程。

Result: 非相干初始条件导致强非指数弛豫和由非线性布居动力学驱动的时间依赖性扩散。相干制备的双激子态表现出显著的早期相干输运，其特性对初始态是驻波还是行波叠加敏感。J和H聚集体（J and H aggregate）的发射动力学几乎相同，但双激子输运性质因能带结构依赖的干涉效应而显著不同。

Conclusion: 双激子动力学受初始态相干性和动量组成的强烈影响。初始态制备是多激子输运的关键控制参数，该框架为超越基于布居描述的非线性光学实验解释提供了通用工具。

Abstract: We present a theoretical framework for biexciton dynamics in molecular aggregates that explicitly treats populations and coherences across excitation manifolds within a reduced density-matrix formalism. By extending kinetic descriptions beyond the weak-coupling limit, the approach captures the influence of exciton delocalization and exciton-exciton annihilation while remaining computationally tractable within a Markovian description of environmental relaxation. Using this framework, we investigate how the spatial profile and momentum composition of the initial biexciton state govern fluorescence decay and transport. Incoherent initial conditions lead to strongly non-exponential relaxation and time-dependent diffusion driven by nonlinear population kinetics. In contrast, coherently prepared biexciton states exhibit pronounced early-time coherent transport, whose character depends sensitively on whether the initial state is prepared as a standing-wave or traveling-wave superposition of single-exciton modes. Despite nearly identical emission dynamics for J and H aggregate, biexciton transport properties differ markedly due to band structure-dependent interference effect. Our results demonstrate that biexciton dynamics remains strongly influenced by initial-state coherence and momentum composition. Besides initial-state preparation, the coherent-to-incoherent crossover and the diffusive spreading of the exciton density are sensitive to internal conversion processes such as exciton fusion and the decay to the first excited state. The present work establishes initial-state preparation as a key control parameter for many-exciton transport in excitonic systems and provides a general framework for interpreting nonlinear optical experiments beyond population-based descriptions.

</details>


### [45] [Ge as an orbitronic platform: giant in-plane orbital magneto-electric effect in a 2-dimensional hole gas](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04500)
*James H. Cullen,Dimitrie Culcer*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该论文计算了二维空穴气体（2DHGs）中的轨道磁电效应（OME），发现锗（Ge）空穴的OME效应非常显著，其轨道角动量密度比Rashba-Edelstein效应大一个数量级，表明Ge等p型半导体是构建未来轨道电子器件的理想候选材料。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 计算能力需求的增长推动了对高能效、稳定存储设备的探索，这构成了轨道电子学（orbitronics）兴起的核心动机。轨道电子器件需要能够高效产生轨道角动量（OAM）的材料，而二维材料中的OAM可以通过轨道磁电效应（OME）电学产生。

Method: 本文报告了对二维空穴气体（2DHGs）中轨道磁电效应（OME）的计算。研究聚焦于Ge空穴系统，计算了在特定电场条件下的OAM密度。

Result: 计算显示Ge空穴的OME效应非常显著：在约10^4 V/m的电场下，轨道角动量密度达到约10^12 ħ/cm^2。该OME效应比二维空穴气体中的Rashba-Edelstein效应大一个数量级，且产生的OAM在平面内对齐，源于重空穴态与轻空穴态之间的跃迁，这是该系统的独特特征。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明Ge以及其他p型半导体是构建未来轨道电子器件（orbitronic devices）的有力候选材料，其显著的轨道磁电效应为高效轨道角动量产生提供了物理基础。

Abstract: Increasing demand for computational power has initiated the hunt for energy efficient and stable memory devices. This is the overarching motivation behind the recent rise of \textit{orbitronics}, which looks to harness the orbital angular momentum of charge carriers in computing devices. Orbitronic devices require materials with efficient generation of orbital angular momentum (OAM). In 2D materials, OAM can be electrically generated via the orbital magneto-electric effect (OME). In this paper we report the calculation of the OME in 2 dimensional hole gases (2DHGs). We show that the OME in Ge holes is very large, for an applied electric field of the order $10^4$ V$/$m the OAM density is of the order $10^{12}$ $\hbar/$cm$^{2}$. Furthermore, we find the OME to be an order of magnitude larger than the Rashba-Edelstein effect in 2DHGs. The OME we calculated in 2DHGs generates OAM aligned in the plane and arises due to transitions between heavy and light hole states, which is unique to this system. Our results put Ge, as well as other p-type semiconductors, forward as strong candidates for building future orbitronic devices.

</details>


### [46] [Thermodynamic Phase Transitions in Finite Su-Schrieffer-Heeger Chains: Metastability and Heat Capacity Anomalies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04515)
*Carlos Magno da Conceição,Julio César Pérez-Pedraza,Alfredo Raya,Cristian Villavicencio*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究分析了有限长度Su-Schrieffer-Heeger（SSH）链在热平衡状态下的热力学性质，揭示了在非二聚化构型中热容出现局部极小值所表征的亚稳态热力学相，这一二阶相变与拓扑相变不同，且随跳跃不对称性和链长增加而更加显著。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机是探究一维拓扑系统中有限尺寸效应、热涨落与拓扑性质之间的相互作用关系。通过分析SSH链的热力学行为，旨在理解拓扑边界态与体热力学性质之间的区别与联系，为冷原子、光子系统和拓扑电路等实验实现提供理论见解。

Method: 采用正则系综（canonical ensemble）和巨正则系综（grand canonical ensemble）方法，在固定温度和化学势条件下计算能量密度、粒子数密度、熵和热容等热力学量。这些量被表达为温度、化学势和跳跃不对称性（hopping asymmetry）的函数。

Result: 分析发现非二聚化构型中热容出现局部极小值，表征了一个亚稳态热力学相，这对应于与拓扑相变不同的二阶相变。该亚稳态相随跳跃不对称性增加和链长增长而更加显著。研究还表明，虽然拓扑性质由边界态决定，但体热力学行为展现出丰富的相结构，可通过跳跃参数比进行调控。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了有限SSH链中拓扑性质、有限尺寸效应和热涨落之间的复杂相互作用。体热力学行为展现出可调控的丰富相结构，与由边界态决定的拓扑性质形成对比。这些发现为一维拓扑系统的实验实现提供了重要见解，特别是在冷原子、光子系统和拓扑电路等领域。

Abstract: We investigate the thermodynamic properties of finite Su-Schrieffer-Heeger (SSH) chains in thermal equilibrium at fixed temperature and chemical potential. Using the canonical and grand canonical ensembles, we calculate the energy density, particle number density, entropy, and heat capacity as functions of temperature, chemical potential, and hopping asymmetry. Our analysis reveals the emergence of a metastable thermodynamic phase characterized by a local minimum in the heat capacity for non-dimerized configurations, signaling a second-order phase transition distinct from the topological phase transition. This metastable phase becomes more pronounced as the hopping asymmetry increases and the chain length grows. We demonstrate that while the topological properties are determined by boundary states, the bulk thermodynamic behavior exhibits rich phase structure that can be tuned through the hopping parameter ratio. These findings provide insights into the interplay between topology, finite-size effects, and thermal fluctuations in one-dimensional topological systems, with potential implications for experimental realizations in cold atoms, photonic systems, and topoelectrical circuits.

</details>


### [47] [Large-Area Deterministic Stamping of 2D Materials on Arbitrarily Patterned Surfaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04623)
*Bernardo S. Dias,Reynolds Dziobek-Garrett,Gabriella Mentasti,Abhishek Gupta,Alexander Lambertz,Esther Alarcon-Llado,Peter Schall,Roland Bliem,Jorik van de Groep*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 二维材料及其单层因其独特的电子和光学性质而备受关注，但现有转移技术在可扩展性和与结构化表面的兼容性方面存在局限。特别是对于纳米光子学领域，将大面积二维材料转移到平坦和图案化基底上的能力对于功能器件开发至关重要。

Method: 提出了一种基于低密度聚乙烯（low-density polyethylene）物理特性的通用可靠转移方法。该方法能够将大面积单层材料和hBN/单层异质结构转移到平坦和纳米结构基底上，保持材料固有光学质量，并与多种器件架构兼容。

Result: 通过制造能够通过操纵光子环境、应变或电门控来调制过渡金属二硫化物单层光致发光的器件，验证了该方法的适用性。进一步使用相同方法成功制备了范德华异质结构（van der Waals heterostructures）。

Conclusion: 该技术能够清洁转移多种单层材料和异质结构，为开发具有改进功能、可扩展性和可调谐性的下一代光电子平台提供了实用途径。

Abstract: 2D materials and their monolayers have attracted widespread interest by virtue of their unique electronic and optical properties. In addition to their remarkable physical characteristics, their atomically thin nature enables their integration in ultra-compact photonic and electronic devices, with potential for dynamic tunability via strain, charge carrier modulation or heterostructure engineering. While early research relied on micrometer-scale mechanically exfoliated flakes, recent advances, particularly gold-assisted exfoliation of transition metal dichalcogenides (TMDCs), have enabled the preparation of high-quality, large-area monolayers, opening new opportunities for scalable device integration. For the field of nanophotonics in particular, the ability to transfer large-area 2D materials onto both flat and patterned substrates is essential for the development of functional devices. However, existing transfer techniques are often limited in scalability, and compatibility with structured surfaces. Here, we present a versatile and reliable transfer method of large-area monolayers and hBN/monolayer heterostructures onto both flat and nanostructured substrates. Our approach, based on the physical properties of low-density polyethylene, preserves the intrinsic optical quality of the materials and is compatible with a variety of device architectures. We demonstrate its applicability by fabricating devices that modulate the photoluminescence of TMDC monolayers through the manipulation of the photonic environment, strain or electrical gating. We further demonstrate the fabrication of van der Waals heterostructures using the same method. By enabling clean transfer of a wide range of monolayers and heterostructures, this technique offers a practical pathway for the development of next-generation optoelectronic platforms with improved functionality, scalability, and tunability.

</details>


### [48] [Unified Integer and Fractional Quantum Hall Effects from Boundary-Induced Edge-State Quantization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04652)
*Pedro Pereyra*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该论文提出边界诱导量子化（boundary-induced quantization）作为量子霍尔输运的微观起源，为整数和分数量子霍尔序列提供了统一描述。通过研究横向受限二维电子系统中的朗道问题，证明边界条件离散化了手性边缘态的引导中心坐标和纵向动量，从而产生具有明确多重性的边缘通道家族。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管朗道能级理论和边缘态输运形式取得了成功，但体量子化与观测到的量子霍尔平台层次结构之间的直接微观联系尚未建立。特别是，在标准量子力学框架内，尚未推导出同时解释整数和分数序列的统一微观机制。

Method: 从横向受限二维电子系统中的朗道问题出发，研究狄利克雷（Dirichlet）、诺伊曼（Neumann）和混合（Robin）边界条件对手性边缘态的影响。证明这些边界条件离散化了引导中心坐标（guiding-center coordinate）和纵向动量，产生边界依赖的能谱。将此边界量子化纳入边缘态输运描述中进行分析。

Result: 边界量子化重现了整数霍尔序列，并同时产生了结构化的分数量子填充因子（fractional filling factors）层次，无需引入单独的微观机制。弱霍尔诱导的宇称破坏贡献重组了低能边缘谱，同时保持体朗道能级完整，增强了小朗道指数下的边缘态多重性，稳定了强磁场下观测到的分数平台。

Conclusion: 量子霍尔响应源于朗道量子化（Landau quantization）和边界诱导的引导中心离散化之间的相互作用，二者共同决定了手性边缘通道的能谱和占据。边界诱导量子化是量子霍尔输运的微观起源，在传统量子力学框架内为整数和分数区域提供了统一描述。

Abstract: Despite the success of Landau-level theory and edge-state transport formalisms, a direct microscopic link between bulk quantization and the observed hierarchy of quantum Hall plateaus has not been established. In particular, no unified microscopic mechanism accounting simultaneously for integer and fractional sequences has been derived within standard quantum mechanics.
  Here we show that boundary-induced quantization of edge states provides this missing bridge. Starting from the Landau problem in laterally confined two-dimensional electron systems, we demonstrate that the imposition of Dirichlet, Neumann, and mixed (Robin) boundary conditions discretizes both the guiding-center coordinate and the longitudinal momentum of chiral edge states. The resulting boundary-dependent spectra generate families of edge channels with well-defined multiplicities that couple to electronic transport.
  When incorporated into an edge-state transport description, this boundary quantization reproduces the integer Hall sequence and simultaneously yields a structured hierarchy of fractional filling factors without invoking separate microscopic mechanisms. We further show that a weak Hall-induced parity-breaking contribution reorganizes the low-energy edge spectrum while leaving the bulk Landau levels intact. This controlled symmetry breaking enhances edge-state multiplicities at small Landau indices and stabilizes the fractional plateaus observed at strong magnetic fields.
  The quantized Hall response thus emerges from the interplay between Landau quantization and boundary-induced guiding-center discretization, which together determine the spectrum and occupation of chiral edge channels. These results establish boundary-induced quantization as the microscopic origin of quantum Hall transport and provide a unified description of both integer and fractional regimes within conventional quantum mechanics.

</details>


### [49] [Absence of Orbital Hall Magnetoresistance in Nonmagnet/Ferromagnet Bilayers with Large Orbital Torque](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04889)
*Yumin Yang,Wenqi Xu,Na Lei,Zhicheng Xie,Dahai Wei,Jianhua Zhao*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究报道了在非磁体/铁磁体双层结构中未观测到轨道霍尔磁阻（OMR），挑战了轨道输运模拟自旋输运的普遍假设。尽管观测到巨轨道力矩证实了轨道电流的产生，但厚度依赖的磁阻测量显示信号主要来自铁磁体的本征磁阻和电流分流，无明显OMR贡献。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在检验轨道输运是否遵循与自旋输运相似的物理规则，特别是验证轨道霍尔磁阻（orbital Hall magnetoresistance, OMR）在非磁体/铁磁体双层结构中的存在性。这挑战了"轨道输运模拟自旋输运"的普遍假设。

Method: 采用厚度依赖的磁阻测量方法分析非磁体/铁磁体双层结构。通过测量不同厚度下的磁阻信号，区分本征磁阻、电流分流效应与可能的轨道霍尔磁阻贡献。

Result: 实验未检测到轨道霍尔磁阻（OMR）信号，尽管观测到巨轨道力矩（giant orbital torques）证实了轨道电流的生成。磁阻信号主要源于铁磁体的本征磁阻和电流分流效应。研究还发现镍基双层结构中的织构诱导磁阻和自力矩会产生误导性信号。

Conclusion: 轨道电流与自旋电流具有不同的输运特性：轨道电流在铁磁体中经历各向同性体吸收而非产生OMR所需各向异性界面反射。这些发现阐明了轨道输运的独特物理规则，并提供了区分自旋与轨道电流的简单方法。

Abstract: We report the absence of orbital Hall magnetoresistance (OMR) in nonmagnet/ferromagnet bilayers, challenging the general assumption that orbital transport mimics spin transport. Despite the observation of giant orbital torques, confirming the generation of orbital currents, thickness-dependent magnetoresistance measurements reveal that the signal is dominated by the intrinsic magnetoresistance of the ferromagnet and current shunting, with no discernible OMR contribution. We attribute this contradiction to the distinct transport properties of orbital compared with spin. Orbital currents undergo isotropic bulk absorption in the ferromagnet rather than anisotropic interfacial reflection required for OMR. Furthermore, we find that texture-induced magnetoresistance and self-torques in Ni-based bilayers can generate misleading signals, suggesting that caution is required when employing Ni in orbitronic studies. These findings clarify the distinct physical rules governing orbital transport and provide a simple method to distinguish spin and orbital currents.

</details>

*Taro Wakamura,Masayuki Hashisaka,Yusuke Nomura,Matthieu Bard,Shota Okazaki,Takao Sasagawa,Takashi Taniguchi,Kenji Watanabe,Koji Muraki,Norio Kumada*

TL;DR: 该研究系统探究了拓扑超导体候选材料T_d-MoTe₂在少层极限下的超导特性，通过实验与理论结合揭示了能带结构与超导性的关系，特别在2层样品中发现了与传统声子介导s_(++)波配对一致的高度空穴掺杂超导机制。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: We present a systematic investigation of superconductivity in a topological superconductor candidate $T_{\rm d}$-MoTe$_2$ in the few-layer limit. By examining multiple mechanically exfoliated samples with different thicknesses, substrates and crystal qualities, we quantitatively correlate superconducting temperature ($T_c$) with disorder, carrier density, carrier type and mobility. By integrating these experimental findings with first-principles calculations, we reveal the relationship between the band structure and superconductivity in this material. Notably, in 2 L samples we access a highly hole-doped regime that has not been systematically explored in previous experiments, providing a complementary perspective to earlier studies. In this regime, we demonstrate that superconductivity can be realized in a manner consistent with a conventional phonon-mediated $s_{(++)}$-wave pairing.

</details>


### [51] [Topological Surface Charge Detection via Active Capacitive Compensation: A Pathway to the 4D Quantum Hall Effect](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05025)
*Yuanze Li,Renfei Wang,Yifan Zhang,Jiahao Chen,Yingdong Deng,Jin Xie,Xufeng Kou,Yang Liu,Tian Liang*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种主动补偿方案，通过引入可调负电容来抵消栅极介电电容，从而有效恢复三维拓扑绝缘体中拓扑磁电效应（TME）的完整量子化信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在双栅轴子绝缘体（axion-insulator）器件中，拓扑磁电效应（TME）诱导的极化电流受到电容比C_total/C_S的抑制，导致信号衰减，这阻碍了对四维量子霍尔效应（4D QHE）的直接精确测量。

Method: 提出一种主动补偿方案，在栅极线路中引入可调负电容C_comp ≈ -C_gate，有效抵消栅极介电电容，使电容比C_total/C_S趋近于1。使用量子反常霍尔（QAH）器件验证该方法，该器件与轴子绝缘体具有相同的表面态物理但允许通过单栅极直接进行电荷测量。

Result: 在量子反常霍尔器件实验中，该方法从初始衰减一半的状态恢复了超过95%的量子化电荷信号，验证了补偿方案的有效性。

Conclusion: 该补偿方法为解析微弱的拓扑磁电效应信号提供了稳健手段，为实现四维量子霍尔效应的直接测量开辟了有前景的途径。

Abstract: The topological magnetoelectric effect (TME) in three-dimensional topological insulators (TIs), described by $ΔP = \frac{e^2}{2h} N_{\rm Ch}^{(2)} ΔB$, serves as a condensed-matter realization of the four-dimensional quantum Hall effect (4D QHE). In dual-gate axion-insulator devices, the TME-induced polarization yields a current $I_{\rm TME} \propto (C_{\rm total}/C_{\rm S})\,Q_{\rm 4D\text{-}QHE}$, where the signal is suppressed by the capacitance ratio $C_{\rm total}/C_{\rm S}$. Here we propose an active compensation scheme that introduces a tunable negative capacitance $C_{\rm comp} \approx -C_{\rm gate}$ into the gate line, effectively canceling the gate dielectric capacitance and driving $C_{\rm total}/C_{\rm S} \to 1$. We validate the method using a quantum anomalous Hall (QAH) device, which shares the same surface-state physics with the axion insulator but permits direct charge measurement via a single gate, recovering over $95\%$ of the quantized charge signal from an initially half-attenuated state. This compensation method provides a robust means of resolving minute TME signals, offering a promising pathway toward direct measurements of the 4D QHE.

### [52] [Fabry-Pérot interferometry with stochastic anyonic sources](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05052)
*Sarthak Girdhar,Edvin G. Idrisov,Thomas L. Schmidt*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文研究了分数量子霍尔（fractional quantum Hall）体系中Laughlin准粒子（quasiparticles）在法布里-珀罗干涉仪（Fabry-Pérot interferometer）中的随机注入干涉现象，揭示了准粒子交换相位（exchange phase）对有效阿哈罗诺夫-玻姆（Aharonov-Bohm）相位的贡献及其在隧穿电流噪声中的可观测特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索介观干涉仪（mesoscopic interferometers）中任意子（anyonic）交换统计的可观测性。通过分析随机注入的Laughlin准粒子在法布里-珀罗干涉仪中的干涉行为，旨在揭示准粒子交换相位对干涉图案的影响机制。

Method: 采用理论分析方法，研究Laughlin准粒子在法布里-珀罗干涉仪中的随机注入过程。重点分析注入准粒子通过干涉仪量子点接触（quantum point contacts）时产生的时间域编织（time-domain braiding）过程，及其对有效阿哈罗诺夫-玻姆相位的影响。

Result: 研究发现每个存在于干涉环路上的准粒子都会给有效阿哈罗诺夫-玻姆相位带来额外贡献$\sin(2πλ)/2$，其中$πλ$为准粒子交换相位。在对称准粒子注入极限下，隧穿电流噪声（tunneling current noise）表现出随总注入电流变化的阿哈罗诺夫-玻姆振荡，从而可提取交换相位$πλ$。在大总注入区域，识别出具有幂律标度（power-law scaling）和特征相移的普适法诺因子（universal Fano factor），反映了沿干涉仪边缘的实空间准粒子编织过程。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了随机注入准粒子干涉中时间域编织过程对有效相位的贡献机制，为通过介观干涉仪测量任意子交换统计提供了理论依据。隧穿电流噪声中的阿哈罗诺夫-玻姆振荡和普适法诺因子特征为实验探测准粒子交换相位提供了可观测信号。

Abstract: We investigate the interference of Laughlin quasiparticles (QPs) in the fractional quantum Hall regime that are stochastically injected into a Fabry-Pérot interferometer. We find that the effective Aharonov-Bohm (AB) phase accumulated along the interferometer loop acquires an additional contribution of $\sin(2πλ)/2$ per QP present on it, where $πλ$ is the QP exchange phase. This contribution originates from time-domain braiding processes associated with injected QPs passing the interferometer quantum point contacts. In the limit of symmetric QP injection, the tunneling current noise exhibits AB oscillations as a function of the total injected current, providing access to the exchange phase $πλ$. In the regime of large total injection, we identify a universal Fano factor that displays power-law scaling and a characteristic phase shift reflecting real-space QP braiding along the interferometer edges. These results are relevant for accessing anyonic exchange statistics in mesoscopic interferometers.

### [53] [Non-equilibrium bosonization of fractional quantum Hall edges](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05088)
*Christian Spånslätt,Jinhong Park,Alexander D. Mirlin*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该论文发展了一个非平衡分数量子霍尔边缘态理论，基于Keldysh作用量和手征Luttinger液体的玻色化方法，用于分析电荷全计数统计、准粒子格林函数和隧穿输运性质，特别关注相互作用诱导的任意子分数化对边缘动力学和输运可观测量（如Fano因子）的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 边缘输运是探测分数量子霍尔态低能性质（包括其激发的任意子特性）的有力工具。然而，需要发展一个系统的非平衡分数量子霍尔边缘态理论框架，以深入理解相互作用诱导的任意子分数化如何影响边缘动力学和相关输运可观测量。

Method: 基于Keldysh作用量，建立了手征Luttinger液体的玻色化非平衡分数量子霍尔边缘理论框架。首先考虑单模Laughlin边缘，分析电荷全计数统计、准粒子格林函数和量子点接触隧穿输运性质；然后将形式扩展到具有模间相互作用的多模边缘，以ν=4/3和ν=2/3边缘为范例，研究相互作用诱导的任意子分数化如何修改边缘动力学。

Result: 电荷全计数统计探测激发的分数化电荷，而格林函数和隧穿输运则由分数化激发与隧穿准粒子之间的相互编织相位（mutual braiding phases）决定。特别强调了相互作用诱导的分数化对Fano因子F和微分Fano因子F_d的影响，这些可观测量可通过实验测量。

Conclusion: 该理论框架为分数量子霍尔边缘和Luttinger液体的非平衡输运提供了统一描述，允许从非平衡边缘输运实验中提取任意子编织信息，并为扩展到更复杂的实验几何结构和边缘结构铺平了道路。

Abstract: Edge transport serves as a powerful probe of remarkable low-energy properties of fractional quantum Hall states, including the anyonic character of their excitations. Here, we develop a theory of fractional quantum Hall edges driven out of equilibrium, which is based on the Keldysh action for the bosonized chiral Luttinger liquid. With this non-equilibrium FQH bosonization framework, we first consider a single-mode Laughlin edge and analyze the full counting statistics of charge, the quasiparticle Green's functions, and tunneling transport properties through a quantum point contact, allowing for generic edge excitations. We then extend the formalism to multi-mode edges with inter-mode interactions, and explore, with focus on the $ν=4/3$ and $ν=2/3$ edges as paradigmatic examples, how interaction-induced fractionalization of anyons modifies the edge dynamics and the associated transport observables. While the full counting statistics probes the fractionalized charge of the excitations, the Green's functions and tunneling transport are governed by mutual braiding phases of fractionalized excitations and tunneling quasiparticles. We emphasize in particular the effect of interaction-induced fractionalization on the Fano factor $F$ and the differential Fano factor $F_d$, observables that can be measured experimentally. Our formalism, which provides a unified framework for non-equilibrium transport in FQH edges and Luttinger liquids, permits extracting anyonic braiding information from non-equilibrium edge-transport experiments, and paves the way to various extensions, including more involved experimental geometries and edge structures.

### [54] [Observation of Superfluidity and Meissner Effect of Composite Bosons in GaAs Quantum Hall System](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05341)
*Yuanze Li,Renfei Wang,Jiahao Chen,Wenfeng Zhang,Adbhut Gupta,Kirk W. Baldwin,Loren Pfeiffer,Rui-Rui Du,Yang Liu,Tian Liang*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究通过实验证实了量子霍尔效应（QHE）中复合玻色子（CBs）的超流性质，观测到量子化的电荷泵浦和电荷积累现象，表明系统具有集体体态响应特性，为研究二维宏观量子相干性提供了新平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子霍尔效应（quantum Hall effect, QHE）理论上被理解为复合玻色子（composite bosons, CBs）的超流凝聚体，但除无耗散输运外，其他超流特征如迈斯纳效应（Meissner effect）尚未得到实验证实。研究旨在通过可控时变磁场实验直接验证复合玻色子的超流性质。

Method: 研究采用Corbino disk几何结构，通过施加可控的时变磁场（time-varying magnetic field）探测系统响应。使用具有多个同心顶栅（multiple concentric top gates）的器件，同时观测量子化的劳克林电荷泵浦（quantized Laughlin charge pumping）和新型量子化电荷积累现象。

Result: 实验观测到量子化电荷积累现象，遵循关系式ΔQₐ/e = ν(ΔΦ/Φ₀)，表明系统主动维持定义复合玻色子的固定电子-磁通比。多栅极器件显示电荷积累均匀分布在量子霍尔流体体态中，证实其为集体体态性质而非边缘效应。顶栅的存在决定了屏蔽机制：在有栅极的"巨正则"（grand canonical）设置中，低库仑能量有利于电荷介导的屏蔽（广义迈斯纳效应）；无栅极时系统进入"正则"（canonical）区域，表现出类似II型超导体的固定电子密度。

Conclusion: 这些观测结果证实了量子霍尔效应基态的复合玻色子超流本质，并建立了一个研究二维宏观量子相干性（macroscopic quantum coherence）及其屏蔽转变（screening transitions）的多功能实验平台。

Abstract: The quantum Hall effect (QHE) is theoretically understood as a superfluid condensate of composite bosons (CBs) -- bound states of electrons and magnetic flux quanta. While dissipationless transport is consistent with this picture, other signatures of superfluidity, such as the Meissner effect, remain elusive. Here, we present direct experimental evidence for CB superfluidity by probing the system's response to a controlled, time-varying magnetic field in Corbino disk geometries. We simultaneously observe the quantized Laughlin charge pumping and a new, quantized charge accumulation phenomenon, governed by the relation $ΔQ_{\rm a}/e = ν\,(ΔΦ/Φ_0)$. This relation signifies that the system actively maintains the fixed electron-to-flux ratio that defines the CBs, neutralizing excess flux by drawing in a precise number of electrons.
  Crucially, devices with multiple concentric top gates reveal that this charge accumulation is uniformly distributed across the bulk of the QHE fluid, demonstrating that it is a collective, bulk property rather than an edge effect -- a key signature of a superfluid condensate. Furthermore, the presence of a top gate determines the screening mechanism: in a "grand canonical" setting with a gate, low Coulomb energy favors a charge-mediated screening (generalized Meissner effect); without a gate, the system enters a "canonical" regime, exhibiting fixed electron density like type-II superconductors. These observations confirm the CB superfluid nature of the QHE ground state and establish a versatile platform for studying macroscopic quantum coherence and its screening transitions in two dimensions.

### [55] [Antialtermagnetic Magnons and Nonrelativistic Thermal Edelstein Effect](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05415)
*Robin R. Neumann,Rodrigo Jaeschke-Ubiergo,Ricardo Zarzuela,Libor Šmejkal,Jairo Sinova,Alexander Mook*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究提出并分析了奇宇称磁体（odd-parity magnets）的自旋动力学和磁振子（magnons）特性，发现了具有p波和f波自旋纹理的非共面模型，并展示了非相对论性磁振子热Edelstein效应（thermal Edelstein effect）的存在。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索奇宇称磁体这一新型磁体类别，其在不依赖自旋轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）和偶极相互作用的情况下具有自旋分裂能带结构，并与交变磁体（altermagnets）形成对比。

Method: 研究方法包括构建不含相对论相互作用的非共面奇宇称磁体最小自旋模型，计算磁振子的能带结构和自旋极化，并分析其自旋动力学特性。

Result: 研究发现这些模型可承载p波和f波自旋纹理的磁激发，其中两个模型表现出共线自旋纹理（collinear spin textures），即磁振子自旋极化受限于全局轴，这导致反交变磁性（antialtermagnetism）。此外，研究证明了p波磁体存在线性响应下的非相对论性磁振子热Edelstein效应。

Conclusion: 研究结论表明绝缘性反交变磁体（insulating antialtermagnets）是磁振子自旋电子学（magnon spintronics）应用的有前景候选材料，其热Edelstein效应继承了自旋极化能带结构的部分波特性（partial-wave character）的各向异性角依赖关系。

Abstract: Odd-parity magnets are noncollinear compensated magnets with spin-split band structure in the absence of spin-orbit coupling and dipolar interactions. In contrast to altermagnets, their spin-polarized band structure breaks inversion symmetry, but preserves time-reversal symmetry rendering their spin texture odd in momentum space. Here, we study the spin dynamics of the magnetic texture and compute the band structure and spin polarization of magnons. We present minimal spin models of noncoplanar odd-parity magnets free of relativistic interactions that host p- and f-wave spin textures for the magnetic excitations. We demonstrate that two of these models exhibit collinear spin textures, i.e., the magnon spin polarization is restricted to a global (quantization) axis independent of the momentum giving rise to antialtermagnetism, previously associated primarily with coplanar ground states. Finally, the nonrelativistic magnonic thermal Edelstein effect -- a nonequilibrium magnetization induced by a temperature gradient -- is shown to exist for p-wave magnets in linear response and inherits its anisotropic angular dependence from the partial-wave character of the spin-polarized band structure. Our findings suggest that insulating antialtermagnets are promising candidates for magnon spintronics applications.

### [56] [Manipulation of ferromagnetism with a light-driven nonlinear Edelstein-Zeeman field](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05456)
*Yinchuan Lv,W. Joe Meese,Azel Murzabekova,Jennifer Freedberg,Changjun Lee,Yiming Sun,Joshua Wakefield,Takashi Kurumaji,Joseph Checkelsky,Fahad Mahmood*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究通过非线性埃德尔斯坦效应（nonlinear Edelstein effect）实现了对中心对称范德华半导体Cr₂Ge₂Te₆中铁磁性的非热超快光学控制，利用时域太赫兹发射光谱直接观测了光驱动磁化动力学产生的磁偶极辐射。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 光学控制磁化通常因电场和磁化在反演和时间反演下变换性质不同而被对称性禁止，但通过偶阶非线性响应可以产生非平衡磁密度（非线性埃德尔斯坦效应），作为内部埃德尔斯坦-塞曼场耦合到较慢的磁自由度。

Method: 采用时域太赫兹发射光谱（time-domain THz emission spectroscopy）在近红外激发下直接观测光驱动磁化动力学产生的磁偶极辐射，并通过弱各向异性海森堡铁磁体在埃德尔斯坦-塞曼场作用下的平均场描述定量分析太赫兹发射的偏振、通量和温度依赖性。

Result: 实验成功观测到由非线性埃德尔斯坦效应驱动的磁偶极辐射，太赫兹发射的偏振、通量和温度依赖性与理论模型定量吻合，证实了通过共振非线性埃德尔斯坦效应实现非热超快光学控制铁磁性的有效性。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了一条通过非平衡路径实现中心对称材料磁学光学控制的通用方法，为对称性禁止的光学磁化控制提供了新的物理机制。

Abstract: Optical control of magnetization is often symmetry-forbidden because electric fields and magnetization transform differently under inversion and time-reversal. However, through even-order nonlinear response, optical excitation can generate a nonequilibrium magnetic density (the nonlinear Edelstein effect) that acts as an internal Edelstein-Zeeman field coupling to slower magnetic degrees of freedom. Here we demonstrate non-thermal, ultrafast optical control of ferromagnetism in the centrosymmetric van der Waals semiconductor Cr$_2$Ge$_2$Te$_6$ via a resonant nonlinear Edelstein effect. Using time-domain THz emission spectroscopy under near-infrared excitation, we directly observe magnetic dipole radiation arising from optically driven magnetization dynamics. The polarization, fluence, and temperature dependences of the THz emission are quantitatively captured by a mean-field description of a weakly anisotropic Heisenberg ferromagnet subject to an Edelstein-Zeeman field. Our results establish a general nonequilibrium route to optical control of magnetism in centrosymmetric materials.

# math.PR [[Back]](#toc)

### [57] [The coordinate change formula for the Liouville quantum gravity metric holds for all conformal maps simultaneously](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04640)
*Charles Devlin VI*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 本文证明了Liouville量子引力（LQG）中距离函数的共形协变性（conformal covariance）——对于所有共形映射（conformal maps）同时成立，从而精确化了量子表面（quantum surface）作为随机等价类的启发性定义。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Liouville量子引力（LQG）理论中，已知面积测度（area measure）对所有共形映射同时具有共形协变性，但距离函数（distance function）的相应性质尚未得到证明。本文旨在填补这一理论空白，为量子表面的随机等价类定义提供严格数学基础。

Method: 通过数学证明方法，建立了LQG距离函数在共形变换下的等价性。具体而言，证明了对于任意开集U和共形映射φ，由场h定义的LQG表面与由变换场h^φ定义的LQG表面在距离函数上几乎必然等价。

Result: 成功证明了LQG距离函数对所有共形映射同时具有共形协变性，即距离函数在共形变换下几乎必然保持等价。这一结果与Sheffield-Wang（2016）关于面积测度的结论相对应，完善了LQG理论的数学框架。

Conclusion: 本文证明了LQG距离函数的共形协变性，使得量子表面作为随机等价类的启发性定义得以精确化。该结果为LQG理论提供了更完整的数学基础，确认了量子表面在共形变换下面积测度和距离函数的双重不变性。

Abstract: Liouville quantum gravity (LQG) is, heuristically, a theory of random Riemannian geometry with Riemannian metric tensor $e^{γh} (\mathrm{d} x^2 + \mathrm{d} y^2)$, where $h$ is a variant of the Gaussian free field and $γ> 0$ is a parameter. If $U \subset \mathbb{C}$ is an open set, $φ\colon U \to φ(U)$ is a conformal map, and $h^φ = h \circ φ^{-1} + Q \log|(φ^{-1})'|$ (where $Q = Q(γ)$ is a parameter), then the LQG surface on $U$ defined with field $h$ is equivalent to the LQG surface on $φ(U)$ with field $h^φ$. This equivalence is meant in the sense that the area measures and distance functions on these surfaces are almost surely equivalent. It is known for the area measure that, in fact, this equivalence holds almost surely for all conformal maps $φ$ simultaneously (Sheffield-Wang 2016). We prove the corresponding result for the distance function. This makes precise the frequently used heuristic definition that a quantum surface is a random equivalence class of domains equipped with the LQG area measure and LQG distance function.

</details>


### [58] [Dyson Brownian motion on a Jordan curve](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05316)
*Vladislav Guskov,Mingchang Liu,Fredrik Viklund*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 本文对Zabrodin提出的平面光滑Jordan曲线上Dyson布朗运动的推广进行了严格构造，研究了该过程的基本性质，推导了相关方程，并分析了低温大偏差和多粒子极限下的平均场行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Zabrodin最近提出了Dyson布朗运动（Dyson Brownian motion）的推广，将粒子限制在平面光滑Jordan曲线（smooth Jordan curve）上。本文旨在对该过程进行严格构造并研究其基本性质。

Method: 在可求长Jordan曲线（rectifiable Jordan curve）上严格构造该过程，并在进一步光滑性假设下，推导相关的Fokker-Planck-Kolmogorov方程，研究低温下的大偏差（large deviations）行为，并分析多粒子极限下的平均场McKean-Vlasov方程。

Result: 成功构造了该过程并证明了其向稳态Coulomb气体分布（stationary Coulomb gas distribution）的收敛性，推导了相关方程并研究了低温大偏差特性，获得了多粒子极限下的平均场方程。

Conclusion: 本文为Jordan曲线上Dyson布朗运动的推广提供了严格的数学框架，建立了相关动力学方程，并分析了其统计力学性质，包括收敛性、大偏差行为和平均场极限。

Abstract: Zabrodin recently proposed a generalization of Dyson Brownian motion to a setting where the particles are confined to a smooth Jordan curve in the plane. In this paper, we discuss a rigorous construction of such a process on a rectifiable Jordan curve and study some of its basic properties. Under further smoothness assumptions, we derive the associated Fokker-Planck-Kolmogorov equation, prove convergence towards the stationary Coulomb gas distribution, study large deviations at low temperature, and derive the limiting mean-field McKean--Vlasov equation in the many-particle limit.

Motivation: 研究动机在于利用机器学习算法推断无序长程相互作用量子自旋链的纠缠结构，通过从强无序重整化群方法中学习，探索机器学习在复杂量子系统分析中的应用潜力。

Result: GNN实现了接近一的平均无序配对精度，并在所有子系统尺寸和相互作用指数上精确复现了与SDRG定量一致的纠缠熵。重整化群流热图证实GNN学习了顺序剔除层次结构，而不仅仅是拟合最终状态可观测量。

Conclusion: 研究表明图神经网络能够有效学习强无序重整化群的物理规则，成功推断量子自旋链的纠缠结构。通过两阶段策略将有限温度效应纳入分析，结果与数值SDRGX和理论预测一致，无需重新训练。

Abstract: We train machine learning algorithms to infer the entanglement structure of disordered long-range interacting quantum spin chains by learning from the strong disorder renormalisation group (SDRG) method. The system consists of $S=1/2$-quantum spins coupled by antiferromagnetic power-law interactions with decay exponent $α$ at random positions on a one-dimensional chain. Using SDRG as a physics-informed teacher, we compare a Random Forest classifier as a classical baseline with a graph neural network (GNN) that operates directly on the interaction graph and learns a bond-ranking rule mirroring the SDRG decimation policy. The GNN achieves a disorder-averaged pairing accuracy close to one and reproduces the entanglement entropy $S(\ell)$ in excellent quantitative agreement with SDRG across all subsystem sizes and interaction exponents. RG flow heat maps confirm that the GNN learns the sequential decimation hierarchy rather than merely fitting final-state observables. Finite-temperature entanglement properties are incorporated via the SDRGX framework through a two-stage strategy, using the zero-temperature GNN to generate the RG flow and sampling thermal occupations from the canonical ensemble, yielding results in agreement with both numerical SDRGX and analytical predictions without retraining.

### [60] [Strong zero modes in random Ising-Majorana chains](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05313)
*Saurav Kantha,Nicolas Laflorencie*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 该研究使用拓扑强零模保真度（SZM fidelity）作为多体诊断工具，探究随机伊辛-马约拉纳链中拓扑强零模的鲁棒性及其在无限随机性固定点（IRFP）的行为特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探究淬火无序（quenched disorder）如何改变拓扑强零模（topological strong zero modes, SZMs）在随机伊辛-马约拉纳链中的命运和鲁棒性，特别关注无限随机性固定点（infinite-randomness fixed point, IRFP）对临界行为的影响。

Method: 采用拓扑强零模保真度 ${\cal F}_{\rm SZM}$ 作为多体诊断工具，该量度量化了SZM算符在整个谱中对相反宇称（parity）扇区映射的精确度。研究分别在微正则（microcanonical）和正则（canonical）系综中分析随机链的行为。

Result: 在拓扑相（包括无能隙格里菲斯（gapless Griffiths）区域）中，SZMs持续存在，保真度指数收敛于1。在IRFP处，保真度分布呈现系综依赖性：微正则系综显示双峰结构{0.5,1}，而正则系综呈现三峰结构{0,0.5,1}并具有幂律奇异性（power-law singularities）。

Conclusion: ${\cal F}_{\rm SZM}$ 被确立为局域化保护拓扑序（localization-protected topological order）的鲁棒探针，揭示了无限随机性临界性的独特拓扑特征。IRFP表现出比清洁伊辛共形场论（clean Ising CFT）更强的内在拓扑特性，其临界分布的选择性边界结构可能反映了IRFP处平均Kramers-Wannier对偶对称性的边界表现。

Abstract: We investigate the fate and robustness of topological strong zero modes (SZMs) in random Ising-Majorana chains using the SZM fidelity, ${\cal F}_{\rm SZM}$, as a many-body diagnostic that quantifies how accurately SZM operators map the {\it entire} spectrum between opposite parity sectors. In clean systems, ${\cal F}_{\rm SZM}=1$ in the topological phase, vanishes in the trivial regime, and takes the universal value $\sqrt{8}/π$ at the $(1+1)$D Ising critical point. Here we study how quenched disorder modifies this picture across the infinite-randomness fixed point (IRFP) governing the criticality of the random chain. In both microcanonical and canonical ensembles, SZMs persist throughout the topological phase, including the gapless Griffiths regime, with fidelities converging exponentially to unity. At the IRFP, however, the fidelity distributions become ensemble dependent: the microcanonical ensemble displays bimodal peaks at $\{0.5,1\}$, while the canonical ensemble develops a triple-peak structure at $\{0,0.5,1\}$ with power-law singularities. Our results establish ${\cal F}_{\rm SZM}$ as a robust probe of localization-protected topological order and uncover distinctive topological features of infinite-randomness criticality. Unlike the clean Ising CFT, where the finite critical value arises from a cancellation of power laws, the IRFP seems to exhibit an intrinsically stronger topological character. The edge-selective structure of the critical distributions may suggest a boundary manifestation of the average Kramers-Wannier duality symmetry at the IRFP.

Method: 通过将观测到的电场时间依赖关系映射到沿簇射轴线的倾斜深度（slant depth）函数所发射的电场，从而推断簇射纵向发展参数。

Result: 研究表明可以从观测电场的时间变化推断出簇射纵向发展参数，这为利用电场信号研究宇宙射线空气簇射提供了理论依据。

Abstract: Ultra-high energy cosmic rays impinge on the atmosphere and induce air shower cascades, in which huge numbers of particles are produced. ### [62] [An efficient and accurate numerical method for computing the ground states of three-dimensional rotating dipolar Bose-Einstein condensates under strongly anisotropic trap](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05194)
*Qinglin Tang,Hanquan Wang,Shaobo Zhang,Yong Zhang*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种高效且谱精确的数值方法，用于计算三维旋转偶极玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体在强各向异性势阱中的基态。该方法结合了各向异性截断核方法与预条件共轭梯度法，实现了谱精度、高效率和内存经济性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 三维旋转偶极玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体在强各向异性势阱中的基态计算面临多重挑战。核奇异性、卷积非定域性和密度各向异性共同使偶极势计算复杂化，而快速旋转机制不仅产生具有多个局部最小值的复杂能量景观，还在凝聚体中产生大量涡旋。这些因素使得基态计算在收敛性、精度和效率方面极具挑战性。

Method: 本文提出了一种预条件共轭梯度法（preconditioned conjugate gradient method, PCG），结合傅里叶谱离散化，并整合了用于偶极势计算的各向异性截断核方法（anisotropic truncated kernel method, ATKM）。设计了自适应步长控制策略，ATKM方法在不引入额外各向异性相关内存需求或计算时间的情况下实现了谱精度。

Result: 该算法具有谱精度、高效率和内存经济性。广泛的数值结果证实了方法的精度和效率，并应用于研究模型参数对临界旋转频率、能量和化学势的影响。模拟还揭示了新的基态模式，如弯曲涡旋（bent vortices）。

Conclusion: 本文提出的数值方法成功解决了三维旋转偶极玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体在强各向异性势阱中基态计算的关键挑战。该方法通过整合ATKM和PCG，实现了高效、精确且内存经济的计算框架，为研究此类复杂系统的物理特性提供了有力工具。

Abstract: In this article, we propose an efficient and spectrally accurate numerical method to compute the ground states of three-dimensional (3D) rotating dipolar Bose-Einstein condensates (BEC) under strongly anisotropic trapping potentials.The kernel singularity, convolution non-locality and density anisotropy together complicate the dipolar potential evaluation. The fast rotation mechanism not only induces a complicated energy landscape with many local minima, but also creates a large number of vortices in the condensates. Such factors collectively make the ground state computation challenging in terms of convergence, accuracy and efficiency, especially for 3D anisotropic systems. Coupled with Fourier spectral discretization, we proposed a preconditioned conjugate gradient method (PCG) by integrating the anisotropic truncated kernel method (ATKM) for the dipolar potential evaluation. An adaptive step size control strategy is designed and ATKM allows for a spectral accuracy without introducing any extra anisotropy-dependent memory requirement or computational time. Our algorithm is spectrally accurate, highly efficient and memory-economic. Extensive numerical results are presented to confirm the accuracy and efficiency, together with applications to study impacts of the model parameters on critical rotational frequency, energies and chemical potential. Furthermore, these simulations reveal additional novel ground state patterns, such as bent vortices.

### [63] [How to improve the accuracy of semiclassical and quasiclassical dynamics with and without generalized quantum master equations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04563)
*Matthew R. Laskowski,Srijan Bhattacharyya,Andrés Montoya-Castillo*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了半经典-广义量子主方程（SC-GQME）精度提升的机制，发现精确的"左手"时间导数能延迟半经典不准确性的出现，但也会在挑战性参数区域产生非物理动力学。研究开发了一种明确确定记忆核截断的协议。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 半经典（semi-classical, SC）理论虽能处理任意原子间相互作用，适用于凝聚相中的量子动力学预测，但存在计算成本高和精度不足的问题。SC-GQME方法虽能提升效率和精度，但其精度提升机制尚不明确，且在挑战性参数区域会产生非物理动力学。

Method: 采用短时分析证明精确的"左手"时间导数（left-handed time-derivatives）能延迟半经典不准确性的出现。通过数值积分展示这些导数即使在没有广义量子主方程（GQME）的情况下也能提升动力学精度。开发了一种明确确定记忆核（memory kernel）截断的协议。

Result: 研究发现"左手"时间导数具有双重性：在提供更高短时精度的同时，在挑战性参数区域会变得非物理。短寿命记忆核能够利用短时精度同时规避长时间不稳定性。新开发的截断协议能在先前方法失败的挑战性区域中明确确定记忆核截断。

Conclusion: 对精度提升机制的理解和记忆核截断协议可应用于超越简单模型的复杂系统。这些发现为解决SC-GQME方法在挑战性参数区域产生非物理动力学的问题提供了理论基础。

Abstract: Semi- and quasi-classical (SC) theories can handle arbitrary interatomic interactions and are thus well-suited to predict quantum dynamics in condensed phases that encode energy and charge transport, spectroscopic responses, and chemical reactivity. However, SC theories can be computationally expensive and inaccurate. When combined with generalized quantum master equations (GQMEs), the resulting SC-GQMEs have been observed to enhance the efficiency and accuracy of SC dynamics. Yet, while the mechanism responsible for improved efficiency is clear, the underlying improved accuracy remains elusive. What is worse, SC-GQMEs can yield unphysical dynamics in challenging parameter regimes -- a shortcoming that might be avoided if the mechanism of accuracy improvement were understood. Here, we uncover this mechanism. We leverage short-time analyses to prove that exact, "left-handed" time-derivatives delay the onset of SC inaccuracy, and show that their numerical integration yields dynamics with improved accuracy, even without the GQME. We find, however, that these derivatives are a double-edged sword: while offering greater short-time accuracy, they become unphysical in challenging parameter regimes. Because short-lived memory kernels can leverage short-time accuracy while circumventing long-time instability, we develop a protocol to unambiguously determine the memory kernel cutoff, even in challenging regimes where previous treatments had failed. Our insights into accuracy improvement and kernel cutoff protocol can be expected to apply to complex systems that go beyond simple models.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究扩展了原子尺度的Madrid-2019力场（force-field）来模拟FeCl₂溶液，通过模拟和实验测量相结合的方法，比较了FeCl₂和MgCl₂溶液的粘度差异，并利用粘度数据推断络合程度。

Result: 研究发现FeCl₂溶液比MgCl₂溶液具有更高的粘度，这一差异被解释为FeCl₂溶液中更强的络合（complexation）形成。该结论得到了近期X射线吸收（X-ray absorption）和中子散射（neutron scattering）实验的支持。

Conclusion: 络合程度显著影响电解质溶液的输运性质，粘度可作为测定高浓度水溶液中络合程度的有效指标。该方法为理解高浓度离子溶液的性质提供了新途径。

Abstract: Electrolyte solutions at high concentration are indispensable and yet poorly understood. In particular, the extent of speciation -- the formation of complexes composed of multiple species -- in concentrated ionic solutions is very challenging to obtain theoretically and experimentally, but can have a strong effect on solution properties. The literature is rife with contradictory estimates of speciation from experiments. We find that speciation affects transport properties, and is therefore, a prerequisite to accurately model concentrated solutions. We turn this to our advantage by showing that the viscosity can be used to determine the extent of complexation in concentrated aqueous solutions. Results of simulations as well as experimental measurements are presented. The atomistic Madrid-2019 force-field is extended to model FeCl$_2$. Solutions of FeCl$_2$ and MgCl$_2$ are compared and the observed difference in viscosity explained by more complexation in the former, a conclusion supported by recently reported X-ray absorption and neutron scattering experiments.

### [65] [Escaping the Hydrolysis Trap: An Agentic Workflow for Inverse Design of Durable Photocatalytic Covalent Organic Frameworks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05188)
*Iman Peivaste,Nicolas D. Boscher,Ahmed Makradi,Salim Belouettar*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 本文介绍了一种名为Ara的大型语言模型（LLM）智能体，用于加速共价有机框架（COFs）光催化剂的组合设计空间搜索，以同时满足带隙、带边和抗水解稳定性等多重标准。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 共价有机框架（COFs）是太阳能制氢的有前景光催化剂，但最具电子优势的亚胺键在水中快速水解，导致稳定性与活性之间存在权衡，限制了实际应用。在节点、连接体、连接键和功能基团的组合设计空间中，同时识别出既具有活性又耐用的候选材料仍然是一项艰巨挑战。

Method: 本文引入Ara，一种利用预训练化学知识、给体-受体理论（donor-acceptor theory）、共轭效应和连接键稳定性层次结构的大型语言模型（LLM）智能体，指导搜索满足联合带隙、带边和水解稳定性标准的COFs。该方法在由各种节点、连接体、连接键和R基团组成的候选空间中，使用GFN1-xTB片段管道进行筛选。

Result: Ara实现了52.7%的命中率（是随机搜索的11.5倍，p=0.006），在第12次迭代中找到第一个命中，而随机搜索需要25次迭代，且显著优于贝叶斯优化（BO）（p=0.006）。智能体的推理轨迹显示出可解释的化学逻辑：早期收敛于乙烯基和β-酮烯胺连接键以获得稳定性，基于吸电子特性选择节点，并系统优化R基团以将带隙中心定在2.0 eV。

Conclusion: 对完整搜索空间的详尽评估揭示了智能体与贝叶斯优化（BO）之间互补的利用-探索权衡，表明混合策略可能结合两种方法的优势。这些结果表明，LLM化学先验知识可以显著加速多标准材料发现。

Abstract: Covalent organic frameworks (COFs) are promising photocatalysts for solar hydrogen production, yet the most electronically favorable linkages, imines, hydrolyze rapidly in water, creating a stability--activity trade-off that limits practical deployment. Navigating the combinatorial design space of nodes, linkers, linkages, and functional groups to identify candidates that are simultaneously active and durable remains a formidable challenge. Here we introduce Ara, a large-language-model (LLM) agent that leverages pretrained chemical knowledge, donor--acceptor theory, conjugation effects, and linkage stability hierarchies, to guide the search for photocatalytic COFs satisfying joint band-gap, band-edge, and hydrolytic-stability criteria. Evaluated against random search and Bayesian optimization (BO) over a space consisting of candidates with various nodes, linkers, linkages, and r-groups, screened with a GFN1-xTB fragment pipeline, Ara achieves a 52.7\% hit rate (11.5$\times$ random, p = 0.006), finds its first hit at iteration 12 versus 25 for random search, and significantly outperforms BO (p = 0.006). Inspection of the agent's reasoning traces reveals interpretable chemical logic: early convergence on vinylene and beta-ketoenamine linkages for stability, node selection informed by electron-withdrawing character, and systematic R-group optimization to center the band gap at 2.0 eV. Exhaustive evaluation of the full search space uncovers a complementary exploitation--exploration trade-off between the agent and BO, suggesting that hybrid strategies may combine the strengths of both approaches. These results demonstrate that LLM chemical priors can substantially accelerate multi-criteria materials discovery.

</details>

### [66] [Quantum field theories with many fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04481)
*Ludo Fraser-Taliente*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文开发了用于解决大N（large-N）量子场论（QFTs）的简化方法，特别是针对melonic QFTs家族，包括SYK-like模型、张量模型和矢量模型。提出了$\tilde{F}$-极值化方法，用于求解强耦合极限下的大N melonic QFTs，并展示了红外共形场论（CFTs）的显著简化特性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大N量子场论为研究强耦合物理提供了重要窗口。论文主要研究大N melonic QFTs家族，这些模型包含Sachdev-Ye-Kitaev-like模型、张量模型和矢量模型，旨在开发解决这类理论的有效方法。

Method: 首先回顾大N极限作为QFTs求解方法，使用零维场论和广义自由场论流作为玩具模型阐明该方法。开发了$\tilde{F}$-极值化方法，用于求解任意大N melonic QFTs的强耦合极限。以连续维度中的四次Yukawa模型为例，将其视为张量场论并求解其共形极限。

Result: 红外共形场论显示出显著简化特性，完全由最大化自由度的要求解决，仅受场间相互作用的简单约束约束。通过$\tilde{F}$（自由能的普适部分）测量共形红外理论的自由度数量。展示了四次Yukawa模型的多重固定点及其稳定性，以及其算符谱，匹配了大N展开和维度展开的数据。

Conclusion: 这些特征反映了melonic共形场论的一般特性：存在性、稳定性和谱特征。论文最后展望了melonic理论的未来研究方向，包括进一步探索这些理论的性质和应用。

Abstract: The large-$N$ quantum field theories provide a window into the regime of strongly-coupled physics. Our principal object of study in this thesis is the large-$N$ family of melonic QFTs, which contain the Sachdev-Ye-Kitaev-like models, tensor models, and vector models. We begin with a review of this limit of a large number of degrees of freedom (large-$N$) as an approach to the solution of QFTs. Two toy models are used to clarify this approach: a zero-dimensional field theory and the flow of a generalized free field theory. Both models are solvable, and so we can explicitly demonstrate: using the former, the simplifications at large $N$; using the latter, the tools used to study scale-dependence of physics -- the renormalization group. We develop $\tilde{F}$-extremization, a simple method of solution for an arbitrary large-$N$ melonic QFT in its strongly-coupled limit. The infrared conformal field theories show remarkable simplicity, in that they are entirely solved by the requirement that they have as many degrees of freedom as possible, up to a simple constraint arising from the interaction between the fields. We measure the number of degrees of freedom of the conformal infrared theory via $\tilde{F}$, the universal part of the free energy. We then present the example of the quartic Yukawa model in continuous dimension. This model is considered as a tensor field theory, and solved for its conformal limit; we then illustrate its multiplicity of fixed points and their stability, as well as its operator spectrum, matching the data between the large-$N$ and dimensional expansions. These features reflect general characteristics of melonic conformal field theories: their existence, stability, and spectral characteristics. We conclude with future directions of exploration for the melonic theories.

</details>


### [67] [Higher-Spin and Higher-Point Constraints on Stringy Amplitudes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04485)
*Ivano Basile,Grant N. Remmen,Georgina Staudt*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该研究通过多粒子因子化（multiparticle factorization）约束树级开弦振幅的形变，发现Koba-Nielsen型振幅的Regge截距（Regge intercept）可唯一确定并匹配玻色弦，同时获得对世界面被积函数形变的新约束。对于超弦形变，利用软运动学（soft kinematics）得到多正性界（multipositivity bounds），证明Gross发现的振幅族中最简单的可因子化卫星形变（factorizable satellite deformation）被幺正性（unitarity）禁止。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探索弦振幅形变的约束条件，特别是验证弦激发的高自旋塔（higher-spin tower）是否比有限数量粒子物种更具刚性。通过分析形变如何影响振幅的因子化性质和幺正性要求，揭示弦理论内在的结构约束。

Method: 采用多粒子因子化方法约束树级开弦振幅形变，假设相同自旋中间态的最小简并度（minimal degeneracy）。对于超弦形变，利用软运动学处理无质量外态和任意谱简并（spectral degeneracy），并在大能级极限（large-level limit）下计算主导和次主导阶的多正性界。

Result: 发现Koba-Nielsen型振幅的Regge截距可通过七点因子化唯一确定，精确匹配玻色弦理论值。获得对世界面被积函数形变的新约束，并证明Gross振幅族中最简单的可因子化卫星形变被幺正性禁止，支持高自旋激发塔具有极强刚性的观点。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明弦理论的高自旋激发塔在振幅形变方面展现出显著的刚性，任何此类形变都受到严格的因子化和幺正性约束。这强化了弦激发塔比有限粒子物种更具结构刚性的传统观点，为理解弦理论的基本特性提供了新见解。

Abstract: We employ multiparticle factorization to constrain deformations of tree-level open string amplitudes. Assuming minimal degeneracy among intermediate states of the same spin up through the second excited level, we find that the Regge intercept among all amplitudes of the Koba-Nielsen type can be uniquely fixed using seven-point factorization, precisely matching the bosonic string. Moreover, we produce novel constraints on deformations of the worldsheet integrand. We then turn to deformations of superstrings, with massless external states and arbitrary spectral degeneracy, using soft kinematics. Accounting for the infinite tower of higher-spin resonances, we obtain novel multipositivity bounds to leading and subleading order in the large-level limit. We apply these bounds to the simplest factorizable satellite deformation in the family of amplitudes found by Gross, showing that any deformation of four-point string amplitudes of this type is forbidden by unitarity. Our results reinforce the folklore that the higher-spin tower of string excitations is dramatically more rigid than any finite number of species.

### [68] [Nonabelian Lattice Weak Gravity Conjecture and Monopole Confinement](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04494)
*Matthew Reece,Tom Rudelius*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该研究验证了弱引力猜想（Weak Gravity Conjecture）违反与分数电荷禁闭磁单极子（fractionally charged confined monopoles）之间的假设关联，通过异弦（heterotic string）的环面轨道折叠（toroidal orbifold）紧致化模型证实了这一关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管多数量子引力理论满足晶格弱引力猜想（Lattice Weak Gravity Conjecture, LWGC），但存在违反该猜想的反例。近期假设认为此类反例必然涉及分数电荷的禁闭磁单极子（fractionally charged confined monopoles），本研究旨在验证这一假设。

Method: 研究采用异弦（heterotic string）的环面轨道折叠紧致化（toroidal orbifold compactifications）作为分析框架，特别关注在阿贝尔（abelian）和非阿贝尔（nonabelian）规范场部分均出现LWGC违反的模型。

Result: 在所有考虑的案例中，均存在规范群中心（center of the gauge group）的离散子群K ⊆ Z(G)，使得超极值粒子（superextremal particles）存在于商群G/K的电荷晶格（charge lattice）的每个格点，而（禁闭的）磁单极子存在于G/K的磁荷晶格（magnetic charge lattice）的所有格点。

Conclusion: 结果表明，对于具有平凡中心（trivial centers）的规范群，LWGC违反不可能发生；更一般地，非阿贝尔规范理论中LWGC违反的程度受中心最大阶数（maximal order of the center）的限制。

Abstract: Within the known landscape of quantum gravity, most theories satisfy the Lattice Weak Gravity Conjecture (LWGC), which requires a superextremal particle at every site in the electric charge lattice $Γ$. However, counterexamples to the LWGC exist, and it was recently hypothesized that such counterexamples necessarily feature fractionally charged confined monopoles. In this work, we verify this hypothesis in toroidal orbifold compactifications of the heterotic string, which notably feature LWGC violation in both the abelian and nonabelian gauge sectors. In all the cases we consider, there exists a discrete subgroup of the center of the gauge group $K \subseteq Z(G)$ such that superextremal particles exist at every site in the charge lattice of the quotient group $G/K$, while (confined) monopoles exist at all sites in the magnetic charge lattice of $G/K$. This suggests that LWGC violation cannot occur for gauge groups with trivial centers, and more generally the degree of LWGC violation in a nonabelian gauge theory is bounded in terms of the maximal order of the center.

### [69] [From BPS geodesics to mode-driven dynamics in the scattering of multiple BPS vortices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04495)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过分析Abelian-Higgs模型在临界耦合条件下的动力学，研究模生成力（mode-generated force）——即模频率沿地测线变化产生的力——对涡旋运动的影响，特别关注具有增强对称性的BPS解和一般情况下的头对头碰撞。

Conclusion: 大质量束缚模的激发会显著改变Abelian-Higgs模型中涡旋的动力学行为，虽然BPS解的地测线结构保持不变，但实际运动轨迹因模生成力而偏离，导致更复杂的混沌动力学，这对理解涡旋系统的集体行为具有重要意义。

Abstract: We analyze how the geodesic motion in the 3- and 4-vortex sectors of the Abelian-Higgs model at critical coupling is deformed by the excitation of a massive bound mode. We find that the geodesics corresponding to BPS solutions with enhanced symmetry remain unchanged, although the direction of the actual motion depends on the mode-generated force, i.e., a force arising from the change of the mode frequency along the geodesic. In a generic case, for example in head-on collisions between the axially symmetric 1- and 2-vortex or between two 2-vortices, the vortex trajectories can differ strongly from the BPS geodesic. This enhances the chaotic behavior in the formation of the final state.

*David Berenstein,Hiroki Kawai*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 在方格晶格上重新表述Kogut-Susskind哈密顿量为约束一维自旋链模型，基于Bethe ansatz方法分析自旋链的可积性，并考虑弦理论的zigzag对称性约束。

Result: 发现存在大量可积子空间，但完整自旋链由于弦理论的zigzag对称性约束而不可积；通过外推基于可积子空间的一阶解析结果，自旋链描述能正确估算粗糙化转变点；高维推广中，无zigzag约束的小子空间同样可积。

Abstract: We study the strong coupling expansion of large $N$ QCD in various dimensions, reformulating the Kogut-Susskind Hamiltonian on a square lattice in terms of (constrained) one dimensional spin chain models. We study the integrability properties of the spin chain obtained this way: there is large class of integrable subsectors, but we show that the full spin chain is not integrable, at least when viewed from a description based on Bethe ansatz. We demonstrate that the spin chains no longer possess integrability due to the constraints arising from the zigzag symmetry of the confining strings. The spin chain description properly estimates the roughening transition point by extrapolating the first-order analytical results based on integrability of some subsectors. The generalization to higher dimensions are also considered, where we also find the small subsectors without the zigzag constraints to be integrable.

### [71] [Regge trajectories from the adjoint sector of Matrix Quantum Mechanics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04522)
*Igor R. Klebanov,Henry W. Lin,Pavel Meshcheriakov*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该研究重新审视了SU(N)对称量子力学的大N极限，发现在费米能级接近势能最大值时存在临界行为，对应于二维弦论。通过求解Marchesini-Onofri方程，揭示了伴随表示（adjoint sector）中的新现象：临界点处谱由Regge轨迹主导，能量特征值按Δ² ∼ n/α'增长，对应于"短"折叠开弦的振荡激发。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 重新审视SU(N)对称量子力学的大N（large N）极限，特别是其伴随表示（adjoint sector）的行为。已知单态（singlet）部分可通过自由费米子精确求解，但伴随表示在临界点附近的行为尚未充分探索。

Method: 采用半经典近似（semiclassical approximations）数值和解析求解Marchesini-Onofri方程。研究费米能级（Fermi level）接近势能最大值时的临界行为，分析不同势能函数趋近临界点的方式。

Result: 在临界点处，能谱由Regge轨迹主导，能量特征值按Δ² ∼ n/α'增长。在二维弦论对偶中，这些态被解释为"短"折叠开弦（"short" folded open string）的振荡激发。该Regge行为具有普适性，对趋近临界点的具体势能选择不敏感。稍微偏离临界点时，高激发态转变为延伸到Liouville方向的"长弦"（"long strings"）。

Conclusion: SU(N)对称量子力学在临界点附近展现出与二维弦论相关的丰富物理现象。伴随表示中的Regge轨迹行为揭示了弦论激发的普适特征，为理解量子力学与弦论之间的对偶关系提供了新见解。

Abstract: We reexamine the large $N$ limit of SU$(N)$ symmetric quantum mechanics of a Hermitian matrix whose singlet sector is well known to be exactly solvable via free fermions. When the Fermi level approaches a maximum of the potential, there is critical behavior corresponding to string theory in two dimensions. We uncover new phenomena in the adjoint sector by solving the Marchesini-Onofri equation both numerically and analytically using semiclassical approximations: at criticality, the spectrum is governed by Regge trajectories with energy eigenvalues growing according to $Δ^2 \sim n/ α'$. In the dual 2D string theory, we interpret these states as oscillatory excitations of a ``short'' folded open string. Up to sub-leading corrections, this Regge behavior is essentially universal and is insensitive to the particular potential we choose to approach criticality. Slightly away from criticality, the highly excited states transition into ``long strings'' that extend far into the Liouville direction.

### [74] [Holographic QCD and quarkonium melting: Finite temperature, density, and external field effects in self-consistent dynamical models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04725)
*Bruno Toniato*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 在爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦-伸缩子（Einstein-Maxwell-dilaton）框架内，从耦合场方程推导出自洽的动力学全息QCD模型。此外，使用非线性爱因斯坦-玻恩-因费尔德-伸缩子（Einstein-Born-Infeld-dilaton）模型研究磁场效应。

Result: 有限温度分析揭示了禁闭-退禁闭相变（confinement-deconfinement transition）和夸克偶素的顺序熔化。有限密度下，化学势增加会加速介子熔化，谱函数在相变线附近平滑演化。磁场效应显示出从逆磁催化（inverse magnetic catalysis）到磁催化（magnetic catalysis）的转变，突显了空间各向异性对夸克偶素稳定性的影响。

Conclusion: 该研究成功构建了全息QCD模型，系统地分析了温度、密度和磁场对重介子与奇异介子性质的影响，揭示了相变行为和熔化机制，为理解QCD非微扰现象提供了全息视角。

Abstract: This MSc dissertation is based on the papers arXiv:2502.12694 and arXiv:2408.14813. The AdS/CFT correspondence provides a powerful framework for modeling strongly coupled gauge theories and, as a consequence, investigating non-perturbative phenomena in QCD. In this work, following an overview of the ideas that encapsulate the AdS/CFT correspondence, we present a self-consistent dynamical holographic QCD model within the Einstein-Maxwell-dilaton framework, derived from the coupled field equations, to study the mass spectra and melting behavior of heavy and exotic mesons at finite temperature and density. At finite density, an increase in chemical potential accelerates meson melting, with spectral functions evolving smoothly across the phase transition line. Finally, using a nonlinear Einstein-Born-Infeld-dilaton model, magnetic field effects demonstrate a shift from inverse magnetic catalysis to magnetic catalysis, highlighting the impact of spatial anisotropy on quarkonium stability.

Abstract: We present a data-driven investigation of the exhaustive ensemble of no-scale type IIB flux vacua constructed in \cite{Chauhan:2025rdj}. Method: 研究方法包括分析闭超弦运动方程至三阶，并纳入$α'$修正。通过计算形变模量的高阶修正来测试精确边际性，同时在场论极限下与已知的Eguchi-Hanson引力瞬子解进行比较。

Abstract: We test exact marginality of the deformation describing the resolution of a $\mathbb{Z}_2$ orbifold by analyzing the closed superstring equations of motion to third order in the size, including $α'$ corrections. We benchmark this framework in a U(1) gauge theory with and without matter fields. ### [79] [Introduction to holography](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05186)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 全息原理（holography）是量子引力研究的一种流行方法，其中引力理论可以通过一个本身不含引力的低维边界理论来描述。最具体的全息模型是AdS/CFT对应关系，该课程旨在为学习者提供对这一重要理论框架的系统性教学介绍。

Method: 课程采用渐进式教学结构：首先回顾量子场论中的庞加莱对称性（Poincaré symmetry），然后讨论共形不变量子场论（CFT）中的共形对称性（conformal symmetry）。接着介绍AdS物理基础，最后将CFT和AdS要素结合，系统阐述AdS/CFT对应关系及其扩展内容。

Result: 课程讲义构建了完整的全息原理知识体系，涵盖了从对称性基础到AdS/CFT对应关系的核心内容，包括有限温度AdS/CFT、黑洞热力学，以及全息中"引力从纠缠中涌现"这一重要概念的介绍。

Conclusion: 该课程讲义为全息原理提供了系统的教学框架，通过对称性分析、AdS物理和CFT理论的结合，深入阐述了AdS/CFT对应关系及其在量子引力研究中的核心地位，特别强调了对称性在全息对偶中的关键作用。

Abstract: These are course notes for the 'Introduction to holography' Master level course at University of Cologne. The goal of the course is to give a pedogogical introduction to holography. Holography is a popular approach to quantum gravity, in which a theory of gravity can be described by a lower-dimensional boundary theory that itself has no gravity. The most concrete known example of a holographic model is the AdS/CFT correspondence, where the gravitational theory has a negative cosmological constant (the universe is asymptotically Anti-de Sitter) and the boundary theory is a conformal field theory. Symmetry plays a very important role in this duality. We therefore start the course with a review of Poincaré symmetry in quantum field theory, before moving on in the second chapter to conformal symmetry in conformally invariant quantum field theories or CFT's. Then we move to the basics of AdS physics in chapters 3 and 4, which will already reveal hints to the existence of a duality with CFT. After gathering the basic ingredients (CFT and AdS), in the second half of the course we are ready to formulate the AdS/CFT correspondence (chapter 5), including finite temperature AdS/CFT (chapter 6), which involves black holes and their thermodynamics in the gravitational theory (chapter 7). We end the course with an introduction to entanglement in AdS/CFT and the origin of statements that 'gravity emerges from entanglement' in holography.

### [81] [Discrete \texorpdfstring{$θ$}{theta} Projection: A Gauge-Protected Solution to the Strong CP Problem Without Axions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05195)
*Sameer Ahmad Mir,Bobby Eka Gunara,Mir Faizal*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种解决强CP问题的新机制——离散θ投影（Discrete theta Projection），通过规范化θ参数的离散平移对称性，无需轴子（axion）即可动态选择接近CP对称点的真空分支，从而自然解释中子电偶极矩的微小性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 强CP问题（strong CP problem）的核心在于解释为何QCD的物理θ-bar参数必须极其微小以满足中子电偶极矩（neutron electric dipole moment）的严格限制。传统的Peccei-Quinn轴子模型虽然能动态弛豫θ-bar，但依赖于可能被量子引力破坏的近似全局对称性，且面临严峻的天体物理和宇宙学约束。

Method: 提出离散θ投影（Discrete theta Projection）方法，通过规范化θ参数2π平移对称性的有限循环子群Z_N来实现。该方法将QCD与紧致、局域且带隙的拓扑扇区耦合，使路径积分（path integral）轨道化（orbifolds），识别相差2π/N的θ值，并仅允许拓扑荷（topological charge）属于Z_N的瞬子扇区。该构造可通过高阶形式/双群结构（higher-form/two-group structure）表述，其整数量子化耦合由反常流入（anomaly inflow）固定。

Result: 在大四维体积极限下，真空能（vacuum energy）成为轨道化像的下包络，理论动态选择最接近CP对称点的分支，从而强制实现|θ-bar| ≤ π/N，无需预先假设其微小性。该框架预测中子电偶极矩被1/N压低，无轴子信号，无畴壁/等曲率（domain-wall/isocurvature）问题，并具有晶格诊断特征：θ依赖呈现分段解析性，在约化周期的奇数分数处出现尖点，全局曲率按1/N^2标度。

Conclusion: 离散θ投影提供了一种无轴子、受规范保护的强CP问题解决方案。该构造具有辐射和引力稳定性，满足混合规范-引力一致性条件，并通过有效场论构造、真空投影的非微扰证明、完整反常分析以及UV嵌入（包括离散钟摆链）展示了其理论自洽性。

Abstract: We address the strong CP problem: why the physical QCD angle theta-bar must be extraordinarily small given the stringent bounds on the neutron electric dipole moment. Peccei-Quinn axion models can relax theta-bar dynamically, but rely on an approximate global symmetry expected to be violated by quantum gravity and face severe astrophysical and cosmological constraints. We propose Discrete theta Projection, an axionless, gauge-protected resolution obtained by gauging a finite cyclic subgroup $Z_N $of the $2π$ shift symmetry of theta. Coupling QCD to a compact, local and gapped topological sector orbifolds the path integral, identifying theta values that differ by $2π/N$ and admitting only instanton sectors whose topological charge lies in $Z_N$. In the large four-volume limit the vacuum energy becomes the lower envelope of the orbifold images, so the theory dynamically selects the branch closest to the CP-symmetric point, enforcing $|\barθ| \le π/N$ without assuming any prior smallness. Because the discrete shift is gauged, continuous renormalization of theta is forbidden; the construction can be formulated via higher-form/two-group structure with integer-quantized couplings fixed by anomaly inflow, ensuring radiative and gravitational stability and satisfying mixed gauge-gravity consistency conditions. The framework predicts a neutron EDM suppressed by $1/N$, no axion signatures, no domain-wall/isocurvature issues, and lattice diagnostics: piecewise-analytic theta dependence with cusps at odd fractions of the reduced period and a global curvature scaling as $1/N^2$. We provide the EFT construction, a nonperturbative proof of vacuum projection, a full anomaly analysis, and UV embeddings (including discrete clockwork chains) that generate large effective N while preserving integrality and consistency throughout.

Focusing on a pair of charged particles interacting via a scalar field, we quantise Hamilton's equations both in flat space and around a non-zero background, perturbing in post-Lorentzian (PL) and self-force (SF) expansions respectively. Our quantisation procedure provides access to the Magnus series, and is perfectly suited for computing matrix elements of $\hat{N}(t,t_0)=- i \hbar \log\hat{U}(t,t_0)$, both with and without external scalar states, for finite time intervals (bound orbits) and infinite time intervals (scattering). We also demonstrate how $\hat{N}$-matrix elements encode physical observables, providing a unified operator-based framework for conservative and radiative dynamics of binary systems.   <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于从基础孤子场论描述出发，系统推导宇宙弦的低能有效作用量，并探究曲率修正项的存在性及其物理机制。

Method: 采用解析与数值相结合的方法：首先从阿贝尔-希格斯模型的孤子场论描述出发，系统推导低能有效作用量；然后使用自适应网格细化的晶格模拟，对完整场论运动方程进行数值验证。

Result: 研究结果表明：当仅保留平移戈德斯通模时，不存在非平凡曲率修正项；曲率贡献仅通过大质量模与世界叶里奇标量的耦合进入有效理论；数值模拟证实了有效作用量在有效范围内的动力学行为，并预测了激发弦的参数不稳定性。

Conclusion: 本文成功建立了宇宙弦的有效理论框架，揭示了曲率修正的物理机制，并通过数值模拟验证了理论预测，包括激发弦的参数不稳定性导致能量从大质量激发向戈德斯通扇区转移的过程。

Abstract: We present a combined analytical and numerical study of the effective action of field theory cosmic strings in the Abelian-Higgs model in flat space. Starting directly from the underlying solitonic field theory description, we provide a systematic derivation of the low energy effective action and present evidence for the absence of nontrivial curvature correction terms when only the translational Goldstone modes are retained. Using this framework, we extend the effective theory to include higher energy fluctuations of the soliton profile, which map to massive degrees of freedom propagating on the worldsheet. We show that the leading curvature contribution enters only through the coupling between these massive modes and the worldsheet Ricci scalar. We validate the resulting effective theory via lattice simulations of the full field theory equations of motion in flat space, implemented with Adaptive Mesh Refinement to capture the string dynamics across different scales. The numerical simulations confirm the dynamics obtained using the effective action in its validity range. Furthermore, they also demonstrate the existence of the predicted parametric instability of excited strings that drives the transfer of energy from massive excitations to the Goldstone sector.

</details>


### [84] [Gauge-string duality, monomial bases and graph determinants](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05259)
*Garreth Kemp,Sanjaye Ramgoolam*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种基于退化图（degeneracy graph）的构造方法，用于在有限维交换结合半单代数中构建单项式基（monomial basis），并探讨其在量子信息理论和AdS/CFT对偶中的应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机源于AdS/CFT对偶（AdS/CFT correspondence）与量子信息理论（quantum information theory）交叉领域的问题，特别是需要研究在有限维交换结合半单代数（finite-dimensional commutative associative semisimple algebras）的递增子代数序列中的投影算子（projectors）。

Method: 方法包括定义退化图（degeneracy graphs）——一种有限分层树图，其节点代表连续子代数中的投影算子。利用退化图的组合性质，给出了用生成元单项式（monomials in the generators）构造代数线性基（linear basis）的简单公式。

Result: 研究证明该构造与代数中投影算子的计数要求兼容，并给出了单层和双层退化图中投影算子的显式构造。通过计算行列式提供了矩阵可逆性的广泛计算证据，在单层情况下该行列式为范德蒙行列式（Vandermonde determinant）。

Conclusion: 该构造通过对称群代数中心（centres of symmetric group algebras）和由Jucys-Murphy元素生成的最大交换子代数（maximally commuting subalgebras）等示例进行说明。单项式基在构造非交换半单代数中矩阵单元（matrix units）的算法中具有应用价值，与多矩阵规范不变算子（multi-matrix gauge-invariant operators）的正交基和量子信息理论相关。

Abstract: Questions at the intersection of the AdS/CFT correspondence and quantum information theory motivate the study of projectors in sequences of subalgebras of finite-dimensional commutative associative semisimple algebras $\mathcal{A}$, obtained by incrementally adjoining one generator at each step to produce a non-linear generating set for $\mathcal{A}$. We define degeneracy graphs, which are finite layered tree graphs whose nodes represent projectors in the successive subalgebras. Using combinatorial properties of the degeneracy graph, we give a simple formula for constructing a linear basis of $\mathcal{A}$ in terms of monomials in the generators.The nodes can be labelled by formal variables corresponding to the eigenvalues of the generators added at each layer. We prove that the construction is compatible with the required counting of projectors in $\mathcal{A}$, and give explicit constructions of the projectors in terms of the monomials, in the cases of one- and two-layer degeneracy graphs with arbitrary numbers of nodes. More generally, we provide extensive computational evidence for the invertibility of the matrix relating the proposed monomial basis to the projector basis, by evaluating its determinant. In the 1-layer case, this is a Vandermonde determinant. A simple formula for the non-vanishing determinant in the general layer case is conjectured and supported by the computational data. The construction is illustrated with examples including centres of symmetric group algebras and maximally commuting subalgebras generated by JucysMurphy elements. We outline applications of the monomial basis to algorithms for constructing matrix units in non-commutative semisimple algebras, with relevance to orthogonal bases of multi-matrix gauge-invariant operators and to quantum information theory.

</details>

*Valentina Bevilacqua,Giuseppe Dibitetto,Giuseppe Sudano*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究在已知的7维半最大规范超重力描述基础上，引入与时空填充源相关的开弦自由度（包括标量和通量）对理论的影响，扩展对这类扭曲紧致化系统的理解。

Method: 从7维超重力角度出发，通过将引力多重态与额外矢量多重态耦合，并向描述规范化的嵌入张量（embedding tensor）添加新分量，实现开弦自由度的引入。

Result: 基础理论的标量势（scalar potential）展现出新颖的AdS7真空解，包括有超对称和无超对称的情况；同时探索了不同真空对之间插值的畴壁解（domain wall solutions），并给出了解析和数值解。

Abstract: Warped compactifications of massive type IIA supergravity on a 3-sphere with spacetime-filling O6/D6 sources are known to admit a half-maximal gauged supergravity description in 7D. We study the effect of introducing open string degrees of freedom (scalars and fluxes) in such dimensional reductions, associated with the spacetime-filling sources. From the 7D supergravity point of view, this can be realized by coupling the gravity multiplet with extra vector multiplets and adding new components to the embedding tensor describing the gauging. The scalar potential of the underlying theory exhibits novel AdS7 vacuum solutions, with and without supersymmetry. Finally, we explore the net of domain wall solutions interpolating between the different pairs of vacua, and present analytical as well as numerical solutions.

### [86] [Scattering amplitudes in dimensionless quadratic gravity coupled to QED](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05476)
*I. F. Cunha,A. C. Lehum*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该研究分析了在引力理论（agravity）与阿贝尔规范理论耦合框架下的超普朗克能标$2\to2$散射过程，推导了多种树级散射通道的紧凑解析表达式，揭示了微分截面在超普朗克能区的普适标度行为$dσ/dΩ\propto 1/s$。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索无标度且可重整化的二次量子引力理论（agravity）与阿贝尔规范理论耦合时，如何在高能区（超普朗克能标）重塑熟悉的量子电动力学（QED）散射过程，为研究引力理论中红外定义和紫外一致性提供解析基础。

Method: 方法聚焦于带电费米子和标量粒子与光子及高阶导数引力子的相互作用，系统计算了包括光子-光子、费米子-费米子、费米子-光子、标量-费米子、标量-光子、标量-标量以及湮灭通道在内的广泛树级过程未极化平方矩阵元，并保留了光子-引力子干涉贡献。

Result: 结果显示振幅具有特征性的前向/后向增强效应，这与小动量转移相关且被$1/p^{4}$引力子传播子放大；所有分析通道的微分截面均表现出普适的超普朗克标度行为$dσ/dΩ\propto 1/s$，其中$s$为曼德尔斯坦不变量（质心能量平方）。

Conclusion: 该研究提供了高阶导数引力在超普朗克能区如何重塑QED散射的统一振幅级描述，所得解析结果为后续研究引力理论中物质场的红外定义和紫外一致性问题提供了基础构建模块。

Abstract: We study ultra-Planckian $2\to2$ scattering in an Abelian gauge theory coupled to agravity, the scale-free and renormalizable realization of quadratic quantum gravity. Focusing on charged fermions and scalars interacting with the photon and the higher-derivative graviton, we present compact analytic expressions for the unpolarized squared matrix elements for a broad set of tree-level processes, including photon--photon, fermion--fermion, fermion--photon, scalar--fermion, scalar--photon, scalar--scalar, and annihilation channels. In contrast to purely graviton-mediated analyses, we retain systematically the photon--graviton interference contributions and verify explicitly the independence of the results on the gravitational gauge-fixing parameter. The amplitudes display characteristic forward/backward enhancements associated with small momentum transfer, amplified by the $1/p^{4}$ graviton propagator, while their high-energy scaling reflects the underlying dimensionless gravitational couplings. Moreover, for all channels analyzed the corresponding differential cross sections exhibit the universal ultra-Planckian scaling $dσ/dΩ\propto 1/s$, where $s$ is the Mandelstam invariant (the squared center-of-momentum energy). Our results furnish a unified amplitude-level description of how higher-derivative gravity reshapes familiar QED scattering at ultra-Planckian energies and provide analytic building blocks for further studies of IR definitions and UV consistency in agravity with matter.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究低能标下夸克-轻子统一的可能性，特别是在多TeV能标建立物质统一的最小框架，其中中微子质量必然通过逆跷跷板机制生成，旨在评估该超越标准模型（BSM）理论的可检验性。

Method: 分析当前实验约束并推导对称性破缺能标的下限；重新审视来自轻子数破坏（lepton number violating）介子衰变的现有限制，考虑未知夸克-轻子混合角（quark-lepton mixing angles）的自由度；研究介子衰变与μ→e转换（μ→e conversion）界限之间的相关性。

Result: 推导了对称性破缺能标的相应下限；展示了介子衰变约束与μ→e转换界限之间的相关性；证明费米实验室（Fermilab）即将进行的μ→e转换实验在探测多TeV能标夸克-轻子统一方面可发挥关键作用。

Conclusion: 多TeV能标的夸克-轻子统一理论可通过当前实验约束进行检验，特别是未来μ→e转换实验将成为探测该统一框架的关键工具，为超越标准模型物理提供重要测试途径。

Abstract: We explore the idea of quark-lepton unification at low energies. In particular, we discuss the minimal framework for matter unification at the multi-TeV scale, in which neutrino masses are necessarily generated via the inverse seesaw mechanism. To assess the testability of this theory for physics beyond the Standard Model, we analyze current experimental constraints and derive the corresponding lower bound on the symmetry breaking scale. We reexamine the impact of existing limits from lepton number violating meson decays, taking into account the freedom associated with unknown quark-lepton mixing angles. Furthermore, we study the correlation between bounds from meson decays and $μ\to e$ conversion. We demonstrate that the upcoming $μ\to e$ conversion experiment at Fermilab can play a crucial role in probing quark-lepton unification at the multi-TeV scale.

### [88] [A baryon-calibrated unified quark-diquark effective mass formalism for heavy multiquarks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04175)
*Binesh Mohan,Rohit Dhir*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于夸克-双夸克有效质量形式化的统一框架，用于研究重四夸克和五夸克系统，将重子校准的构造扩展到多夸克态而不引入扇区依赖参数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于建立一个统一框架来处理重四夸克和五夸克系统，扩展重子校准的构造方法到多夸克态，同时避免引入扇区依赖参数，确保动力学一致性。

Method: 方法基于夸克-双夸克有效质量形式化（quark-diquark effective mass formalism），将双夸克内的色-自旋关联编码在从重子谱学固定的有效双夸克质量中，而簇间色磁标度则独立地从矢量-赝标量介子劈裂确定，并保持不变地传播到奇异构型中。

Result: 在该框架下计算了四夸克中$\bar{\mathbf{3}}_c\otimes\mathbf{3}_c$和$\mathbf{6}_c\otimes\bar{\mathbf{6}}_c$构型的完整谱，五夸克分析则聚焦于主导的$\bar{\mathbf{3}}_c\otimes\bar{\mathbf{3}}_c\otimes\bar{\mathbf{3}}_c$聚类。重夸克自旋对称性和轻、粲、底扇区间的味对称性破缺通过校准耦合的显式$1/(m_{D_1}m_{D_2})$标度自然出现。

Conclusion: 该框架为重重子谱学提供了一个参数经济、系统约束的基准，具有统一的动力学一致性。所得谱展示了跨越重子和多夸克态的相干动力学层次，已确立的奇异候选态在强子不确定性范围内被重现，而统一校准实现了跨味扇区的定量预测控制。

Abstract: We present a unified framework for heavy tetraquark and pentaquark systems within the quark-diquark effective mass formalism, extending its baryon-calibrated construction to multiquark states without introducing sector-dependent parameters. Intra-diquark color-spin correlations are encoded in effective diquark masses fixed from baryon spectroscopy, while the inter-cluster chromomagnetic scale, independently determined from vector-pseudoscalar meson splittings, is propagated unchanged to exotic configurations, ensuring residual one-gluon exchange dynamics only between composite color sources. Within this framework, we compute the complete spectra for both $\bar{\mathbf{3}}_c\otimes\mathbf{3}_c$ and $\mathbf{6}_c\otimes\bar{\mathbf{6}}_c$ configurations in tetraquarks, whereas the pentaquark analysis focuses on the dominant $\bar{\mathbf{3}}_c\otimes\bar{\mathbf{3}}_c\otimes\bar{\mathbf{3}}_c$ clustering. Heavy-quark spin symmetry and flavor-symmetry breaking across light, charm, and bottom sectors emerge naturally through the explicit $1/(m_{D_1}m_{D_2})$ scaling of the calibrated couplings. The resulting spectra exhibit a coherent dynamical hierarchy spanning baryons and multiquark states. Established exotic candidates are reproduced within hadronic uncertainties, while the unified calibration enables quantitative predictive control across flavor sectors. The framework thus provides a parameter-economical, systematically constrained baseline with unified dynamical consistency for heavy multiquark spectroscopy.
