### [89] [Covariant canonical-spinor amplitudes for partial wave analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04487)
*Hong Huang,Yi-Ning Wang,Jiang-Hao Yu*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 提出了一种基于大质量旋量-螺旋度形式（massive spinor-helicity formalism）的协变轨道-自旋（LS）分解振幅方法，用于分波分析（partial wave analysis）。该方法利用大质量正则旋量变量（massive canonical-spinor variables）在单一小群空间（single little group space）中实现自旋-轨道分解，同时保持洛伦兹协变性（Lorentz covariance）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统LS方法在小群空间（little group space）中操作，而Zemach张量方法在SO(3)空间的双覆盖（double cover）中实现，但这些方法在恢复SO(3,1)洛伦兹协变性方面存在挑战。现有协变LS张量构造方法（如协变张量、纯自旋和一般自旋方案中的协变投影张量）难以在保持协变性的同时实现LS耦合的内在分离。

Method: 利用大质量正则旋量变量（massive canonical-spinor variables）确定一般三点振幅（three-point amplitudes）。通过将每个粒子的小群指标投影到一个单一小群空间中，实现自旋-轨道分解，同时旋量形式自然确保了洛伦兹协变性。该方法允许在任何参考系中直接计算，并在单一框架内简化级联衰变（cascade decays）处理，无需非协变处理中的额外对齐旋转。

Result: 在TF-PWA中实现了该方法，并分析了Λc⁺→Λπ⁺π⁰衰变过程。发现螺旋度（helicity）、传统LS和正则旋量振幅的拟合结果一致，验证了正则旋量振幅作为复杂衰变链（decay chains）现代分波分析实用工具的有效性。

Conclusion: 正则旋量振幅方法提供了一种协变的LS分解方案，克服了传统方法在保持洛伦兹协变性方面的限制。该方法为复杂衰变链的分波分析提供了实用工具，能够在单一框架内处理级联衰变，简化计算流程并确保物理结果的一致性。

Abstract: We propose a covariant orbital-spin ($LS$) decomposed amplitude for the partial wave analysis using the massive spinor-helicity formalism. First we review the traditional-$LS$ method in the little group space and the Zemach tensor method in the double cover of the $\mathrm{SO}(3)$ space. To recover the $\mathrm{SO}(3,1)$ Lorentz covariance, several Lorentz covariant $LS$ tensors have been constructed in several different methods: covariant tensor, covariant projection tensor in pure-spin and general-spin schemes, but performing a intrinsic separation between $LS$ coupling while maintaining covariance is not obvious. We utilize the massive canonical-spinor variables to determine general three-point amplitudes, in which the spin-orbital decomposition is realized in single little group space by projecting little group indices of each particles into one, while the Lorentz covariance is ensured by the spinor form naturally. This covariant spinor method allows direct evaluation in any frame and a streamlined treatment of cascade decays within a single frame without additional alignment rotations in non-covariant treatment. As a benchmark, we implement the method in TF-PWA and analyze $Λ_c^+\toΛπ^+π^0$, finding consistent fit results across the helicity, traditional-$LS$, and canonical-spinor amplitudes. This validates the canonical-spinor amplitude as a practical tool for modern partial wave analyses of complex decay chains.

</details>


### [90] [On the robustness of the indirect determination of the width of the detected Higgs boson](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05020)
*Panagiotis Stylianou,Georg Weiglein*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该研究分析了在标准模型扩展中，当希格斯玻色子的壳上和壳外耦合修正因子不同时，其总宽度的间接测量界限的有效性。研究发现，在大部分参数空间中，ATLAS和CMS的现有界限仍然有效，但在新粒子质量较小时可能出现偏差。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LHC实验通过假设壳上（on-shell）和壳外（off-shell）希格斯耦合修正因子相同来间接测量希格斯总宽度。然而，超出标准模型（BSM）的物理可能以不同方式影响这两个区域，从而使得实际宽度可能大于基于该假设得到的界限。

Method: 研究放松了壳上和壳外耦合修正因子相等的假设，分析了不同类型的标准模型扩展。特别考虑了带有额外标量态的扩展，这些态可能作为共振态或在圈图水平上贡献。

Result: 对于考虑的标量扩展情景，在大部分参数空间中ATLAS和CMS的间接界限仍然有效。例外情况出现在额外粒子质量相对较小的参数区域。与假设耦合修正因子相等的情况相比，放松该假设后希格斯总宽度的上限最多减弱约两倍。

Conclusion: 在现实的标准模型扩展中，放松LHC实验中使用的壳上和壳外耦合修正因子相等的假设，希格斯总宽度的上限最多比该假设有效时减弱约两倍。新粒子搜索实验有潜力进一步约束此类情景。

Abstract: The indirect determination of the total width of the detected Higgs boson that is carried out by the experimental collaborations at the LHC relies on the assumption that the coupling modifiers for the on-shell and off-shell couplings are the same. However, physics beyond the Standard Model affecting the on-shell and off-shell regions differently could invalidate this assumption, so that the actual width of the detected Higgs boson could be larger than the bounds obtained under this assumption. Relaxing the assumption and investigating different types of extensions of the Standard Model, we analyse under which conditions a larger total width of the detected Higgs boson is compatible with all experimental and theoretical constraints. For the considered scenarios of scalar extensions with an additional state contributing as a resonance or at the loop level, we find that the indirect bounds obtained by ATLAS and CMS remain valid over large parts of the parameter space, with the exception of parameter regions where the additional particles have relatively small masses. We discuss the potential of experimental searches for new particles to further constrain such scenarios. Based on the existing experimental and theoretical constraints we conclude that relaxing the assumption of equal on-shell and off-shell coupling modifiers that is used in the experimental analyses at the LHC yields an upper bound on the total width of the detected Higgs boson in realistic extensions of the Standard Model that is only weakened by up to a factor of about two compared to the case where this assumption is valid.

</details>


### [91] [Muon collider experiments as electron/positron beam sources: case studies of new light-particle searches](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05086)
*Yasuhito Sakaki,Daiki Ueda*

TL;DR: 该研究定量分析了从未来μ子对撞机（IMCC和μTRISTAN）中提取μ子衰变产生的高能电子/正电子的可行性，并基于两种对撞机的不同束流特性提出了互补的新物理搜索策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: μ子对撞机中μ子衰变自然产生的高强度电子和正电子具有高能量、高重复率和小本征不确定性的独特特征，这些特性在现有加速器设施中无法获得。研究旨在探索提取这些粒子用于物理研究的可行性。

Method: 采用蒙特卡洛模拟方法，针对IMCC和μTRISTAN两种代表性未来μ子对撞机设计，使用相应设计参数研究对撞机环弯曲段中衰变电子和正电子的空间、角度和能量分布。

Result: 研究发现，即使对于携带μ子束流能量大部分（约0.6-1.0）的高能电子，也能实现典型的0.1-10 mrad偏转。环弯曲磁铁（或提供等效场的磁铁）可有效作为预分离磁铁，在主分离磁铁前部分偏转束流，表明提取方案具有实际可行性。

Conclusion: 利用IMCC和μTRISTAN的独特束流特性，提出了互补的搜索策略：在μTRISTAN进行暗物质（dark matter）的丢失能量和动量搜索，在IMCC进行类轴子粒子（axion-like particles）和轻标量粒子的可见衰变搜索，这些策略能够探测当前和其他提议实验无法覆盖的参数空间。

Abstract: At muon colliders, muon decays naturally produce intense electrons and positrons with unique features, namely high energies, high repetition rates, and small intrinsic uncertainties, that are unavailable at existing accelerator facilities. We quantitatively study the feasibility of extracting such particles in two representative future muon collider designs, IMCC and $μ$TRISTAN. Using Monte Carlo simulations with the corresponding design parameters, we study the spatial, angular, and energy distributions of decay electrons and positrons in the curved sections of the collider ring. We find that typical deflections of $0.1-10~\mathrm{mrad}$ can be achieved even for high-energy electrons carrying large energy fractions ($\simeq 0.6 - 1.0$) of the muon beam energy, with the ring bending magnets (or magnets providing an equivalent field) effectively serving as a pre-septum magnet, that partially deflects the beam before the main septum magnet, suggesting that the extraction scheme could be practically feasible. Exploiting the distinct beam properties of IMCC and $μ$TRISTAN, we propose complementary search strategies, missing energy and momentum searches for dark matter at $μ$TRISTAN and visible-decay searches for axion-like particles and light scalars at IMCC, which probe parameter space beyond the reach of current and other proposed experiments.

</details>


### [92] [Axial-vector neutral-current measurements in coherent elastic neutrino-nucleus scattering experiments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05281)
*D. Aristizabal Sierra,Pablo M. Candela,Valentina De Romeri,Dimitrios K. Papoulias,Laura Trincado S*

Method: 研究评估了中微子和暗物质实验社区当前使用的靶材中矢量与轴矢分量的相对大小。通过识别氟基化合物作为最有前景的靶材，特别聚焦于八氟丙烷（C₃F₈），并考虑π介子衰变静止源和反应堆中微子通量进行分析。

Result: 研究发现氟基化合物是探测轴矢流事件率的最有前景靶材，其中八氟丙烷因其在自旋相关暗物质搜索中的广泛应用和对未来CEνNS实验的相关性而成为特别合适的候选。测量可在通量不确定性和探测器阈值条件下，实现轴矢耦合常数约10%水平的间接测定。

Conclusion: 轴矢流测量不仅能够间接确定轴矢耦合常数，还将通过CEνNS探测自旋相关的新物理场景。八氟丙烷等氟基化合物为这类测量提供了有前景的实验平台。

Abstract: Coherent elastic neutrino-nucleus scattering (CE$ν$NS) is predominantly governed by vector neutral-current interactions, with subleading contributions arising from the axial current in nuclei with non-zero ground-state spin. Experimentally, the extraction of axial-current contributions has been so far of little interest, mainly because of the challenges its measurement entail. In this work, we investigate the relative size of the vector and axial components for target materials currently employed by the neutrino and dark matter experimental communities. We identify fluorine-based compounds as the most promising targets for probing the axial-current event rate. Among them, octafluoropropane ($\text{C}_3\text{F}_8$) emerges as a particularly suitable candidate, given its widespread use in spin-dependent dark matter searches and its relevance for upcoming dedicated CE$ν$NS experiments. Considering both pion decay-at-rest and reactor neutrino fluxes, we show that such measurements can allow an indirect determination of the axial coupling at the $\sim 10\%$ level, depending on flux uncertainties and detector thresholds. We further emphasize that measurements of the axial current will allow to probe spin-dependent new physics scenarios through CE$ν$NS.

Abstract: We investigate the spectrum of $T_{ΥΥ}$ tetraquark candidates within a coupled-channels framework. We find a rich spectrum of resonant, and virtual, states distributed between the $η_b(1S)η_b(1S)$ and $Υ(2S)Υ(2S)$ thresholds. The pattern of poles exhibits approximate heavy-quark spin symmetry multiplets. Several states are dominated by a single channel and can be associated with threshold-driven structures, while higher-mass resonances show sizable mixing among channels involving radially excited bottomonia. The predicted widths range from tens to several hundred MeV. Branching ratios indicate that many states couple predominantly to final states with at least one excited bottomonium, whereas only a subset of the spectrum is expected to be visible in the $η_b(1S)η_b(1S)$, $η_b(1S)Υ(1S)$ and $Υ(1S)Υ(1S)$ channels. ### [94] [Connecting Flavor and Baryon Asymmetry via Leptogenesis in Effective Froggatt-Nielsen Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05372)
*Cheshta Batra,Rusa Mandal,Kunal Rawat,Tom Tong*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文在Froggatt-Nielsen框架中研究标准模型层次味结构，通过引入三个右手中微子和复系数，统一描述味层次、中微子质量、CP破坏、暗物质和重子生成。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究标准模型（Standard Model）层次味结构（hierarchical flavor structure）的起源，并扩展框架以统一描述中微子质量、CP破坏、暗物质（dark matter）和宇宙重子不对称性（baryon asymmetry of the Universe）。

Method: 采用Froggatt-Nielsen（FN）框架，通过$U(1)_{\rm FN}$对称性自发破缺产生费米子质量和混合模式；引入三个右手中微子（right-handed neutrinos, RHNs）实现Type-I跷跷板机制（Type-I seesaw mechanism）；允许复FN系数以描述CKM和PMNS矩阵；通过重RHNs的非平衡衰变产生轻子不对称性（lepton asymmetry）。

Result: 计算了相应的一圈CP不对称性（one-loop CP asymmetries）并纳入玻尔兹曼方程（Boltzmann equations）；证明在FN对称性破缺尺度$v_φ$的两个不同区域（freeze-in和freeze-out兼容区域）均可实现成功的热轻子生成（thermal leptogenesis）；大$v_φ$区域接近标准轻子生成极限，小$v_φ$区域需要共振增强（resonant enhancement）。

Conclusion: 该框架中$v_φ$同时控制RHNs质量以及flavon和暗物质扇区的相互作用强度，为味层次、中微子质量、CP破坏、暗物质和重子生成提供了预测性和统一的描述。

Abstract: We investigate the hierarchical flavor structure of the Standard Model in a Froggatt-Nielsen (FN) framework, where the spontaneous breaking of a $U(1)_{\rm FN}$ symmetry by a complex flavon field generates fermion masses and mixing patterns through higher-dimensional operators. Extending the setup with three right-handed neutrinos (RHNs), light neutrino masses arise via the Type-I seesaw mechanism. Allowing complex FN coefficients enables a consistent description of the CKM and PMNS matrices while inducing CP-violating signatures in meson decays. Building on our previous work, where the lightest RHN acts as a viable dark matter (DM) candidate produced through freeze-in or freeze-out mechanisms, we investigate the origin of the baryon asymmetry of the Universe. The heavier RHNs generate a lepton asymmetry through out-of-equilibrium decays, including both Standard Model channels and additional flavon-induced processes in which the flavon appears as an intermediate or final-state particle. We compute the corresponding one-loop CP asymmetries and incorporate these effects in the Boltzmann equations. We show that although freeze-in and freeze-out DM production occur in two qualitatively distinct regions of the FN symmetry-breaking scale $v_φ$, successful thermal leptogenesis can be achieved in both regimes. In the large-$v_φ$ (freeze-in-compatible) region the results approach the standard leptogenesis limit, while in the freeze-out-compatible region the lower value of $v_φ$ implies lighter RHNs, requiring resonant enhancement. This tightly constrained framework, in which $v_φ$ simultaneously controls RHN masses and the interaction strengths of the flavon and DM sectors, provides a predictive and unified description of flavor hierarchies, neutrino masses, CP violation, dark matter, and baryogenesis within a single effective theory.

They have also led to the intertwining of particle physics, cosmology, and strings. Since supersymmetry and supergravity are manifest in the low energy limit of superstring below the Planck scale, experimental test of them are of interest regarding the validity of the superstring itself. For that reason, over the past decades, after the advent of supersymmetry and SUGRA models, there have been sustained experimental searches for supersymmetry at colliders, in precision experiments, and in astrophysical and cosmological data. The SUSY and SUGRA models have also had deep impact on theories related to inflation, dark matter, and dark energy. The purpose of this article is to provide a view from the bridge of these developments over the past fifty years circa 1974-2024.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 研究结论表明，奇异隐底五夸克态的磁矩主要由整体自旋-味结构决定，对夸克团簇细节不敏感，这为未来奇特多夸克态（exotic multiquark states）的实验研究提供了理论基准（theoretical benchmarks）。

Abstract: We investigate the magnetic moments of strange hidden bottom pentaquark states within the constituent quark model considering molecular and compact configurations. The system with quark content qqqbb is analyzed in three scenarios a baryon meson molecular configuration bq1bq2q3 a diquark diquark antiquark configuration bq1q2q3b and a diquark triquark configuration bq1bq2q3. The negative parity states with are studied for strangeness. We find that for the dominant spin couplings and maximally aligned configurations the diquark diquark antiquark qqqbb and diquark triquark bqqqb descriptions yield identical or numerically very close magnetic moments indicating that in the hidden bottom sector the magnetic properties are governed primarily by the global spin flavor structure rather than clustering details. A systematic suppression with increasing strangeness and a clear spin hierarchy are observed in all configurations. Due to the large bottom quark mass, heavy quark contributions are strongly suppressed, making the magnetic moments primarily sensitive to light strange spin correlations. These results provide theoretical benchmarks for future experimental studies of exotic multiquark states.

### [98] [Renormalisation of Chiral Gauge Theories with Non-Anticommuting $γ_5$ at the Multi-Loop Level](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05059)
*Matthias Weißwange*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该论文系统研究了手征规范理论（chiral gauge theories）在维度正规化（dimensional regularisation）下的多圈重整化，采用BMHV方案处理γ₅非反对易性，并建立了恢复规范对称性的算法化程序，实现了阿贝尔手征规范理论的完整4圈重整化以及标准模型的1圈重整化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用数学上一致的Breitenlohner-Maison/'t Hooft-Veltman（BMHV）方案处理非反对易γ₅，基于量子作用原理（quantum action principle）建立了透明且完全算法化的对称性恢复程序，并开发了自动化高性能计算框架。

Result: 实现了阿贝尔手征规范理论的完整4圈重整化——这是BMHV方案迄今为止最高阶的应用，并完成了标准模型（Standard Model）在BMHV方案中的完整1圈重整化，分析了维度模糊性和不同正规化实现对应的消失细节。

Conclusion: 研究表明即使在很高圈阶下，对γ₅进行严格自洽的处理是可行的，为标准模型的完全自洽多圈重整化奠定了基础，并为未来高精度电弱现象学建立了坚实基础。

Abstract: This thesis presents a comprehensive study of the renormalisation of chiral gauge theories in dimensional regularisation (DReg) at the multi-loop level. We employ the mathematically consistent Breitenlohner-Maison/`t~Hooft-Veltman (BMHV) scheme with non-anticommuting $γ_5$, whose modified algebraic relations induce a spurious violation of gauge and BRST invariance. A central focus is the systematic restoration of the broken symmetry, for which we provide a transparent and fully algorithmic procedure based on the quantum action principle. A major achievement of this work is the complete 4-loop renormalisation of an Abelian chiral gauge theory -- the highest-order application of the BMHV scheme to date. This calculation is made possible by an automated, high-performance computational framework incorporating several optimised algorithms. Our results demonstrate that a rigorous, self-consistent treatment of $γ_5$ is feasible even at very high loop orders. We further analyse dimensional ambiguities and evanescent details corresponding to different implementations of the regularisation, and identify practically efficient prescriptions for $D$-dimensional fermions and gauge interactions. Building on these insights, we present the complete 1-loop renormalisation of the full Standard Model (SM) in the BMHV scheme, providing a first step towards a fully self-consistent multi-loop renormalisation of the SM and establishing a solid foundation for future high-precision electroweak phenomenology.

*Cheng-Wei Chiang,Shu-Yu Ho,Van Que Tran*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该论文提出，TeV能级的重中性轻子（HNLs）在通过逆跷跷板机制产生中微子质量的同时，可以解释暗物质（DM）的宇宙学丰度和衰变特性。自发轻子数破缺产生的赝Nambu-Goldstone玻色子作为轻暗物质候选者，其质量源于小的显式破缺项。相同的HNLs既产生中微子质量，又通过冻结机制产生暗物质，并介导其衰变为中微子，从而在中微子质量、暗物质遗迹丰度和寿命之间建立了紧密关联。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在建立中微子质量生成机制与暗物质性质之间的理论联系。当前需要解释中微子微小质量的起源，同时解决暗物质的宇宙学丰度和特性问题。通过重中性轻子（HNLs）框架，研究者试图将这两个基本物理问题统一起来，形成一个可预测且实验可检验的理论模型。

Method: 采用逆跷跷板（inverse-seesaw）机制产生中微子质量，其中TeV能级的重中性轻子（HNLs）是关键媒介。通过自发轻子数破缺产生赝Nambu-Goldstone玻色子作为暗物质候选者，其质量来源于小的显式破缺项。暗物质通过冻结机制（freeze-in）产生，并由相同的HNLs介导其衰变为中微子。

Result: 对于对撞机可探测的TeV能级HNLs，观测到的暗物质遗迹丰度和寿命限制指向亚GeV能级的暗物质质量。该框架预测在下一代探测器如Hyper-Kamiokande、DUNE和JUNO中可观测到相关中微子信号。研究建立了中微子质量生成与暗物质性质之间的可预测关联，为实验检验提供了明确目标。

Conclusion: 该研究证明，负责逆跷跷板中微子质量生成的TeV能级重中性轻子（HNLs）可以同时确定暗物质的宇宙学丰度和衰变特性。这一框架在中微子质量、暗物质遗迹丰度和寿命之间建立了紧密的关联性，为下一代中微子探测器提供了可观测的预测信号，实现了理论预测与实验检验的统一。

Abstract: We demonstrate that TeV-scale heavy neutral leptons (HNLs) responsible for inverse-seesaw neutrino mass generation can simultaneously fix the cosmological abundance and decay properties of dark matter (DM). The spontaneous breaking of lepton number gives rise to a pseudo-Nambu-Goldstone boson that serves as a light DM candidate, whose mass originates from a small explicit breaking term. The same HNLs that generate neutrino masses produce the DM via freeze-in and mediate its decay into neutrinos, leading to a tight correlation among neutrino masses, DM relic abundance, and DM lifetime. For collider-accessible TeV-scale HNLs, the observed relic density and lifetime constraints point to sub-GeV DM, yielding observable neutrino signals at next-generation detectors such as Hyper-Kamiokande, DUNE, and JUNO. This framework establishes a predictive and experimentally testable link between neutrino mass generation and dark matter.

</details>

Conclusion: MexNICA合作自2016年成立以来，在探测器技术、现象学研究和理论物理方面取得了显著进展，为NICA实验项目的成功实施做出了重要贡献。

Abstract: The MexNICA Collaboration coordinates the activities of Mexican scientists, engineers, postdoctoral fellows and students in the Multi-Purpose Detector experiment at the Nuclotron-based Ion Collider fAcility of the Joint Institute for Nuclear Research in Dubna, Russia. Established in 2016, the collaboration brings together five Mexican institutions whose contributions span detector development as well phenomenological and theoretical studies, including modeling by means of Monte Carlo simulations. This work summarizes the main achievements of MexNICA, consisting of the development of the miniBeBe trigger detector as well of results of phenomenological investigations of the baryon-rich region in the QCD phase diagram accessible at NICA energies, and theoretical advances based on lattice QCD and effective models.

### [101] [Superconducting States and Intertwined Orders in Metallic Altermagnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04503)
*Xuan Zou,Rafael M. Fernandes,Eduardo Fradkin*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文研究了交变磁体（altermagnet）中的多分量超导性和涨落诱导的交织序，揭示了丰富的相图结构，包括向列性和拓扑超导相。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 交变磁体作为具有节点自旋分裂能带结构的新型磁体，为研究非常规超导性和交织序提供了理想平台。本文旨在探究交变磁体中多分量超导性和涨落诱导的交织序的物理机制。

Method: 在平均场理论框架下，研究了一个具有$C_4T$对称性的相互作用$d$波金属交变磁体。分析了两个等自旋双分量$p$波能隙函数$(Δ_A^x,Δ_B^y)$和$(Δ_A^y,Δ_B^x)$的超导基态流形。

Result: 由于两组能隙函数在不同温度下凝聚，产生了具有多个超导相变的丰富相图。向列涨落增强不同超导分量间的竞争并稳定向列超导相，而自旋电流环涨落促进共存并选择一对手征态。

Conclusion: 研究结果揭示了交变磁体中配对结构，阐明了交织的次主导涨落如何塑造超导序，为实现向列性和拓扑超导性提供了理论途径。

Abstract: Altermagnets are a newly identified class of magnets with nodal spin-split band structures, providing a fertile platform for studying unconventional superconductivity and intertwined orders. Here we investigate multicomponent superconductivity and fluctuation-induced intertwined orders in an interacting $d$-wave metallic altermagnet that is invariant under a combination of a fourfold rotation $C_4$ and time-reversal symmetry $T$. Within mean-field theory, the superconducting ground-state manifold is described in terms of two equal-spin two-component $p$-wave gap functions $(Δ_A^x,Δ_B^y)$ and $(Δ_A^y,Δ_B^x)$, where $A$ and $B$ refer to the two spin-polarized Fermi surfaces related by $C_4T$ symmetry. Because these two sets of gap functions condense at different temperatures, a rich phase diagram with multiple superconducting phase transitions emerges. Distinct fluctuations of sub-leading normal-state instabilities that compete with altermagnetism lift the degeneracy of the multicomponent pairing state in different ways. While nematic fluctuations enhance competition between distinct superconducting components and stabilize nematic superconducting phases, spin current-loop fluctuations promote coexistence and select a pair of chiral states. Our results uncover the pairing structure and elucidate how intertwined sub-leading fluctuations shape superconducting order in altermagnetic metals, suggesting a route toward realizing nematic and topological superconductivity.

</details>


### [102] [Spectroscopic evidence of disorder-induced quantum phase transitions in monolayer Fe(Te,Se) superconductor](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04717)
*Guanyang He,Ziqiao Wang,Longxin Pan,Yuxuan Lei,Fa Wang,Yi Liu,Nandini Trivedi,Jian Wang*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究通过可控引入无序（disorder）探索了二维高温超导体中的超导-绝缘相变，揭示了无序增强的库珀对关联（Cooper pair correlation）在强无序条件下导致U形能隙（U-shaped gaps）的形成。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超导-绝缘相变（superconductor-insulator transition）作为量子相变（quantum phase transitions）的范例受到广泛关注，但无序在其中的作用因超导性与电子局域化（electron localization）的复杂相互作用而未被充分理解。

Method: 通过在二维高温超导体单层Fe(Te,Se)晶态薄膜上沉积铁簇（iron clusters）来可控引入无序，并利用扫描隧道谱（scanning tunneling spectroscopy）测量技术探测光谱演化。

Result: 随着无序增强，光谱从超导能隙（superconducting gaps）演变为绝缘能隙（insulating gaps）；强无序条件下观察到大的U形能隙，这归因于局域化增强的库珀对关联。

Conclusion: 该观测为理解低维和高温超导体在无序条件下的涌现相（emergent phases）提供了重要见解，揭示了无序对超导相变的关键影响机制。

Abstract: The superconductor-insulator transition as a paradigm of quantum phase transitions has attracted tremendous interest over the past three decades. While the magnetic field and carrier density can be tuned to drive the transition, the role of disorder in the transition is not well understood due to the complicated interplay between superconductivity and electron localization. In this work, we controllably introduce disorder in a two-dimensional high-temperature superconductor by depositing iron clusters onto the superconducting monolayer Fe(Te,Se) crystalline film. The spectral evolution from superconducting gaps to insulating gaps with increasing disorder is detected by scanning tunneling spectroscopy measurements. When the disorder is strong, large U-shaped gaps are observed and attributed to the localization-enhanced Cooper pair correlation. Our observations provide the insight into the emergent phases of low-dimensional and high-temperature superconductors with disorder.

</details>


### [103] [Spin-polarized Andreev molecules and anomalous nonlocal Josephson effects in altermagnetic junctions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04954)
*Sayan Mondal,Jorge Cayao*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文研究了两个约瑟夫森结（Josephson junctions）在d波交变磁性（d-wave altermagnetism）作用下的相干耦合，发现弱耦合时安德列夫束缚态（Andreev bound states）杂化形成自旋极化的安德列夫分子（spin-polarized Andreev molecules），从而诱导出反常非局域约瑟夫森效应（anomalous nonlocal Josephson effect）和非局域约瑟夫森二极管效应（nonlocal Josephson diode effect）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 交变磁性（altermagnetism）已成为实现非平凡约瑟夫森相（nontrivial Josephson phases）的有前景要素，但此前研究局限于单约瑟夫森结。本文旨在探索两个约瑟夫森结在交变磁性作用下的相干耦合效应。

Method: 研究考虑了两个具有自旋单态s波超导性（spin-singlet s-wave superconductivity）的约瑟夫森结的相干耦合，重点分析d波交变磁性（d-wave altermagnetism）对系统的影响。

Result: 弱耦合时，d波交变磁性导致每个结的安德列夫束缚态杂化，形成自旋极化的安德列夫分子。这些分子诱导出反常非局域约瑟夫森效应，其中由于交变磁性，一个结的相位变化会在另一个结中产生0-π和φ₀转变的电流。此外，非局域约瑟夫森电流表现出非互易临界电流，实现极性可通过交变磁强度和相位调谐的非局域约瑟夫森二极管效应。

Conclusion: 交变磁性为设计非局域自旋约瑟夫森现象（nonlocal spin Josephson phenomena）提供了有前景的平台，其独特的自旋极化安德列夫分子和非互易电流特性为新型量子器件设计开辟了道路。

Abstract: Altermagnetism has emerged as a promising ingredient for realizing nontrivial Josephson phases, but so far explored in single Josephson junctions. In this work, we consider the coherent coupling of two Josephson junctions with spin-singlet $s$-wave superconductivity and demonstrate that $d$-wave altermagnetism gives rise to spin-polarized Andreev molecules due to the hybridization of Andreev bound states of each junction when the coupling is weak. Interestingly, these spin-polarized Andreev molecules induce an anomalous nonlocal Josephson effect, where the current flow across one Josephson junction due to phase changes across the other junction develops $0-π$ and $φ_{0}$ transitions originating from altermagnetism. Furthermore, the nonlocal Josephson current carried by spin-polarized Andreev molecules exhibits nonreciprocal critical currents, enabling a nonlocal Josephson diode effect whose polarity is tunable by the altermagnetic strength and right phase. Our findings put forward altermagnetism as a promising arena for designing nonlocal spin Josephson phenomena.

</details>


### [104] [First-principles calculation of coherence length and penetration depth based on density functional theory for superconductors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05123)
*Mitsuaki Kawamura,Takuya Nomoto,Niklas Witt,Ryotaro Arita*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文开发了一种基于第一性原理的超导密度泛函理论（SCDFT）框架，用于一致性地计算超导相干长度ξ₀和磁穿透深度λ_L等基本长度尺度，并构建了完全基于第一性原理的Uemura图。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超导体的基本长度尺度（相干长度ξ₀和磁穿透深度λ_L）通常需要不同的理论框架分别计算，缺乏统一的第一性原理预测方法。本文旨在开发一个能够一致性地确定这些关键参数的理论框架。

Method: 通过将有限动量库珀对（finite-momentum Cooper pairs）纳入超导密度泛函理论（superconducting density functional theory, SCDFT），构建了一个微观方案，能够在同一理论基础上一致且无参数地确定ξ₀、λ_L和超导转变温度T_c。

Result: 该方法应用于代表性元素超导体、A15化合物V₃Si和高压下的H₃S，获得了与实验数据良好吻合的结果。通过统一获取ξ₀和λ_L，首次从第一性原理构建了Uemura图，揭示了常规元素超导体具有小的T_c/T_F比值，而高T_c体系则同时实现了强配对和大相位刚度。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了预测超导长度尺度的第一性原理路径，为超导中的经验相关性提供了微观解释，实现了对超导基本参数的一致性和无参数计算。

Abstract: We develop a first-principles framework for evaluating the fundamental length scales of superconductivity, namely the coherence length $ξ_0$ and the magnetic penetration depth $λ_\mathrm{L}$, within superconducting density functional theory (SCDFT). By incorporating finite-momentum Cooper pairs, we formulate a microscopic scheme that enables a consistent and parameter-free determination of $ξ_0$, $λ_\mathrm{L}$, and the superconducting transition temperature $T_\mathrm{c}$ on the same theoretical footing. Applying the method to representative elemental superconductors, the A15 compound V$_3$Si, and H$_3$S under high pressure, we obtain results in good agreement with available experimental data. Furthermore, the unified access to $ξ_0$ and $λ_\mathrm{L}$ allows us to construct the Uemura plot entirely from first principles, demonstrating that conventional elemental superconductors systematically exhibit small $T_\mathrm{c}$/$T_\mathrm{F}$, while higher-$T_\mathrm{c}$ systems are characterized by the simultaneous realization of strong pairing and large phase stiffness. Our results establish a predictive first-principles route to superconducting length scales and provide a microscopic interpretation of empirical correlations in superconductivity.

</details>


### [105] [Thin amorphous molybdenum silicide superconducting shells around individual nanowires deposited via magnetron co-sputtering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05176)
*Luize Dipane,Martins Zubkins,Gunta Kunakova,Eriks Dipans,Tom Yager,Boris Polyakov,Edgars Butanovs*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究展示了通过脉冲直流磁控共溅射技术在平面和纳米线基底上沉积非晶超导MoSi薄膜，通过调控Mo/Si比例将临界温度优化至7.25K，为量子器件应用提供了新材料平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 采用非晶超导体如二硅化钼（MoSi）替代晶体材料可显著简化材料沉积和纳米尺度原型制备，有利于量子电子和光子器件的制造。本研究旨在探索非晶超导MoSi薄膜在平面和纳米线基底上的沉积与应用。

Method: 采用脉冲直流磁控共溅射（pulsed direct-current magnetron co-sputtering）技术在氩气氛围中从钼和硅靶材共溅射沉积MoSi薄膜。基底包括氧化硅晶片和具有6nm Al2O3绝缘壳的Ga2O3纳米线。通过控制靶材溅射功率调节Mo/Si比例，使用扫描/透射电子显微镜、X射线衍射和X射线光电子能谱进行表征，并通过光刻技术制备四电极Cr/Au电接触进行低温电学测量。

Result: 通过优化Mo/Si比例，成功将MoSi薄膜的临界温度（critical temperature）Tc提升至7.25K。在Ga2O3-Al2O3-MoSi核壳纳米线上实现了超导壳层沉积，为量子器件应用提供了新型材料结构。

Conclusion: 这种超导壳层纳米线为基础研究和与其他材料的界面集成提供了新途径，有望推动量子器件应用的发展。非晶MoSi超导薄膜的沉积技术简化了纳米尺度原型制备，具有实际应用潜力。

Abstract: Employing amorphous superconductors, such as Type-II molybdenum silicide (MoSi), instead of crystalline materials significantly simplifies the material deposition and scalable nanoscale prototyping, beneficial for quantum electronic and photonic device fabrication. In this work, deposition of amorphous superconductive MoSi thin films on flat and nanowire (NW) substrates was demonstrated via pulsed direct-current magnetron co-sputtering from molybdenum and silicon targets in an argon atmosphere. MoSi films were deposited on oxidized silicon wafers and Ga2O3 NWs with 6 nm Al2O3 insulating shell, grown around the NWs using atomic layer deposition, and studied using scanning and transmission electron microscopy, X-ray diffraction, and X-ray photoelectron spectroscopy. Four-point Cr/Au electrical contacts were defined on the thin films and on individual Ga2O3-Al2O3-MoSi core-shell NWs using lithography for low-temperature electrical measurements. By controlling the sputtering power of the targets and thus adjusting the molybdenum-to-silicon ratio in the MoSi films, their properties were optimized to achieve critical temperature Tc of 7.25 K. Such superconducting shell NWs could provide new avenues for fundamental studies and interfacing with other materials for quantum device applications.

</details>


### [106] [Temperature-Dependent Dielectric Function of Tantalum Nitride Formed by Atomic Layer Deposition for Tunnel Barriers in Josephson Junctions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05383)
*Ekta Bhatia,Aaron Lopez Gonzalez,Yoshitha Hettige,Tuan Vo,Sandra Schujman,Kevin Musick,Thomas Murray,Kim Kisslinger,Chenyu Zhou,Mingzhao Liu,Satyavolu S. Papa Rao,Stefan Zollner*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文通过原子层沉积（ALD）制备绝缘氮化钽（TaN）薄膜，研究其介电函数以评估其作为超导量子电路中钽基约瑟夫森结（JJ）隧道势垒的适用性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在评估原子层沉积（ALD）氮化钽（TaN）薄膜作为钽基约瑟夫森结（Josephson junctions）隧道势垒的适用性，以替代传统的氧化铝（AlOx）势垒，从而改善超导量子电路的性能。

Method: 在300 mm硅/二氧化硅衬底上沉积不同厚度（13 nm和25 nm）的ALD TaN薄膜，采用变温椭圆偏振光谱法测量介电函数，并结合透射电子显微镜（TEM）、X射线衍射（XRD）和X射线光电子能谱（XPS）进行材料表征。

Result: ALD TaN薄膜在所有温度下均表现出绝缘特性（中红外透明），无自由载流子红外吸收，带隙为1.5-1.8 eV，氮/钽比约为1.2，且具有低粗糙度和热稳定性。

Conclusion: 与AlOx相比，ALD TaN具有更低的带隙、更好的厚度与成分控制、更低的粗糙度和抗老化能力，有望制备更厚势垒的约瑟夫森结，同时满足量子比特所需的临界电流密度。

Abstract: We report the dielectric functions of insulating tantalum nitride (TaN) films, deposited using atomic layer deposition (ALD) on 300 mm Si/SiO2 substrates, to demonstrate their suitability as tunnel barriers in tantalum-based Josephson junctions (JJ) for superconducting quantum circuits. The temperature-dependent ellipsometric angles were measured using ALD TaN films with nominal thicknesses of 13 nm and 25 nm at an incidence angle of 70 degrees, across photon energy ranges of 0.03 eV to 0.7 eV (80-300 K) and 0.5 eV to 6.5 eV (80-600 K). This data was used to develop a dispersion model for insulating ALD TaN films that incorporates a Tauc-Lorentz oscillator with a band gap of 1.5-1.8 eV to model the interband optical transitions. The extracted dielectric function of ALD TaN films shows an insulating behavior (mid-infrared transparency) at all temperatures and for both film thicknesses tested. ALD TaN does not exhibit infrared absorption due to free carriers, even at elevated temperatures, demonstrating its insulating nature, which is required for the tunnel barrier of the JJ in quantum applications. The results of transmission electron microscopy, including selected area electron diffraction, and X-ray diffraction are also discussed. Sputter depth-profile X-ray photoelectron spectroscopy (XPS) shows an N/Ta ratio of ~1.2 throughout the film. The lower band gap, low roughness, and thermal stability of ALD TaN compared to AlOx suggest the possibility of fabricating JJs with thicker barriers while achieving critical current densities required for qubits, better control of thickness and composition, reduced topography, and resistance to aging.

</details>

### [107] [Strongly clustered random graphs via triadic closure: Degree correlations and clustering spectrum](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04669)
*Lorenzo Cirigliano,Gareth J. Baxter,Gábor Timár*

Main category: physics.soc-ph

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种用于强聚类随机图（strongly clustered random graphs）的模型，其中随机骨架（random backbone）中的每个三元组以特定概率闭合，并提供了局部聚类谱（local clustering spectrum）和度相关性（degree correlations）的精确表达式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现实世界网络常表现出强传递性（strong transitivity），具有非平凡的局部聚类谱和度相关性，但这些特征在易处理的网络模型中难以建模，阻碍了对复杂网络结构的理论理解。

Method: 采用强聚类随机图模型，其中随机骨架中的每个三元组以特定概率闭合，尽管获得的图具有复杂的环状局部结构，但提供了精确的解析表达式。

Result: 获得了局部聚类谱和度相关性的精确表达式，发现高传递性伴随正度同配性（positive degree assortativity），以及聚类谱中的非平凡结构，并通过数值模拟补充了有限尺寸效应分析。

Conclusion: 该研究填补了强聚类随机图模型理论描述的空白，为理解现实世界网络的复杂结构提供了精确的理论框架，特别是揭示了传递性与度相关性之间的关联。

Abstract: Real-world networks often exhibit strong transitivity with nontrivial local clustering spectra and degree correlations. Such features are not easily modelled in tractable network models, creating an obstacle to the theoretical understanding of such complex network structures. Here, we address this problem using a model for strongly clustered random graphs in which each triad of a random backbone is closed with a certain probability. Despite the intricate loopy local structure of the graphs obtained, we provide exact expressions for the local clustering spectrum and the degree correlations, filling the gap in the theoretical description of this model for random graphs. In particular, we find positive degree assortativity accompanies high transitivity, and non-trivial structure in the clustering spectrum. Exact asymptotic analytical results are complemented with extensive numerical characterization of finite size effects.

</details>


### [108] [Wealth Tax Neutrality as Drift-Shift Symmetry: A Statistical Physics Formulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05283)
*Anders G. Froeseth*

Main category: physics.soc-ph

TL;DR: 该研究将财富税中性框架重新表述为随机动力学和统计物理语言，通过福克-普朗克方程分析财富分布演化，揭示了税收中性对应于漂移系数平移对称性，并识别了实践中破坏中性的各种机制对应的对称性破缺。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在将Froeseth（2026）的财富税中性框架重新表述为随机动力学和统计物理语言，以更精确地理解财富税的中性特性及其在实践中的偏离机制。

Method: 采用几何布朗运动描述个体财富动态，建立朗之万方程（Langevin equation）和福克-普朗克方程（Fokker-Planck equation）框架；将比例财富税建模为漂移系数的均匀减少，分析其对称性特性。

Result: 发现比例财富税在市值评估下表现为漂移系数的平移对称性，这是税收中性的物理内涵；实践中破坏中性的各种机制（账面价值评估、流动性摩擦等）对应特定的对称性破缺，表现为状态依赖、资产依赖或流动依赖的福克-普朗克方程修正。

Conclusion: 该框架明确了财富税何时仅是动态过程的良性重新标度，何时引入了真正的新物理机制，为理解财富税的中性特性和实际效应提供了清晰的物理类比和数学表述。

Abstract: We reformulate the neutral wealth tax framework of Froeseth (2026) in the language of stochastic dynamics and statistical physics. Individual wealth under geometric Brownian motion satisfies a Langevin equation with multiplicative noise; the probability density of wealth across a population then evolves according to a Fokker-Planck equation. A proportional wealth tax at market value enters as a uniform reduction of the drift coefficient, preserving the diffusion structure and all relative probability currents. This drift-shift symmetry is the physical content of tax neutrality. Each channel through which neutrality breaks down in practice, book-value assessment, liquidity frictions, forced dividend extraction, migration, and market impact, corresponds to a specific violation of this symmetry: a state-dependent, asset-dependent, or flow-dependent modification of the Fokker-Planck equation. The framework clarifies when wealth taxation is a benign rescaling of the dynamics and when it introduces genuinely new physics.

</details>

### [109] [Raman scattering spectroscopic observation of a ferroelastic crossover in bond-frustrated PrCd$_3$P$_3$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04539)
*Jackson Davis,Jesse Liebman,Dibyata Rout,S. J. Gomez Alvarado,Stephen D. Wilson,Natalia Drichko*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究通过拉曼散射光谱揭示了PrCd₃P₃材料中CdP层的结构不稳定性及其对Pr³⁺离子晶体电场激发的影响，为通过半导体层调控三角晶格磁性层提供了新思路。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 三角晶格（triangular lattice）中的二维磁性已展现出承载奇异磁态的潜力，控制这些磁态（包括磁性质和电荷掺杂）是下一步目标。结合磁性三角晶格层与具有有趣结构或电子性质的层状材料特别有价值。

Method: 使用拉曼散射光谱（Raman scattering spectroscopy）研究PrCd₃P₃材料，该材料中磁性稀土离子三角晶格层与半导体六方CdP层交替排列。通过分析声子软模行为（soft mode behavior）和晶体电场激发（crystal electric field excitations）来探测结构不稳定性。

Result: 在CdP层中发现结构不稳定性，表现为这些层中声子的软模行为。拉曼散射检测到晶体电场激发，确认了Pr³⁺的单重态基态（singlet ground state），以及CdP层结构不稳定性导致的双重态能级分裂。尽管Pr³⁺在PrCd₃P₃中是非磁性的，但推测该材料家族可通过CdP层实现磁性层调控。

Conclusion: 该材料家族有望通过CdP层（在应变下可能变为铁电体）实现对磁性层的调控，从而缓解阻挫（frustration）。这种层间耦合为通过半导体层控制三角晶格磁性态提供了新途径。

Abstract: 2D magnetism in triangular lattices has already shown potential for hosting exotic magnetic states. Control of these magnetic states, both in terms of magnetic properties and in terms of charge doping would be the next step. This makes materials which combine triangular lattice magnetic layers with layers hosting interesting structural or electronic properties particularly useful. PrCd$_3$P$_3$, studied in this work, is one of a family of materials where triangular lattice layers of magnetic rare earth ions alternate with semiconducting hexagonal CdP layers. Using Raman scattering spectroscopy we uncover a structural instability in the CdP layers, associated with a soft mode behavior of a phonon in these layers. Raman scattering detects crystal electric field excitations, and confirms a singlet ground state for Pr$^{3+}$ and splitting of the doublet levels as a result of the structural instability in CdP layers. While Pr$^{3+}$ is non-magnetic in PrCd$_3$P$_3$ we speculate that this family of materials can realize control of the magnetic layer through the CdP layer which can become ferroelectric under strain that would relieve frustration.

</details>


### [110] [Rapid modeling of segregation-driven metal-oxide adhesion in high-entropy alloys using macroscopic atom model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04575)
*Dennis Boakye,Chuang Deng*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文扩展了宏观原子模型（MAM）用于预测高熵合金（HEAs）与金属氧化物之间的界面粘附性能，通过引入成分一致的表面分数和界面配对概率形式，克服了第一性原理计算的高成本限制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 准确预测高熵合金（HEAs）与金属氧化物之间的粘附性能具有挑战性，因为界面偏析、原子环境和宏观热力学量之间存在强相关性。单纯依赖第一性原理方法探索成分、溶质浓度和共偏析效应的成本过高。

Method: 扩展了多组分合金的宏观原子模型（macroscopic atom model, MAM），采用成分一致的表面分数（composition-consistent surface fractions）和界面配对概率形式（interfacial pair-probability formalism），以捕捉偏离随机接触统计的偏差。将该模型应用于CoCrFeNi（AlCoCrFeNi）HEA与Cr2O3（Al2O3）的接触体系。

Result: 模型能够预测偏析能和分离功作为成分的连续函数，正确再现了Hf、Y、Zr和S的偏析层级。同时捕捉到Al2O3界面更强的偏析趋势，以及表面能和粘附对溶质含量和共偏析的非线性依赖关系。与DFT计算结果对比显示一致趋势，特别是Hf和Zr通过强金属-氧键增强粘附，而S则削弱粘附。

Conclusion: 扩展的宏观原子模型提供了一个物理可解释、计算高效且定量预测的框架，可用于筛选超出DFT计算限制的偏析控制粘附性能，为高熵合金-氧化物界面设计提供了有效工具。

Abstract: Accurate prediction of metal-oxide adhesion in high-entropy alloys (HEAs) is challenging because interfacial segregation, atomic environments, and macroscopic thermodynamic quantities are strongly correlated. Relying solely on first-principles approaches is too expensive for exploring composition, solute concentration, and co-segregation effects. To address this, we extend the macroscopic atom model (MAM) for multicomponent alloys using composition-consistent surface fractions and an interfacial pair-probability formalism that captures deviations from random contact statistics. Applied to CoCrFeNi (AlCoCrFeNi) HEA in contact with Cr2O3 (Al2O3), the model predicts segregation energies and work of separation as continuous functions of composition, reproducing the correct segregation hierarchy of Hf, Y, Zr, and S. The stronger segregation tendency at Al2O3 interfaces, and the non-linear dependence of surface energy and adhesion on solute content and co-segregation is also captured. The results are benchmarked with DFT calculations, which shows consistent trends, particularly the strengthening of adhesion by Hf and Zr through strong metal-oxygen bonding and the weakening effect of S. These results demonstrate that the extended MAM provides a physically interpretable, computationally efficient, and quantitatively predictive framework for screening segregation-controlled adhesion beyond the limits of DFT.

</details>


### [111] [Moire Topological Magnetism Twist-Engineered from 2D Spin Spirals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04620)
*Zhonglin He,Kaiying Dou,Wenhui Du,Ying Dai,Evgeny Y. Tsymbal,Yandong Ma*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种无需外磁场即可实现二维拓扑磁性的通用方法，通过扭曲反铁磁双层结构将拓扑平庸的自旋螺旋转化为拓扑非平庸的磁结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 拓扑磁性（topological magnetism）具有丰富的物理特性和对自旋电子学（spintronics）的变革性前景，但其稳定通常需要外部磁场，限制了实际应用。因此需要开发无需外磁场的实现方法。

Method: 该方法利用扭曲反铁磁（antiferromagnetic）双层结构，其中两个子层的锁定自旋螺旋（spin spirals）在扭曲后形成空间交替的铁磁（ferromagnetic）和反铁磁（antiferromagnetic）畴。这些畴使均匀的反铁磁层间交换（interlayer exchange）受挫，从而自发稳定莫尔拓扑磁性（moire topological magnetisms）。研究采用第一性原理（first-principles）和原子自旋模型（atomistic spin-model）模拟进行验证。

Result: 以NiCl2和NiBr2双层为例验证了该方法。对于扭曲NiCl2，预测了可通过扭转角调谐的拓扑自旋态，包括孤立和高阶反铁磁双子（antiferromagnetic bimerons）。对于扭曲NiBr2，强受挫效应产生平庸的三重q自旋螺旋（triple-q spin spirals），但在垂直压缩应变（vertical compressive strain）作用下可转变为莫尔拓扑磁性。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明，拓扑非平庸自旋纹理（topologically non-trivial spin textures）可以从其拓扑平庸对应物中设计实现，这为拓扑自旋电子学提供了新的范式（paradigm）。

Abstract: Topological magnetism, characterized by topologically protected spin textures, offers rich physics and transformative prospects for spintronics. However, its stabilization typically demands external magnetic fields, preventing straightforward implementation. Here, we report a universal field-free approach for engineering 2D topologically-trivial spin spirals into topological magnetisms. This approach leverages twisted antiferromagnetic bilayers, where locked spin spirals in the two sublayers form spatially alternating ferromagnetic and antiferromagnetic domains upon twisting. These domains frustrate the uniform antiferromagnetic interlayer exchange, spontaneously stabilizing moire topological magnetisms without external fields. Using first-principles and atomistic spin-model simulations, we validate this approach using bilayers NiCl2 and NiBr2, as representative examples. For twisted NiCl2, we predict topological spin states tunable by the twist angle, including isolated and high-order antiferromagnetic bimerons. For twisted NiBr2, strong frustration yields trivial triple-q spin spirals, which transform into moire topological magnetism with the application of vertical compressive strain. Our findings demonstrate that topologically non-trivial spin textures can be engineered from their trivial counterparts, thus providing a new paradigm for topological spintronics

</details>


### [112] [High pressure melt dynamics in shock-compressed titanium](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04680)
*Saransh Singh,Reetam Paul,Nikhil Rampal,Rhys J. Bunting,Sebastien Hamel,Nathan Palmer,Christopher P. McGuire,Samantha M. Clarke,Amy Coleman,Cara Vennari,Trevor M. Hutchinson,\\Kimberly A. Pereira,Bob Nagler,Dimitri Khaghani,Hae Ja Lee,Nicholas A. Czapla,Travis Volz,Ian K. OCampo,James McNaney,Thomas E. Lockard,Jon H. Eggert,Amy Lazicki,Christopher E. Wehrenberg,Andrew Krygier,Raymond F. Smith*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究结合激光驱动冲击压缩、飞秒X射线衍射原位测量与基于机器学习原子势的分子动力学模拟，系统研究了钛的高压熔化行为，揭示了固液共存区间及残余晶体的持续存在现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探究钛在高压条件下的熔化行为，特别是通过先进实验技术与模拟方法相结合，精确确定熔化起始与完成压力，评估当前激光冲击实验平台在测定熔化压力方面的准确性。

Method: 采用激光驱动冲击压缩（laser-driven shock compression）结合原位飞秒X射线衍射（in situ femtosecond x-ray diffraction）实验技术，同时基于机器学习原子势（machine-learned interatomic potential）进行分子动力学（molecular-dynamics）模拟。

Result: 分子动力学模拟预测Hugoniot曲线上约111-124 GPa范围内存在固液共存；实验在86 GPa首次观测到液体证据，并在约110-126 GPa范围内观察到与液体出现相关的显著微观结构变化和强烈晶粒细化；在126 GPa以上，观察到高度织构化晶体钛的残余水平持续存在至约180 GPa，远高于预期熔化完成压力。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了钛在高压下的复杂熔化行为，包括固液共存区间和残余晶体的持续存在，并讨论了当前激光冲击实验平台在确定熔化起始与完成压力方面的准确性，为高压相变研究提供了重要见解。

Abstract: We study the high-pressure melting behavior of titanium using laser-driven shock compression with in situ femtosecond x-ray diffraction and molecular-dynamics simulations based on a machine-learned interatomic potential. The MD simulations predict the solid-liquid coexistence on the Hugoniot in the $\sim$$111-124$ GPa range. Experimentally, we observe the first evidence of liquid at 86 GPa. We also observe pronounced microstructural changes with pressure with strong grain refinement associated with the emergence of liquid, within the solid-liquid coexistence ($\sim$$110-126$ GPa). Above 126 GPa, we observe the persistence of residual levels of highly textured crystalline Ti to $\sim$$180$ GPa, well above the expected melt completion pressure. We discuss the accuracy that current laser-shock experimental platforms have at determining the melt onset and completion pressures.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 开发了在MOOSE中实现的三场耦合热-力学断裂模型，包含弹性、损伤相场和热传导三个模块；提出了简单拉伸和简单剪切下裂纹长度尺度的解析确定方法。

Conclusion: 该三场耦合模型能够有效预测α-SiC在宽温度范围内的损伤行为，验证了其在弯曲强度和断裂韧性方面的准确性，并展示了良好的计算可扩展性。

Abstract: A three-way coupled thermo-mechanical fracture model is presented to predict the damage of brittle ceramics, in particular α-SiC, over a wide range of temperatures (20-1400 C). Predicting damage over such a range of temperatures is crucial for thermal protection systems for many systems such as spacecraft. The model, which has been implemented in MOOSE, is divided into three modules: elasticity, damage phase field, and heat conduction. Analytical approaches for determining crack length scales are presented for both simple tension and simple shear. Validation tests are conducted for both flexural strength and fracture toughness over the specified range of temperatures. Flexural strength simulation results fall within the uncertainty region of the experimental data, and mode I fracture toughness simulation results are also in agreement with the experimental data. Mode II and mixed mode fracture toughness simulations results are presented with the modified G-criterion. Finally, the parallel computing capabilities of the model is considered in various scalability tests.

The high-temperature structural evolution of the as-synthesized borides was investigated using in situ synchrotron X-ray diffraction (SXRD). The oxidation behavior was further characterized using a combination of SXRD and thermogravimetric analysis (TGA), allowing direct comparison with other potential accident-tolerant fuels such as UB$_2$, U$_3$Si$_2$, UC, and UN. The UB$_4$-UBC composite shows higher uranium loading than monolithic UB$_4$ and demonstrates promising oxidation behavior at elevated temperature, pointing to its potential as an improved uranium boride-based fuel form.

### [115] [Energy conservation and pressure relaxation in an extended two-temperature model for copper with an electron temperature-dependent interaction potential](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04907)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 研究结果通过大规模双温模型分子动力学模拟验证了所提方法的有效性，并与其他现有方法进行了比较分析，评估了各种扩展对模拟结果的影响。

### [118] [Domain-Direct Band Gaps: Classification and Material Realization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05103)
*Yalan Wei,Hairui Ding,Shifang Li,Yuke Song,Chi Ren,Xiao Dong,Chaoyu He*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该论文提出了"畴直接带隙（domain-direct band gap）"新概念，其中导带最小值（CBM）和价带最大值（VBM）在布里渊区形成扩展的二维流形，而非传统点状极值。通过扭曲金刚石材料实现极端2D-2D畴直接带隙，展现出强烈的方向各向异性载流子动力学和增强的光学吸收特性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统直接带隙半导体分类依赖于动量空间中的点状极值。本研究旨在引入畴直接带隙新概念，其中导带最小值（CBM）和价带最大值（VBM）形成布里渊区中的扩展流形，为各向异性光电子应用开辟新机会。

Method: 通过第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）在扭曲金刚石材料中实现畴直接带隙概念。分析显示CBM和VBM在kx-ky平面形成几乎平坦的二维流形，能量变化极小（仅几meV），产生3.264 eV的直接带隙。

Result: 计算结果表明强烈的面外kz方向色散导致各向异性载流子动力学：面内费米速度（Fermi velocities）被强烈抑制（某些方向低至约10¹-10³ m/s），而面外速度大得多（约10⁶ m/s）。近乎平坦的CBM和VBM流形增强了联合态密度（joint density of states），在带隙起始处产生显著的光学吸收峰。

Conclusion: 畴直接带隙与强方向各向异性相结合，为各向异性光电子应用开辟了新机遇。研究结果确立了畴直接带隙作为半导体新类别，并证明了其在真实材料中的可行性。

Abstract: The conventional classification of direct band-gap semiconductors relies on point-like extrema in momentum space. Here, we introduce the concept of domain-direct band gaps, where the conduction-band minimum (CBM) and valence-band maximum (VBM) form extended manifolds in the Brillouin zone. We demonstrate this concept through the material realization of an extreme two-dimensional-two-dimensional (2D-2D) domain-direct band gap in twisted diamond. First-principles calculations show that both the CBM and VBM exhibit nearly flat 2D manifolds in the kx-ky plane with minimal energy variation (a few meV), yielding a direct band gap of 3.264 eV. In contrast, strong dispersion along the out-of-plane kz direction induces anisotropic carrier dynamics, with strongly suppressed in-plane Fermi velocities (down to about 10$^1$-10$^3$ m/s in certain directions) and much larger out-of-plane velocities (about 10$^6$ m/s). The nearly flat CBM and VBM manifolds enhance the joint density of states, leading to a pronounced optical absorption peak at the band gap onset. This new type of domain-direct gap, coupled with strong directional anisotropy, opens up opportunities for anisotropic optoelectronic applications. Our results establish domain-direct band gaps as a new class of semiconductors, demonstrating their feasibility in real materials.

Abstract: Altermagnetism has recently emerged as a new class of spin compensated magnetic materials that exhibit momentum dependent spin splitting despite having zero net magnetization. The origin of these electronic signatures lies in symmetry operations that connect opposite spin sublattices while allowing spin splitting in momentum space. While most candidate materials identified so far belong to inorganic crystals with fixed lattice symmetries, the realization of altermagnetism ultimately requires platforms in which magnetic symmetry can be deliberately engineered. In this Perspective, we discuss how metal-organic frameworks (MOFs) provide a unique chemical platform to address this challenge. We first place altermagnetism in the broader context of magnetic and electronically active metal-organic networks, highlighting how reticular chemistry enables precise control over lattice geometry, dimensionality and electronic structure. We then discuss how these features position framework materials as promising candidates for realizing altermagnetism and highlight the key challenges that must be addressed to translate theoretical proposals into experimentally accessible systems. Finally, we critically assess current experimental challenges and outline emerging directions for realizing and controlling altermagnetism in coordination framework materials, which emerge as a versatile and powerful platform for exploring new paradigms in spintronics.

Abstract: Magnonic crystals (MCs) are emerging spintronic metamaterials capable of manipulating transmission properties of magnons, the quanta of spin waves. In this study, we demonstrated an inverse-design framework for two-dimensional MCs to explore unconventional lattice structures with large magnonic band gaps. We employed genetic algorithms to enable global exploration of structures with a complete band gap as the objective property, and used frequency-domain micromagnetic simulations for computationally efficient band gap evaluation. Our established inverse-design method successfully discovered several previously unreported designs of MCs, whose performance was validated using time-domain micromagnetic simulations. Furthermore, we observed that the design landscape becomes increasingly non-convex at high-order bands, suggesting the existence of multiple design solutions. ### [121] [A Geometry-Adaptive Deep Variational Framework for Phase Discovery in the Landau-Brazovskii Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05161)
*Yuchen Xie,Jianyuan Yin,Lei Zhang*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种几何自适应深度变分框架（GeoDVF），通过联合优化神经网络参数化的序参数和计算域的几何参数，解决了传统数值求解器对计算域尺寸敏感的问题，能够自发地从随机初始化中发现复杂三维有序相。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在Landau-Brazovskii（LB）模型等图案形成系统中，有序结构的发现常受限于数值求解器对计算域尺寸的敏感性。不兼容的域会引入人工应力，使系统陷入高能亚稳态构型。

Method: 提出了几何自适应深度变分框架（Geometry-Adaptive Deep Variational Framework, GeoDVF），该框架联合优化由神经网络参数化的无限维序参数和计算域的有限维几何参数。通过将域尺寸作为变分公式中的可训练变量，自然消除了训练过程中的人工应力。引入了预热惩罚机制（warmup penalty mechanism）来逃离无序相的吸引盆，并设计了引导初始化协议（guided initialization protocol）来解决与窄吸引盆相关的拓扑复杂相。

Result: 广泛的数值实验表明，GeoDVF提供了一个鲁棒且几何一致的变分解算器，能够在没有先验知识的情况下识别稳定态和亚稳态。该框架能够从随机初始化中自发成核复杂三维有序相。

Conclusion: GeoDVF通过联合优化序参数和域几何参数，有效解决了计算域尺寸敏感性导致的数值求解器限制问题，为图案形成系统中的相发现提供了鲁棒的变分解算框架。

Abstract: The discovery of ordered structures in pattern-forming systems, such as the Landau-Brazovskii (LB) model, is often limited by the sensitivity of numerical solvers to the prescribed computational domain size. Incompatible domains induce artificial stress, frequently trapping the system in high-energy metastable configurations. To resolve this issue, we propose a Geometry-Adaptive Deep Variational Framework (GeoDVF) that jointly optimizes the infinite-dimensional order parameter, which is parameterized by a neural network, and the finite-dimensional geometric parameters of the computational domain. By explicitly treating the domain size as trainable variables within the variational formulation, GeoDVF naturally eliminates artificial stress during training. To escape the attraction basin of the disordered phase under small initializations, we introduce a warmup penalty mechanism, which effectively destabilizes the disordered phase, enabling the spontaneous nucleation of complex three-dimensional ordered phases from random initializations. Furthermore, we design a guided initialization protocol to resolve topologically intricate phases associated with narrow basins of attraction. Extensive numerical experiments show that GeoDVF provides a robust and geometry-consistent variational solver capable of identifying both stable and metastable states without prior knowledge.

We show that selenium passivation of the substrate is key to enable a quasi van der Waals epitaxy effectively suppressing strong interfacial bonding and promoting the growth of quasi free standing bilayer films. Analysis of the measured dispersions yields hole effective masses of 0.46 +- 0.04 me and 0.75 +- 0.06 me for the upper and lower valence bands at K point, respectively. These results establish a robust route for synthesizing quasi free standing 3R-WSe2 and provide a platform for exploring the electronic, optical, and ferroelectric functionalities that emerge from inversion symmetry breaking in layered TMDs. Motivation: 当前基础机器学习原子间势（foundation MLIPs）在描述半导体Sb2Se3的缺陷物理方面存在不足，特别是当配位环境和电子计数偏离原始参考结构时，对缺陷的描述仍具挑战性。

Method: 研究引入全局缺陷电荷嵌入（global defect charge embeddings）来区分不同电荷态的成键特性，并采用多保真度方法（multi-fidelity approach）结合低成本（半局域交换关联泛函）和高精度（非局域杂化泛函）参考数据，以准确描述缺陷能量景观的细微差别。

Result: 所开发的缺陷能力力场（defect-capable force fields）能够找到稳定的结构构型，并预测与直接量子力学计算定量一致的电荷跃迁能级（charge-transition levels），同时计算成本显著降低。

Conclusion: 通过引入全局缺陷电荷嵌入和多保真度策略，研究成功克服了当前机器学习原子间势在缺陷描述方面的局限性，为半导体缺陷物理的准确模拟提供了高效的计算工具。

Abstract: Machine learning interatomic potentials (MLIPs) can now reproduce the energy, forces and stresses of bulk materials with high accuracy compared to first-principles calculations. The description of imperfections, where coordination environments and electron counts deviate from those found in pristine reference structures, remains a challenge. We find that the current generation of foundation MLIPs do not describe the defect physics of the semiconductor Sb2Se3. We introduce global defect charge embeddings that distinguish the bonding characteristics of different charge states. We further employ a multi-fidelity approach that combines low-cost (semi-local exchange-correlation functional) reference data with high-quality (non-local hybrid functional) energies and forces that describe well the subtleties of the defect energy landscape. The resulting defect-capable force fields can find stable structural configurations and predict charge-transition levels in quantitative agreement with direct quantum mechanical calculations, at a fraction of the computational cost.

</details>


### [124] [Precise control of crystallography and magnetism in focused-ion-beam transformed iron-nickel thin films](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05242)
*Jakub Holobrádek,Libor Vojáček,Ondřej Wojewoda,Michael Schmid,Michal Urbánek*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 聚焦离子束辐照成功实现了局部区域从顺磁面心立方（fcc）到铁磁体心立方（bcc）的结构转变，产生了八个具有不同磁性的晶体学畴；磁各向异性（magnetic anisotropy）可归因于fcc→bcc相变后的残余晶格应变（residual lattice strain）。

Conclusion: 该研究深化了对Fe₇₈Ni₂₂材料系统及其相变行为的理解，为制备具有精确可控磁化图案（magnetization landscapes）的高质量磁性纳米结构提供了有效途径。

Abstract: Focused ion beam irradiation of metastable Fe$_{78}$Ni$_{22}$ thin films grown on Cu(100) substrates results in the localized transformation of the originally paramagnetic, face-centered-cubic continuous film into ferromagnetic patterns with body-centered-cubic structure. The direction of the magnetic easy axis can be controlled by the focused ion beam scanning strategy, resulting in eight differently oriented crystallographic domains with different magnetic properties. We study the local crystallographic orientations of the transformed areas by electron backscatter diffraction and correlate these results with local magnetometry measurements. The observed magnetic anisotropy can be explained as a result of residual lattice strain after the fcc$\to$bcc transformation. These results extend the understanding of this material system and its transformation and allow for the patterning of high-quality magnetic nanostructures with precisely controlled magnetization landscapes.

### [125] [Lattice dynamics of the charge density wave compounds TaTe$_4$ and NbTe$_4$ and their evolution across solid solutions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05257)
*D. Silvera-Vega,G. Cardenas-Chirivi,J. A. Galvis,A. C. García-Castro,P. Giraldo-Gallo*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究结合密度泛函理论计算与拉曼光谱测量，研究了准一维过渡金属四硫族化合物TaTe₄、NbTe₄及其固溶体Ta₁₋ₓNbₓTe₄的振动性质，揭示了与电荷密度波相关的晶格畸变机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解晶格动力学对于阐明电荷密度波（charge density waves, CDWs）的微观起源至关重要，特别是在电子-声子耦合（electron-phonon coupling）起主导作用的材料中。拉曼光谱（Raman spectroscopy）结合第一性原理计算为识别相关振动模式及其在受控扰动下的演化提供了直接手段。

Method: 本研究结合密度泛函理论（density functional theory）计算与拉曼光谱测量，系统研究了准一维（quasi-one-dimensional）过渡金属四硫族化合物TaTe₄、NbTe₄及其固溶体Ta₁₋ₓNbₓTe₄（x = 0.0-1.0）的振动性质。

Result: 对于化学计量化合物，第一性原理计算预测了与CDW相相关的三聚化（trimerization）一致的声子不稳定性，为驱动相变的晶格畸变提供了理论证据。计算得到的拉曼活性模式与室温实验光谱吻合良好，实现了对观测峰的系统归属。在固溶体中，最高频率的E_g模式表现出独特行为：其频率接近母体化合物，但强度随化学计量比重新分布。

Conclusion: 最高频率E_g模式的演化突显了该振动模式的短程特性，并表明其与这些材料中CDW相关的晶格畸变具有相关性。该研究为理解准一维过渡金属四硫族化合物中电荷密度波的微观机制提供了重要见解。

Abstract: Understanding lattice dynamics is central to elucidating the microscopic origin of charge density waves (CDWs), particularly in materials where electron-phonon coupling can play a dominant role. Raman spectroscopy, combined with first-principles calculations, offers a direct means to identify the vibrational modes involved and to monitor their evolution under controlled perturbations. In this work, we combine density functional theory calculations and Raman spectroscopy measurements to investigate the vibrational properties of the quasi-one-dimensional transition metal tetrachalcogenides TaTe$_4$ and NbTe$_4$, as well as their solid solutions Ta$_{1-x}$Nb$_{x}$Te$_4$ ($x$ = 0.0 - 1.0). For the stoichiometric compounds, first-principles calculations predict a phonon instability consistent with the trimerization associated with the CDW phase, providing theoretical evidence for the lattice distortion driving the transition. The calculated Raman-active modes show good agreement with room-temperature experimental spectra, enabling a systematic assignment of the observed peaks. Across the solid solution, most Raman modes evolve smoothly with composition. In contrast, the highest-frequency E$_{g}$ mode, dominated by transition-metal motion, exhibits a distinct behavior: its frequency remains close to that of the parent compounds while its intensity redistributes with stoichiometry. This evolution highlights the short-range character of this vibrational mode and suggests its relevance to the CDW-related lattice distortion in these materials.

### [126] [A Shift-Invariant Deep Learning Framework for Automated Analysis of XPS Spectra](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05350)
*Issa Saddiq,Yuxin Fan,Robert G. Palgrave,Mark A. Isaacs,David Morgan,Keith T. Butler*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用空间变换网络（Spatial Transformer Network）这一能够隐式学习谱图对齐的神经网络架构。模型使用官能团作为代理来分类输入谱图中的化学环境，并在包含10万个谱图的合成数据集上进行训练和测试，该数据集通过线性组合104种聚合物的真实实验数据生成，并应用了随机均匀位移和展宽来模拟实验变异性。

Result: 空间变换网络能够有效校正随机静电位移（高达3.0 eV），并在识别官能团方面实现了相对较高的准确率（约82%），尽管其架构比先前工作简单得多。这表明神经网络能够有效学习谱图特征与化学成分之间的内在关系。

Conclusion: 该研究推动了更可靠的自动化XPS分析的发展，为研究人员提供了潜在的辅助工具，并可作为未来自主系统（如自驱动实验室）的核心组件。神经网络通过内在考虑可变位移，能够有效学习谱图特征与化学成分之间的关系。

Abstract: X-ray Photoelectron Spectroscopy (XPS) is a crucial technique for material surface analysis, yet interpreting its spectra is often challenging for both human analysts and automated methods due to the prevalence of variable spectral shifts and overlapping peaks. This project introduces a machine learning solution using a Spatial Transformer Network (STN), a type of neural network that implicitly learns to align spectra. An STN model was designed to classify the chemical environments present in an input spectrum, using functional groups as a proxy. The model was trained and tested on a large synthetic dataset of 100,000 spectra, created by linearly combining real experimental data from a library of 104 polymers. \cite{RN22} To simulate experimental variability, random uniform shifts and broadening were applied to the data. The STN was found to effectively correct for random electrostatic shifts (up to 3.0 eV) and achieved relatively high accuracy ($\sim$ 82\%) in identifying functional groups, despite utilizing a much simpler architecture than previous work. These findings demonstrate that neural networks can effectively learn the underlying relationships between spectral features and chemical composition when they are able to intrinsically account for variable shifts. This work advances the development of more reliable automated XPS analysis, offering potential as an assistive tool for researchers and as a core component in future autonomous systems like self-driving laboratories.

### [128] [Correcting hybrid density functionals to model Y6 and other non-fullerene acceptors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05379)
*Tom Ward,Isabel Creed,Tim Rein,Jarvist Moore Frost*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究通过调整Y6有机电子受体的范围分离杂化泛函（range-separated hybrid functional），解释了其固态二聚体中的溶剂化显色效应（solvatochromic effects），并基于Penn模型解释了短优化范围分离参数的原因。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究调整了Y6的范围分离杂化泛函（range-separated hybrid functional），表征了固态代表性二聚体（dimers），并基于Penn模型（Penn model）解释频率依赖介电常数。

Result: Y6二聚体显示出广泛的溶剂化显色效应（solvatochromic effects），部分原因是振子强度借用（oscillator strength borrowing）。研究发现标准范围分离杂化泛函对这些材料的准确性低于全局杂化泛函（global hybrids），而减少范围分离长度（range-separation length）可提高标准泛函的准确性，无需复杂的调参过程。

Conclusion: 研究为Y6有机电子受体提供了优化的电子结构方法，解释了其光物理性质，并指出标准范围分离杂化泛函的局限性，同时提供了无需复杂调参即可提高准确性的替代方案。

Abstract: Recently developed fused-ring organic electron-acceptors such as Y6 have strong oscillator strength, good charge-carrier transport and low bandgaps. They therefore have enormous current technical application to optoelectronic devices, such as solar cells. Due to the large number of atoms involved in representative aggregates of these materials, we need an efficient electronic structure method to model them. Standard density functional theory poorly describe charge-transfer states, and were developed for vacuum calculations of individual molecules.
  In this work we tune a range-separated hybrid functional for Y6. We characterise representative dimers of the solid-state and show that Y6 dimers show the extensive solvatochromic effects are due, in part, to oscillator strength borrowing. We provide an explanation for the short optimally-tuned range-separation parameter, based in the Penn model for the frequency dependent dielectric of a semiconductor. We caution that standard range-separated hybrids are less accurate than global hybrids for these, and similar, materials. We show how reducing the range-separation length improves the accuracy of standard functionals, without an involved tuning process.

### [129] [Equilibrium Thermochemistry and Crystallographic Morphology of Manganese Sulfide Nanocrystals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05420)
*Junchi Chen,Tamilarasan Subramani,Deep Mekan,Danielle Gendler,Ray Yang,Manish Kumar,Megan Householder,Alexis Rosado Ortiz,Emil A. Hernandez-Pagan,Kristina Lilova,Robert B. Wexler*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用密度泛函理论（DFT），使用r²SCAN meta-GGA泛函并加入Hubbard U修正（r²SCAN+U，U=2.7 eV），结合Gibbs-Wulff定理预测平衡形貌；通过实验合成验证理论预测。

Abstract: Manganese sulfide (MnS) is a p-type magnetic semiconductor whose physicochemical properties are sensitive to nanocrystal (NC) morphology, yet the thermodynamic driving forces governing morphology across MnS polymorphs remain poorly understood. Here, we use density functional theory (DFT) to predict the equilibrium morphologies of rock salt (RS), zinc blende (ZB), and wurtzite (WZ) MnS NCs as a function of the relative chemical potential of sulfur, $Δμ_{S}$. Benchmarking against Heyd$\unicode{x2013}$Scuseria$\unicode{x2013}$Ernzerhof (HSE06) hybrid functional calculations reveals that the r$^2$SCAN meta-generalized gradient approximation reproduces experimental lattice constants and thermochemical reaction energies but underestimates S-terminated polar surface energies by up to a factor of five; applying a Hubbard $U$ correction (r$^2$SCAN+$U$, $U = 2.7$ eV) to the Mn 3d states brings the results into close agreement with HSE06. Using the validated r$^2$SCAN+$U$ framework with the Gibbs$\unicode{x2013}$Wulff theorem, we predict that RS-MnS NCs favor nanocubes across nearly the entire stability window, ZB-MnS NCs transform from rhombic dodecahedra (Mn-rich) to polyhedra with 16 triangular faces (S-rich), and WZ-MnS NCs adopt rod-like morphologies with $Δμ_{S}$-sensitive base truncation. Synthesized RS-MnS NCs confirm the predicted cubic morphology, and high-temperature oxidative solution calorimetry yields an apparent surface energy of 1.15 $\pm$ 0.38 J$\cdot$m$^{-2}$, higher than the theoretical equilibrium value (0.42$\unicode{x2013}$0.43 J$\cdot$m$^{-2}$) due to high-index facet exposure, surface area uncertainty, and non-ideal surface configurations in real samples. This work establishes a framework for predicting the equilibrium morphologies of metal chalcogenide NCs.

### [130] [High-Pressure Inelastic Neutron Spectroscopy: A true test of Machine-Learned Interatomic Potential energy landscapes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05442)
*Jeff Armstrong,Adam Jackson,Alin Elena*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究首次通过高压中子非弹性散射实验验证了机器学习原子间势（MLIPs）在不同热力学状态间的可迁移性，建立了高压中子光谱作为MLIP预测能力的严格基准。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 机器学习原子间势（machine-learned interatomic potentials, MLIPs）虽承诺提供接近密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）的精度且计算成本更低，但其在训练范围之外的预测有效性仍缺乏实验验证。

Method: 采用压力依赖的宽带非弹性中子散射（inelastic neutron spectroscopy, INS）作为MLIP可迁移性的直接实验探针。使用新开发的高压超合金夹紧池，在10K温度下测量了结晶2,5-二碘噻吩在常压和1.5GPa条件下的INS光谱。基于MACE框架的MLIP在目标DFT数据上进行微调，并通过300K下的严格分子动力学验证保持热力学稳定性。

Result: 该MLIP模型在0-1200 cm⁻¹范围内成功复现了两个压力下的实验光谱。模型捕捉到由空间位阻硬化引起的系统性压力诱导蓝移，并再现了453 cm⁻¹处由压力修饰的分子间相互作用驱动的异常红移，直接验证了其多体特征。

Conclusion: 这是首次使用中子光谱实验证明MLIP在不同热力学状态间的可迁移性，确立了高压INS作为预测性机器学习势能的严格基准方法。

Abstract: Machine-learned interatomic potentials (MLIPs) promise to provide near density-functional theory accuracy at a fraction of the computational cost, offering a transformative route toward genuinely predictive chemistry. Yet their predictive validity beyond the training regime remains largely untested experimentally.
  Here we use pressure-dependent broadband inelastic neutron spectroscopy (INS) as a direct experimental probe of MLIP transferability. Employing a newly developed high-pressure superalloy clamp cell, we measure INS spectra of crystalline 2,5-diiodothiophene at 10~K under ambient conditions and at 1.5~GPa. A MACE-based MLIP, fine-tuned on targeted DFT data, reproduces the experimental spectra across 0--1200~cm$^{-1}$ at both pressures and remains thermodynamically stable under rigorous molecular dynamics validation at 300~K. The model captures systematic pressure-induced blue shifts arising from steric stiffening and reproduces an anomalous red shift at 453~cm$^{-1}$ driven by pressure-modified intermolecular interactions, providing direct validation of its many-body character.
  This constitutes the first experimental demonstration of MLIP transferability across distinct thermodynamic states using neutron spectroscopy, and establishes high-pressure INS as a stringent benchmark for predictive machine-learned potentials.

</details>

### [131] [A Geometric Perspective on the Difficulties of Learning GNN-based SAT Solvers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.21513)
*Geri Skenderi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文提出基于图里奇曲率（graph Ricci curvature）的几何解释，说明图神经网络（GNNs）在解决布尔可满足性问题（SATs）时，性能随问题难度增加而下降的原因在于负曲率导致的过压缩（oversquashing）现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 图神经网络（Graph Neural Networks, GNNs）作为布尔可满足性问题（Boolean Satisfiability Problems, SATs）的可学习求解器受到关注，但其性能在更困难、约束更强的实例上急剧下降，引发了对架构局限性的疑问。

Method: 论文基于图里奇曲率（graph Ricci Curvature, RC）构建几何解释，证明从随机k-SAT公式导出的二分图具有固有的负曲率，且曲率随实例难度降低。通过不同SAT基准测试进行实证验证。

Result: 负图里奇曲率表明存在局部连接瓶颈，导致GNN求解器受到过压缩（oversquashing）现象影响，即长程依赖无法压缩到固定长度表示中。曲率既是问题复杂度的强指标，也可用于预测泛化误差。

Conclusion: 研究结果与现有求解器设计相关联，并指出了未来工作的有前景方向，为理解GNN在SAT问题上的性能限制提供了几何理论基础。

Abstract: Graph Neural Networks (GNNs) have gathered increasing interest as learnable solvers of Boolean Satisfiability Problems (SATs), operating on graph representations of logical formulas. However, their performance degrades sharply on harder and more constrained instances, raising questions about architectural limitations. In this paper, we work towards a geometric explanation built upon graph Ricci Curvature (RC). We prove that bipartite graphs derived from random k-SAT formulas are inherently negatively curved, and that this curvature decreases with instance difficulty. Given that negative graph RC indicates local connectivity bottlenecks, we argue that GNN solvers are affected by oversquashing, a phenomenon where long-range dependencies become impossible to compress into fixed-length representations. We validate our claims empirically across different SAT benchmarks and confirm that curvature is both a strong indicator of problem complexity and can be used to predict generalization error. Finally, we connect our findings to the design of existing solvers and outline promising directions for future work.

</details>

### [132] [Modular memristor model with synaptic-like plasticity and volatile memory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04934)
*Daniel Habart,Stephen H. Foulger,Kristyna Kovacova,Ambika Pandey,Yadu R. Panthi,Jiri Pfleger,Jarmila Vilcakova,Lubomir Kostal*

Main category: physics.app-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种模块化忆阻器模型，通过整合物理学和计算神经科学原理，在保持计算效率的同时描述了挥发性弛豫和突触可塑性等复杂动力学。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有忆阻器紧凑模型（compact models）通常无法描述挥发性弛豫（volatile relaxation）和突触可塑性（synaptic plasticity）等复杂动力学，这限制了大规模神经形态系统（neuromorphic systems）的仿真能力。

Method: 模型采用模块化设计，包含：标准忆阻器件动力学公式、状态变量到累积电导的映射函数、基于线性粘弹性理论（linear viscoelasticity）的挥发性模块、采用线性-非线性技术的饱和模块，以及受生物尖峰时序依赖可塑性（STDP）启发的突触可塑性公式。此外，提出了基于拉普拉斯变换（Laplace transform）的技术来推导状态变量到累积电导的精确映射。

Result: 模型在展现增强（potentiation）、突触样可塑性（synaptic-like plasticity）和挥发性衰减（volatile decay）的聚合物忆阻器（polymeric memristors）实验数据上进行了定量验证，证明了其有效性。

Conclusion: 该工作提出了一种新的忆阻器建模范式，既适用于大规模仿真，又具有丰富的解释能力，为下一代神经形态硬件（neuromorphic hardware）设计提供了原理性工具。

Abstract: Compact models of memristors are essential for simulating large-scale neuromorphic systems, yet they often do not include description of complex dynamics like volatile relaxation and synaptic plasticity. We introduce a modular, computationally efficient memristor model that bridges this gap by integrating principles from physics and computational neuroscience. The model defines a framework consisting of a standard formulation of memristive device dynamics, a functional rule mapping state variables to cumulative conductance, a volatility module inspired by the theory of linear viscoelasticity and a saturation module implementing a linear-nonlinear technique. Additionally, we develop a formulation of synaptic-like plasticity inspired by a biological spike-timing-dependent plasticity (STDP) rule, which is compatible with the general framework for memristive devices. Finally, we propose a Laplace transform-based technique to derive the precise form of the mapping from state variables to cumulative conductance, replacing ad hoc voltage-current relationships with principled construction.
  We quantitatively validate the complete model against a rich set of experimental data from polymeric memristors exhibiting potentiation, synaptic-like plasticity and volatile decay. Our work presents a new paradigm for memristor modeling that is both practical for large-scale simulation and rich in explanatory power, providing a principled tool for the design of next-generation neuromorphic hardware.

</details>
