### [133] [Perspective on "Active Brownian Particles Moving in a Random Lorentz Gas"](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04602)
*C. Reichhardt,C. J. O. Reichhardt*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究比较了活性物质（active matter）粒子与布朗粒子在随机障碍阵列中的运动行为，发现两者在障碍渗流密度附近均表现出亚扩散（subdiffusive）行为，但活性粒子更快达到稳态；高活性下，活性粒子因自陷效应（self-trapping）增强而具有更低的有效扩散。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自驱动活性物质（self-propelled active matter）与纯布朗运动系统可能表现出显著不同的行为。研究旨在比较活性粒子与布朗粒子在随机障碍阵列中的运动特性差异，探索活性对粒子在无序介质中扩散行为的影响。

Method: 研究采用比较分析方法，将活性物质粒子与布朗粒子置于随机障碍阵列（random obstacle array）中，考察它们在障碍渗流密度（percolation density）附近的运动行为。通过分析粒子的扩散特性，特别是亚扩散行为和稳态到达时间。

Result: 在障碍渗流密度附近，布朗粒子和活性粒子均表现出相同的亚扩散行为，但活性粒子达到稳态的速度更快。高活性条件下，活性粒子由于活动性增强产生的自陷效应（self-trapping effect），其有效扩散（effective diffusion）反而低于布朗粒子。

Conclusion: 该结果为研究无序介质中的活性物质开辟了新方向，包括多孔介质中的细菌（bacteria in porous media）、淬火无序（quenched disorder）上的活性胶体（active colloids），以及拥挤环境（crowded environments）中的活性粒子等系统。

Abstract: Self-propelled active matter can exhibit vastly different behavior than systems with purely Brownian motion. In Eur. Phys. J. E 40, 23 (2017), Zeitz, Wolf, and Stark compared an active matter particle with a Brownian particle moving in a random obstacle array. They showed that near the obstacle percolation density, both Brownian and active particles exhibit the same subdiffusive behavior, but the active particle reaches a steady state more rapidly. They also found that for high activity, the active particle has a lower effective diffusion than the Brownian particle due to the increased self-trapping effect generated by the activity. This result opens new directions for the study of active matter in disordered media, including bacteria in porous media, active colloids on quenched disorder,and active particles in crowded environments.

</details>


### [134] [Electrochromic chiral ferroelectric nematic liquid crystals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04641)
*Md Sakhawat Hossain Himel,James T. Gleeson,Robert J. Twieg,Samuel Sprunt,Antal Jakli*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究展示了铁电向列相液晶（ferroelectric nematic liquid crystals）中反射颜色可通过沿螺旋轴施加电场实现可逆调谐，峰值波长可增加达200纳米，并提出解释该现象的螺旋轴变形理论模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统手性向列相液晶（chiral nematic liquid crystals）的反射波长虽可通过温度良好调谐，但电场调谐能力有限且不可逆。本研究旨在探索铁电向列相液晶中沿螺旋轴电场调谐反射颜色的可能性，以扩展对这类材料的理解并开发潜在应用。

Method: 使用裸导电ITO基板组装夹层电池（sandwich cells），施加沿螺旋轴方向高达0.4 kV/mm的电场。对比实验采用经电绝缘聚合物层处理的ITO基板以观察反射偏移的抑制效应。

Result: 在裸ITO基板电池中，反射峰值波长可增加达200纳米，且调谐过程可逆。当ITO基板经绝缘聚合物处理后，反射偏移被抑制。研究提出了螺旋轴在电场下发生螺旋变形的理论模型，该模型能解释所有观察结果并估算难以通过其他方法确定的展曲弹性常数（splay elastic constant）。

Conclusion: 铁电向列相液晶的反射颜色可通过沿螺旋轴施加电场实现可逆调谐，这一发现扩展了对该类材料的理解，并为其在可调谐反射器和节能智能窗户（energy-efficient smart windows）等领域的应用提供了新思路。

Abstract: Chiral nematic liquid crystals are one-dimensional photonic band-gap materials whose reflection wavelength can be well tuned by temperature, but only limited and irreversible tuning can be achieved by electric fields. In contrast, oblique heliconical chiral nematic materials blueshift with <1kV/mm fields applied along the helix axis, whereas chiral ferroelectric nematic liquid crystals can be redshifted by <0.1kV/mm fields applied perpendicular to the helix axis. Here we demonstrate that in ferroelectric nematic liquid crystals, the reflection color can be reversibly tuned also by electric fields applied along the helix axis. In sandwich cells assembled with bare conducting indium tin oxide (ITO) substrates, the reflectivity peak wavelength increases by up to 200 nm under fields up to 0.4 kV/mm. When the ITO substrates are treated with an electrically insulating polymer layer, the reflectivity shift is suppressed. We propose a theoretical model assuming helical deformation of the helix axis under electric field. This model accounts for all observations and also yields an estimate of the splay elastic constant which is challenging to determine by other methods. Our findings expand understanding of ferroelectric nematic liquid crystals and suggest potential applications in both tunable reflectors and energy-efficient smart windows.

</details>


### [135] [Anomalous Ion Confinement Penalties and Giant Ion-Screening Effects in One-Dimensional Nanopores](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04651)
*Kevin Leung*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究使用经典力场和碳纳米管模型，量化了纳米限域对单个离子水合自由能的影响，发现限域效应显著且与经典Born方程不符，同时揭示了电解质在纳米孔中对限域效应的浓度依赖性屏蔽作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 纳米限域会降低单个离子的有利水合自由能，这与离子在充水纳米孔中的排斥和化学活性改变相关。然而，影响限域效应大小的多种因素尚未得到系统评估。

Method: 采用简单的经典力场（classical force fields）和填充水的非极化碳纳米管（non-polarizable carbon nanotubes）作为最小化模型，评估单个离子的本征限域水合自由能惩罚（Delta Delta G(hyd)）。研究在半径R=7.5埃的纳米管中进行模拟计算。

Result: 在7.5埃半径的纳米管中，预测的Delta Delta G(hyd)高达7.8 kcal/mol，且Cl-的限域效应远大于较小的Na+离子，这与经典的离子溶剂化Born方程（Born Equation）相矛盾。添加1.0 M背景电解质使Na+/Cl-对的Delta Delta G(hyd)降低幅度，比非限域介质中的Debye-Huckel估计值（Debye-Huckel estimate）高出近一个数量级。

Conclusion: 研究识别出浓度依赖性的离子屏蔽限域效应（concentration-dependent ion-screening of confinement effects），这是电解质在圆柱形纳米孔中的一个重要且未被充分认识的结果，对理解纳米孔中的离子行为具有重要意义。

Abstract: Nanoconfinement reduces the favorable hydration free energies of single ions, which is correlated with ion rejection and modified chemical reactivity in water-filled nanopores. Many factors contribute to the magnitude of the observed confinement effect. Here we use simple classical force fields and non-polarizable carbon nanotubes filled with water as minimal, "hydrogen atom"-like models to evaluate the single-ion intrinsic confinement hydration free energy penalty (Delta Delta G(hyd)). In tubes of radius R=7.5 Angstrom, we predict Delta Delta G(hyd)'s that are up to 7.8 kcal/mol, are much larger for Cl- than the smaller Na+ ion, and contradict the canonical Born Equation for ion solvation. Adding a 1.0~M background electrolyte reduces Delta Delta G(hyd) for the Na+/Cl- pair by an amount exceeding the Debye-Huckel estimate in unconfined media by almost an order of magnitude. We identify concentration-dependent ion-screening of confinement effects as a major, unheralded consequence of electrolytes in cylindrical nanopores.

</details>


### [136] [Rotational 3D printing of active-passive filaments and lattices with programmable shape morphing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04694)
*Mustafa K. Abdelrahman,Jackson K. Wilt,Yeonsu Jung,Rodrigo Telles,Gurminder K. Paink,Natalie M. Larson,Joanna Aizenberg,L. Mahadevan,Jennifer A. Lewis*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于多材料弹性体细丝（multimaterial elastomeric filaments）的可编程形状变形策略，通过旋转式多材料3D打印（RM-3DP）技术直接编码细丝的本征曲率和扭转，实现了复杂三维形状的可控变形。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 天然细丝（如蛋白质、植物卷须、章鱼触手等）能够通过主动与被动区域的复杂图案化实现任意三维形状变形，但这种行为在合成材料中难以复制。本研究旨在开发一种可编程的形状变形策略，用于自适应、机器人或可展开结构等应用。

Method: 采用旋转式多材料3D打印（RM-3DP）技术，通过控制材料分布和螺旋液晶介晶（liquid crystal mesogen）排列，直接编码细丝的本征曲率-扭转场（natural curvature-twist field）。利用向列相-各向同性相转变温度（nematic-to-isotropic transition temperature）下的热响应特性，实现主动区域沿局部指向矢场（local director field）的收缩。

Result: 该方法实现了沿细丝中心线每个横截面上弯曲和扭转的独立控制，包括沿两个正交轴的主本征曲率和局部扭转。通过打印由正弦细丝组成的结构晶格（architected lattices），实现了可逆收缩、膨胀或面外变形。离散弹性杆模拟（discrete elastic rod simulations）能够准确预测观察到的形状变形行为。

Conclusion: 通过整合主动-被动弹性体、增材制造和计算建模，本研究创造了具有复杂可编程响应的形状变形材料，为自适应、机器人或可展开结构等应用提供了新的可能性。

Abstract: Natural filaments, such as proteins, plant tendrils, octopus tentacles, and elephant trunks, can transform into arbitrary three-dimensional shapes that carry out vital functions. Their shape-morphing behavior arises from intricate patterning of active and passive regions, which are difficult to replicate in synthetic matter. Here, we introduce a filament-centric strategy for programmable shape morphing in which intrinsic curvature and twist are directly encoded within multimaterial elastomeric filaments during fabrication. By harnessing rotational multimaterial 3D printing (RM-3DP), we directly prescribe the filament's natural curvature--twist field $\mathbf{k}(s)$ through controlled material distribution and helical liquid crystal mesogen alignment. When heated above their nematic-to-isotropic transition temperature ($T_\mathrm{NI}$), the helically aligned LCE regions contract along their local director field, while passive regions remain essentially unchanged. This approach enables independent control of bending and torsion at every cross-section along the filament centerline: the principal natural curvatures of the filament along two orthogonal axes as well as the local twist. Next, we printed architected lattices composed of unit cells formed by sinusoidal filaments that either reversibly contract, expand, or exhibit out-of-plane deformations. Discrete elastic rod simulations of Janus filaments with different natural curvatures and twist, which are interconnected within the printed lattices, allow accurate prediction of their observed shape-morphing behavior. By integrating active-passive elastomers, additive manufacturing, and computational modeling, we have created shape-morphing matter with complex programmable responses for applications that rely on adaptive, robotic, or deployable architectures.

</details>


### [137] [Extended dynamical density functional theory for nonisothermal binary systems including momentum density](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04973)
*Michael te Vrugt,Hartmut Löwen,Helmut R. Brand,Raphael Wittkowski*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种新的扩展动态密度泛函理论（EDDFT），用于描述两相流或二元混合物（如胶体悬浮液）的非等温微观动力学，该理论包含了质量密度、浓度、动量密度和能量密度等变量，并考虑了扩散和对流过程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为了在微观层面描述两相流或二元混合物（如胶体颗粒和溶剂组成的胶体悬浮液）的非等温动力学，需要发展一种新的理论框架。现有方法通常无法同时考虑扩散和对流过程，特别是在包含动量密度的情况下。

Method: 采用Mori-Zwanzig-Forster投影算符技术，推导出新的扩展动态密度泛函理论（EDDFT），该理论以总质量密度、局部浓度、总动量密度和能量密度为变量。通过将动量密度纳入EDDFT，同时考虑了扩散和对流动力学。

Result: 为硬球体系推导了精确的熵和自由能泛函。讨论了新EDDFT的流体动力学极限及其与玻璃化转变的模耦合理论（mode-coupling theory）的关系。证明EDDFT能够获得正确的声速值。

Conclusion: 新发展的扩展动态密度泛函理论（EDDFT）为描述复杂流体系统的非等温动力学提供了更全面的理论框架，成功整合了扩散和对流过程，并在硬球体系中实现了精确描述，为理解玻璃化转变等复杂现象提供了新途径。

Abstract: In order to describe the nonisothermal dynamics of two-phase flows or binary mixtures such as colloidal suspensions consisting of colloidal particles and solvent on a microscopic level, we derive a new extended dynamical density functional theory (EDDFT) that includes the total mass density, the local concentration of one species, the total momentum density, and the energy density as variables using the Mori-Zwanzig-Forster projection operator technique. Through the incorporation of the momentum density into EDDFT, not only the diffusive but also the convective dynamics is taken into account. We derive an exact entropy and free-energy functional for the case of hard spheres. The hydrodynamic limit of our new EDDFT and its relation to the mode-coupling theory of the glass transition are discussed. It is shown that EDDFT allows to obtain the correct value for the speed of sound.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 设计了具有卤素取代基的原始分子结构，在电子给体基团位置引入卤素取代。首次在铁电向列相材料的分子核心中应用氯原子，并研究了其介晶行为和铁电特性。

Abstract: Ferroelectric nematic phase (NF) represents an attractive and foremost field of liquid crystals, combining fluidity with ferroelectricity. NF materials exhibit large polarization values and remarkable non-linear optical properties. We have designed an original molecular structure with halogen substituents in the position of an electron donating group. In a prolonged molecular core, such a modification led to the presence of the ferroelectric nematic phase (NF) below the nematic one. Besides, an application of Cl atom in the molecular core of one of the presented materials has been utilized for the first time for ferroelectric nematogens. We have examined mesogenic behaviour and ferroelectric characteristics of the NF phase. In the NF phase for the cell with antiparallel rubbing, we have detected a textural transformation, which evidences strong polar character of anchoring at the surfaces. The presented results provide valuable insight into the design of ferroelectric nematic liquid crystalline compounds.

### [139] [Theories of the Glass Transition Based on Local Excitations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05209)
*Massimo Pica Ciamarra,Jeppe C. Dyre,Edan Lerner,Matthieu Wyart*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该综述批判性地评估了玻璃化转变中动力学减慢的理论解释，提出基于局域激发（localized excitations）及其弹性相互作用的框架，而非传统热力学长度尺度增长理论，为简单玻璃形成液体的脆性（fragility）提供了定量解释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 过冷液体在接近玻璃转变时动力学显著减慢是凝聚态物理的核心未解问题。传统理论将这种减慢归因于热力学或结构长度尺度的增长，但难以解释最近的数值结果，这促使本文批判性地考察基于局域激发及其弹性相互作用的替代理论。

Method: 综述首先回顾关键现象学，重点关注液体脆性、动力学异质性（dynamical heterogeneities）、热力学-动力学关联以及动力学规则和交换算法（swap algorithms）效应。随后比较基于均匀和局域异质弹性的弹性描述与包含非线性响应的激发理论。

Result: 研究结果将全局和局域弹性模量、德拜-沃勒因子（Debye-Waller factor）和激发密度联系起来，建立了可在实验中检验的定量理论。激发谱的热演化提供了无参数的活化能解释，而其弹性相互作用通过热雪崩过程（thermal avalanche processes）定量再现了动力学异质性。

Conclusion: 综合这些结果形成了一个理论框架：在简单玻璃形成液体中，激发谱的演化（而非热力学长度尺度的增长）控制着脆性。然而，动力学转变的平均场概念对于描述激发和建立弛豫的实空间图像仍然至关重要。

Abstract: The dramatic slowdown of dynamics in supercooled liquids approaching the glass transition remains one of the central unresolved problems in condensed matter physics. We review approaches that attribute this slowdown to growing thermodynamic or structural length scales and discuss their difficulties in accounting for recent numerical results. These limitations motivate the present review, which critically examines alternative theories in which the glassy slowdown is instead controlled by localized excitations and their elastic interactions. After reviewing key phenomenology with a focus on the fragility of liquids, dynamical heterogeneities, thermodynamics-dynamics correlation, and the effect of kinetic rules and swap algorithms, we compare elastic descriptions based on homogeneous and local heterogeneous elasticity to excitation-based theories incorporating nonlinear responses. Results are compiled to relate global and local elastic moduli, the Debye-Waller factor, and the density of excitations, leading to a quantitative theory testable in experiments. The thermal evolution of the excitation spectrum provides a parameter-free account of the activation energy, while their elastic interactions quantitatively reproduce dynamical heterogeneities via thermal avalanche processes. Synthesized together, these results lead to a framework where the evolution of the excitation spectrum, rather than the growth of a thermodynamic length scale, governs fragility in simple glass-forming liquids -- yet mean-field concepts of dynamical transitions remain central to describing excitations and building a real-space picture of relaxation.

</details>


### [140] [Dynamic Wettability Modulation of Textured, Soft and LIS Interfaces Using Electrowetting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05297)
*Deepak J.,Suman Chakraborty,Shubham S. Ganar,Arindam Das*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究发现，在特定微纹理和润滑剂注入表面上施加直流电压时，液滴会发生快速切向喷射而非预期的铺展增强，这一反直觉现象源于接触线处不平衡的电毛细力与最小钉扎效应的共同作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统电润湿理论预期，在纹理化和润滑剂注入表面上施加电压会通过减小表观接触角来增强液滴铺展。然而，本研究旨在探索这种常规直觉之外的异常现象，特别是在特定微结构表面上观察到的液滴快速切向喷射行为。

Method: 采用高速成像技术和精确控制的电润湿实验装置，系统研究液滴动力学对表面拓扑结构、润湿状态（Cassie态与Wenzel态）以及润滑剂存在的依赖性。实验使用间距为5-10微米的密集纹理厚PDMS基底，在低滞后非润湿Cassie状态下进行观测。

Result: 在密集纹理的厚PDMS基底（间距5-10微米）的低滞后非润湿Cassie态表面，以及所有润滑剂注入的纹理表面上，液滴经历突然的横向运动并最终脱离。这一反直觉现象归因于接触线处不平衡的电毛细力（electrocapillary forces）与最小钉扎效应的结合，使电场应力不对称性直接转化为净横向运动。相比之下，Wenzel态液滴或具有较大纹理间距的表面表现出传统铺展行为并伴有强粘附。

Conclusion: 通过揭示静电力、接触线钉扎和界面迁移率之间的基本相互作用，该研究为电润湿系统中基于密集微柱和润滑剂诱导界面的可控液滴传输与喷射提供了新范式（new paradigm）。

Abstract: Electrowetting on textured and lubricant infused surfaces is conventionally expected to promote enhanced droplet spreading by reducing apparent contact angles. Contrary to this intuition, we report rapid tangential droplet ejection at applied DC voltages on specific microtextured, lubricant infused surfaces. Using high speed imaging and a precisely controlled electrowetting setup, we reveal the dependence of droplet dynamics on surface topology, wetting state, and the presence of a lubricant. On densely textured thick PDMS substrates of post spacing 5 to 10 um in a low hysteresis non-wetting Cassie state, and on all lubricant infused textured surfaces, droplets experience sudden lateral motion and eventual detachment. We attribute this counterintuitive phenomenon to unbalanced electrocapillary forces at the contact line combined with minimal pinning, which allows asymmetries in electric stresses to translate directly into net lateral motion. In contrast, Wenzel state droplets or surfaces with larger texture spacing exhibit conventional spreading with strong adhesion. By capturing the fundamental interplay among electrostatic driving forces, contact line pinning, and interfacial mobility, our results provide a new paradigm for controlled droplet transport and ejection in electrowetting systems mediated by dense micro posts and lubricant induced interfaces.

</details>

### [141] [Rethinking quantum smooth entropies: Tight one-shot analysis of quantum privacy amplification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04493)
*Bartosz Regula,Marco Tomamichel*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种改进的单次随机性提取（privacy amplification）表征方法，通过定义新的光滑条件熵类，建立了更紧致的剩余哈希引理（leftover hash lemma），显著改进了量子隐私放大（quantum privacy amplification）的边界，并在渐近独立同分布（i.i.d.）极限下恢复了最优误差指数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有量子侧信息（quantum side information）下的随机性提取（privacy amplification）的单次表征存在改进空间，需要建立更紧致的边界并统一推导已知的最紧渐近约束。

Method: 主要工具是通过测量提升经典光滑散度（smooth divergences）定义的新光滑条件熵类。对于关键的测量光滑Rényi散度（measured smooth Rényi divergence）阶数2，该方法允许在状态和非正定Hermitian算子上进行光滑化（smoothing）。

Result: 建立了更紧致的剩余哈希引理（leftover hash lemma），显著改进了量子隐私放大（quantum privacy amplification）的所有已知光滑最小熵（smooth min-entropy）边界，并恢复了最尖锐的经典可实现结果。通过匹配的单次逆边界（converse bound）证明了结果的近似最优性。

Conclusion: 该方法在迹距离（trace distance）下建立了隐私放大的最优二阶渐近展开，提供了比先前工作更紧致的单次可实现结果，并证明了其对所有哈希函数的最优性。同时将方法扩展到解耦（decoupling），获得了相应的改进单次边界。

Abstract: We introduce an improved one-shot characterisation of randomness extraction against quantum side information (privacy amplification), strengthening known one-shot bounds and providing a unified derivation of the tightest known asymptotic constraints. Our main tool is a new class of smooth conditional entropies defined by lifting classical smooth divergences through measurements. For the key case of measured smooth Rényi divergence of order 2, we show that this can be alternatively understood as allowing for smoothing over not only states, but also non-positive Hermitian operators. Building on this, we establish a tightened leftover hash lemma, significantly improving over all known smooth min-entropy bounds on quantum privacy amplification and recovering the sharpest classical achievability results. We extend these methods to decoupling, the coherent analogue of randomness extraction, obtaining a corresponding improved one-shot bound. Relaxing our smooth entropy bounds leads to one-shot achievability results in terms of measured Rényi divergences, which in the asymptotic i.i.d. limit recover the state-of-the-art error exponent of [Dupuis, arXiv:2105.05342]. We show an approximate optimality of our results by giving a matching one-shot converse bound up to additive logarithmic terms. This yields an optimal second-order asymptotic expansion of privacy amplification under trace distance, establishing a significantly tighter one-shot achievability result than previously shown in [Shen et al., arXiv:2202.11590] and proving its optimality for all hash functions.

</details>


### [142] [Markovian quantum master equations are exponentially accurate in the weak coupling regime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04504)
*Johannes Agerskov,Frederik Nathan*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文证明弱耦合开放量子系统可用马尔可夫量子主方程（MQME）描述，其非马尔可夫修正项随系统-环境耦合强度的倒数呈指数衰减，并通过可迭代的广义玻恩-马尔可夫近似获得任意阶精度的方程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究开放量子系统与一个或多个高斯环境耦合时的演化特性，旨在证明在弱耦合条件下，非马尔可夫演化分量可被指数抑制，从而建立更精确的马尔可夫描述框架。

Method: 采用广义玻恩-马尔可夫近似（generalized Born-Markov approximation），该方法可在系统-环境耦合强度上迭代至任意阶；通过严格误差界分析，并对精确可解模型进行数值基准测试。

Result: 推导出马尔可夫量子主方程（MQME）的显式表达式，并给出其残余修正项的严格误差界；数值基准测试验证了理论结果，误差界随迭代阶数渐近收敛至零。

Conclusion: 开放量子系统的非马尔可夫演化分量虽可能不可避免，但在弱耦合条件下可被指数抑制；广义玻恩-马尔可夫近似为弱耦合开放量子系统提供了精确的马尔可夫描述框架。

Abstract: We consider the evolution of open quantum systems coupled to one or more Gaussian environments. We demonstrate that such systems can be described by a Markovian quantum master equation (MQME) up to a correction that decreases exponentially with the inverse system-bath coupling strength. We provide an explicit expression for this MQME, along with rigorous bounds on its residual correction, and numerically benchmark it for an exactly solvable model. The MQME is obtained via a generalized Born-Markov approximation that can be iterated to arbitrary orders in the system-bath coupling; our error bound converges asymptotically to zero with the iteration order. Our results thus demonstrate that the non-Markovian component in the evolution of an open quantum system, while possibly inevitable, can be exponentially suppressed at weak coupling.

</details>


### [143] [Tight inapproximability of max-LINSAT and implications for decoded quantum interferometry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04540)
*Maximilian J. Kramer,Carsten Schubert,Jens Eisert*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明了max-LINSAT问题（在有限域$\mathbb{F}_q$上最大化满足线性约束的数量）的紧不可近似性界：除非$\mathsf{P} \neq \mathsf{NP}$，否则任何多项式时间算法都无法超越随机分配比率$r/q$的常数倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究max-LINSAT问题的计算复杂性边界，特别是确定多项式时间算法可达到的最佳近似比率。该问题涉及在有限域$\mathbb{F}_q$上最大化满足线性约束的数量，其中每个约束接受$r$个值。

Method: 通过从Håstad定理的直接归约（direct reduction）证明不可近似性界。该方法将max-LINSAT问题的近似难度与已知的复杂性结果联系起来。

Result: 证明了在$\mathsf{P} \neq \mathsf{NP}$假设下，任何多项式时间算法都无法超越随机分配比率$r/q$的常数倍。这一阈值与解码量子干涉测量（decoded quantum interferometry, DQI）的半圆定律（semicircle law）在$\ell/m \to 0$极限下的近似比率一致。

Conclusion: 研究结果划定了最坏情况硬度（worst-case hardness）与潜在量子优势（quantum advantage）之间的边界，表明任何超越$r/q$比率的算法必须利用实例特定的代数结构（algebraic structure）。

Abstract: We establish tight inapproximability bounds for max-LINSAT, the problem of maximizing the number of satisfied linear constraints over the finite field $\mathbb{F}_q$, where each constraint accepts $r$ values. Specifically, we prove by a direct reduction from Håstad's theorem that no polynomial-time algorithm can exceed the random-assignment ratio $r/q$ by any constant, assuming $\mathsf{P} \neq \mathsf{NP}$. This threshold coincides with the $\ell/m \to 0$ limit of the semicircle law governing decoded quantum interferometry (DQI), where $\ell$ is the decoding radius of the underlying code: as the decodable structure vanishes, DQI's approximation ratio degrades to exactly the worst-case bound established by our result. Together, these observations delineate the boundary between worst-case hardness and potential quantum advantage, showing that any algorithm surpassing $r/q$ must exploit algebraic structure specific to the instance.

</details>


### [144] [Quantum Weight Reduction with Layer Codes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04883)
*Andrew C. Yuan,Nouédyn Baspin,Dominic J. Williamson*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种简单通用的量子权重缩减（quantum weight reduction）方法，通过将任意CSS码中的每个量子比特和校验子替换为表面码（surface code）补丁，构建几何非局域的层码（Layer Code），实现校验权重6和总量子比特度6的优化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子权重缩减方法通过稀疏化量子码来简化实现，但目前仅有少数方法被探索。现有方法在降低校验权重和量子比特度方面仍有改进空间，需要更简单通用的解决方案。

Method: 该方法将任意Calderbank-Shor-Steane（CSS）码中的每个量子比特和校验子替换为表面码补丁，然后将这些补丁连接形成几何非局域的层码。这是经典权重缩减方法的量子类比，其中每个比特和校验子被重复码替换。

Result: 该方法实现了校验权重6和总量子比特度6，低于现有方法，代价是可能增加量子比特开销。由于方法的简单性，结果码的权重和度界限可直接从层码构造推导，易于通过检查验证。

Conclusion: 该权重缩减方法特别适合由表面码补丁通过长程互连网络连接的模块化架构实现。其简单性和通用性为量子码实现提供了新的优化途径。

Abstract: Quantum weight reduction procedures ease the implementation of quantum codes by sparsifying them, resulting in low-weight checks and low-degree qubits. However, to date, only few quantum weight reduction methods have been explored. In this work we introduce a simple and general procedure for quantum weight reduction that achieves check weight 6 and total qubit degree 6, lower than existing procedures at the cost of a potentially larger qubit overhead. Our quantum weight reduction procedure replaces each qubit and check in an arbitrary Calderbank-Shor-Steane code with an ample patch of surface code, these patches are then joined together to form a geometrically nonlocal Layer Code. This is a quantum analog of the simple classical weight reduction procedure where each bit and check is replaced by a repetition code. Due to the simplicity of our weight reduction procedure, bounds on the weight and degree of the resulting code follow directly from the Layer Code construction and hence are easily verified by inspection. Our procedure is well suited for implementation in modular architectures that consist of surface code patches networked via long-range interconnects.

</details>


### [145] [Parsimonious Quantum Low-Density Parity-Check Code Surgery](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05082)
*Andrew C. Yuan,Alexander Cowtan,Zhiyang He,Ting-Chun Lin,Dominic J. Williamson*

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种在任意量子低密度奇偶校验（qLDPC）稳定子码中测量任意权重为W的逻辑泡利算符的辅助系统构造方法，将量子比特规模从O(W²)降低到O(W log W)，显著减少了量子码手术方案的开销。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 本文引入了一种构造辅助系统的方法，能够在任意qLDPC稳定子码（qLDPC stabilizer code）中测量权重为W的任意逻辑泡利算符（logical Pauli operator），所需量子比特规模为O(W log W)。

Result: 新构造方法将辅助系统的量子比特规模从先前方法的O(W²)降低到O(W log W)，这一改进立即减少了各种量子码手术方案的渐近开销（asymptotic overhead）。

Conclusion: 该方法显著提升了量子码手术框架的效率，为并行手术（parallel surgery）、通用适配器（universal adapters）和快速手术（fast surgery）等容错逻辑计算方案提供了更高效的实现基础。

Abstract: Quantum code surgery offers a flexible, low-overhead framework for executing logical measurements within quantum error-correcting codes. It encompasses several fault-tolerant logical computation schemes, including parallel surgery, universal adapters and fast surgery, and serves as the key primitive in extractor architectures. The efficiency of these schemes crucially depends on constructing low-overhead ancilla systems for measuring arbitrary logical operators in general quantum Low-Density Parity-Check (qLDPC) codes. In this work, we introduce a method to construct an ancilla system of qubit size $O(W \log W)$ to measure an arbitrary logical Pauli operator of weight $W$ in any qLDPC stabilizer code. This new construction immediately reduces the asymptotic overhead across various quantum code surgery schemes.

*Christof Wetterich*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 成功将具有概率性初始条件的经典场论重新表述为量子场论框架，详细讨论了具有相互作用的经典相对论性克莱因-戈登方程（Klein-Gordon equation）作为具体实例。

Conclusion: 通过引入统计可观测量，概率性经典场论可以自然地转化为量子场论，非对易算符的出现源于经典概率规则，为经典与量子理论之间的连接提供了新视角。

Abstract: For classical field theories with probabilistic initial conditions the classical field observables are an idealization. Their arbitrarily precise values poorly reflect the characteristic uncertainty in the presence of substantial fluctuations. Non-commuting operators are associated to observables. The quantum rules follow from the laws for classical probabilities. We construct the functional integral for the quantum field theory, and discuss in detail the classical relativistic Klein-Gordon equation with interactions.

Abstract: Developing measures of quantum ergodicity and chaos stands as a foundational task in the study of quantum many-body systems. In particular, we show how ergodicity and chaos improve the robustness of Hamiltonian learning to small errors and furthermore demonstrate that this robustness can be used as a metric for such phenomena. We analytically and numerically show that our metrics not only distinguish between integrable and ergodic regimes in various spin chains but also quantify chaos and ergodicity, allowing us to locate regions of parameter space displaying maximal ergodicity and maximal sensitivity to local perturbations. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 表征纠缠分布（entanglement distribution）的极限速率对于基础研究和量子技术实际部署至关重要。研究旨在探索受偏振模色散（polarization mode dispersion）影响的现实光纤中量子通信的极限性能。

Method: 引入描述光纤中偏振纠缠分布的擦除-泡利信道模型（erasure-Pauli channel model）。在该模型下推导最优本地操作和双向经典通信（optimal local operations and two-way classical communication）辅助下的纠缠分布速率及相关量子资源界限。

Result: 确定了受偏振模色散影响的现实光纤中无中继器（repeaterless）可达到的最优性能，为长距离偏振基量子通信提供了严格基准。模型和容量界限在包含探测器暗计数（detector dark counts）的情况下仍保持鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了光纤偏振纠缠分布的理论框架，推导的容量界限为评估现实光纤量子通信性能提供了可靠基准，且结果对探测器噪声具有鲁棒性。

Abstract: Characterizing the ultimate rates of entanglement distribution is essential for both foundational research and the practical deployment of quantum technologies. To investigate these limits, we introduce an erasure-Pauli channel model describing the distribution of polarization entanglement in optical fiber. For this channel, we derive bounds on the rates of entanglement distribution and related quantum resources under optimal local operations and two-way classical communication (two-way assisted capacities). This framework allows us to determine the optimal repeaterless performance achievable over realistic optical fibers affected by polarization mode dispersion, thereby providing a rigorous benchmark for long-distance polarization-based quantum communication. Finally, we show that both our model and capacity bounds remain robust under the inclusion of detector dark counts.

### [149] [Long-range waveguide-quantum electrodynamics with left-handed transmission lines](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04581)

Method: 提出了一种由单个发射体耦合到左手传输线构成的波导量子电动力学系统。该系统模拟了具有对数衰减跳跃幅度的合成光子晶格，其衰减距离完全由线色散的紫外和红外截止比决定。采用"运行指数（running exponents）"方法，建立了波导色散与强长程跳跃机制下获得的束缚态和光前轮廓之间的统一图像。

Result: 左手传输线系统展现出内在的长程特性，表现为原子-光子束缚态和散射态的性质：束缚态呈现代数局域化（algebraic localization），而散射态则表现出加速光子传播（accelerated photon propagation）。该系统能够在强长程跳跃机制下实现可调范围相互作用。

Conclusion: 这些结果表明传输线能够实现具有可调范围相互作用的多量子比特信息处理。该系统为波导量子电动力学提供了具有本征长程相互作用的替代方案，克服了传统基于局域耦合系统的局限性。

Abstract: While engineering long-range light-matter interactions is the principal aim in waveguide-QED, ironically most of the building blocks rest on local short-range couplings, such as nearest-neighbor-coupled cavity arrays employed in canonical models. Here, we propose a waveguide-QED system with native long-range interactions, comprising a single emitter coupled to a left-handed transmission line (LHTL). Interestingly, the LHTL emulates a synthetic photonic lattice with a slow logarithmic decay of hopping amplitudes over a distance set entirely by the ratio of UV and IR cutoffs of line dispersion. Its intrinsic long-range nature manifests both in the properties of atom-photon bound and scattering states, which exhibit algebraic localization and accelerated photon propagation respectively. Using a method of 'running exponents', we develop a unified picture connecting waveguide dispersion to bound state and light front profiles obtained in the strong long-range hopping regime. These results motivate how transmission lines can enable multi-qubit information processing with tunable-range interactions.

Abstract: Quantum sensors based on individual spins provide unprecedented access to local magnetic fields in condensed matter, chemistry, and biology, with solid-state defect spins emerging as the leading platform. However, their molecular-sensing capabilities are limited by confinement to a host lattice, which prevents placement in close proximity to a target molecule. Molecular spins offer an alternative, enabling chemical tunability and flexible positioning relative to the target system. Here we present a nanoscale sensing platform that combines molecular electron spins, ultrasensitive mechanical readout, and Hamiltonian engineering. Using a modified XYXY dipolar decoupling sequence, we suppress electron-electron dipolar interactions across a broad distribution of control fields, extending coherence times to $\sim 400~μ$s in an attoliter-scale droplet containing $\sim$100 trityl-OX063 radicals. Leveraging this sequence, we demonstrate frequency-selective detection of nanotesla-scale AC fields and perform sensing and spectroscopy of small, local nuclear-spin ensembles. Collectively, these results establish SQUINT (Spin-based QUantum Integrated Nanomechanical Transduction) as a framework for quantum sensing that affords molecular-level control over sensor properties and enables direct integration into complex molecular targets.

### [151] [Extending spin-lattice relaxation theory to three-phonon processes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05393)
*Nilanjana Chanda,Alessandro Lunghi*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究将自旋弛豫的第一性原理理论扩展到三声子过程，应用于自旋-1/2氮化铬复合物的vdW晶体，验证了弱自旋-声子耦合假设的有效性，并揭示了强耦合条件下三声子效应在室温下可能变得显著。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自旋-晶格弛豫理论发展近一个世纪，但其中关于相互作用性质的基本假设（如弱耦合近似）从未得到充分验证。该近似使自旋动力学能够进行微扰描述，并导致自旋弛豫的规范描述仅包含单声子和双声子过程。

Result: 结果表明，对于该分子体系，三声子过程对自旋弛豫的贡献仅在实验无法达到的温度下才变得显著，这为弱自旋-声子耦合假设在自旋弛豫理论中的有效性提供了前所未有的证据。同时，数值计算显示，自旋-声子耦合强度相对较小的增加会导致三声子与双声子过程效率在室温下发生交叉。

Abstract: Spin-lattice relaxation theory has been developed over almost a century, but some cardinal assumptions on the nature of the interactions involved have never been fully verified. This includes the weak coupling approximation, which makes it possible to describe spin dynamics perturbatively and leads to the canonical description of spin relaxation in terms of one- and two-phonon processes. Here, we extend the first-principles theory of spin relaxation to three-phonon processes and apply it to the vdW crystal of a spin-1/2 Chromium nitride complex. Results show that three-phonon contributions to spin relaxation only become relevant at temperatures inaccessible to experiments for this molecule, thus providing unprecedented evidence for the validity of the weak spin-phonon coupling assumption in spin relaxation theory. At the same time, we numerically show that a relatively small increase in spin-phonon coupling would lead to a crossover between three- and two-phonon processes' efficiency at room temperature, illustrating the possibility for three-phonon effects in molecular materials as well as paving the way to a systematic exploration of strong coupling in spin systems.

### [152] [Optimal Decoding with the Worm](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05428)
*Zac Tobias,Nikolas P. Breuckmann,Benedikt Placke*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种用于"可匹配"qLDPC码的新解码器，该解码器使用马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛算法（蠕虫算法）来近似计算给定校验子下逻辑错误类的概率，从而实现近似最优解码。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 针对可匹配量子低密度奇偶校验码（matchable qLDPC codes）需要高效且近似最优的解码方法。现有解码器在处理测量错误和相关噪声时存在局限性，需要开发能够提供软信息（soft information）并适用于更广泛噪声模型的解码方案。

Method: 提出基于蠕虫算法（worm algorithm）的马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛解码器，通过计算逻辑错误类的概率分布实现近似最优解码。该方法适用于表面码（surface code）、蜂窝弗洛凯码（honeycomb Floquet code）和双曲表面码（hyperbolic surface codes）等多种编码结构。

Result: 解码器效率取决于马尔可夫链的混合时间，通过缺陷敏感性（defect susceptibility）概念提供严格的混合时间保证。数值模拟显示，在表面码和双曲表面码中，该解码器能有效处理测量错误。在相关解码方案中，针对表面码的退极化噪声，相关蠕虫解码（correlated worm decoding）的阈值显著高于最小权重完美匹配和相关匹配方法。

Conclusion: 蠕虫解码器为可匹配qLDPC码提供了一种近似最优且计算高效的解码方案，特别适用于包含测量错误的噪声环境。虽然直接应用受限于独立比特翻转、相位翻转和测量错误的噪声模型，但其提供的软信息使其在更广泛的相关解码方案中具有实用价值。

Abstract: We propose a new decoder for ``matchable'' qLDPC codes that uses a Markov-Chain Monte-Carlo algorithm -- called the \emph{worm algorithm} -- to approximately compute the probabilities of logical error classes given a syndrome. The algorithm hence performs (approximate) \emph{optimal} decoding, and we expect it to be computationally efficient in certain settings.
  The algorithm is applicable to decoding random errors for the surface code, the honeycomb Floquet code, and hyperbolic surface codes with constant rate, in all cases with and without measurement errors.
  The efficiency of the decoder hinges on the mixing time of the underlying Markov chain. We give a rigorous mixing time guarantee in terms of a quantity that we call the \emph{defect susceptibility}. We connect this quantity to the notion of disorder operators in statistical mechanics and use this to argue (non-rigorously) that the algorithm is efficient for \emph{typical} errors in the entire decodable phase.
  We also demonstrate the effectiveness of the worm decoder numerically by applying it to the surface code with measurement errors as well as a family of hyperbolic surface codes.
  For most codes, the matchability condition restricts direct application of our decoder to noise models with independent bit-flip, phase-flip, and measurement errors. However, our decoder returns \emph{soft information} which makes it useful also in heuristic ``correlated decoding'' schemes which work beyond this simple setting. We demonstrate this by simulating decoding of the surface code under depolarizing noise, and we find that the threshold for ``correlated worm decoding'' is substantially higher than for both minimum-weight perfect matching and for correlated matching.

</details>

Method: 方法基于量子极端学习和量子储备计算框架，其中固定量子动力学生成非线性特征映射。引入动态注意力机制，通过哈密顿量中的输入依赖相互作用项实现，调制量子演化并将特征嵌入偏向任务相关相关性。

Conclusion: 极端量子认知机为审慎决策提供了一种量子学习架构，具有对噪声和矛盾数据的容忍性。该框架在生物学、法医学和网络安全等领域具有直接相关性，展示了量子计算在复杂认知任务中的应用前景。

Abstract: We introduce Extreme Quantum Cognition Machines, a class of quantum learning architectures for deliberative decision making that is tolerant to noisy and contradictory training data. Inspired by the quantum cognition paradigm, Extreme Quantum Cognition Machines are closely related to quantum extreme learning and quantum reservoir computing, where fixed quantum dynamics generates a nonlinear feature map and learning is confined to a linear readout. A dynamical attention mechanism, implemented through an input-dependent interaction term in the Hamiltonian, modulates the quantum evolution and biases the resulting feature embedding toward task-relevant correlations. The approach is validated on linguistic classification tasks, which serve as paradigmatic examples of deliberative inference. Hardware-compatible quantum implementations of the proposed framework are discussed, together with potential applications in symbolic inference, sequence analysis, anomaly detection, and automatic diagnosis, with direct relevance to domains such as biology, forensics, and cybersecurity.

### [154] [Measurement Induced Asymmetric Entanglement in Deconfined Quantum Critical Ground State](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05436)
*K. G. S. H. Gunawardana*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究数值模拟了弱测量（weak measurement）对解禁闭量子临界点（deconfined quantum critical point, DQCP）的影响，发现测量后态（post-measurement states）的纠缠熵（entanglement entropy）在相变边界两侧呈现不对称重构，可能导致弱一级相变（weak first order phase transition）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在探究弱测量对解禁闭量子临界点（DQCP）的影响。DQCP是一种超越朗道-金兹堡范式（Landau-Ginzburg paradigm）的量子相变，而弱测量作为一种非幺正扰动，可能对其临界行为产生独特影响。

Method: 研究采用数值方法，考虑一个具有长程交换相互作用（long range exchange interactions, K）的一维自旋1/2系统，该系统在热力学极限下展现出与DQCP类似的相变。通过将辅助系统（ancilla system）与临界系统幺正耦合，然后对辅助自旋进行投影测量（projective measurement）来实现弱测量。使用均匀矩阵乘积态（uniform matrix product state）表示热力学极限下的量子多体态，计算测量后态的纠缠熵、关联长度和序参数。

Result: 数值结果显示，在弱测量下，测量后态的纠缠在相变边界两侧呈现不对称重构（asymmetric restructuring of entanglement）。特别是，当所有辅助自旋初始化为相同向下态时，描述均匀测量结果的轨迹（trajectory (↓↓)）在增加弱测量强度时表现出反常纠缠行为：当K<K_c时，二分纠缠熵（bipartite entanglement entropy）显著增加；而当K>K_c时，其微弱减小。数值证据表明，这种纠缠不对称性可能导致热力学极限下的弱一级相变边界。

Conclusion: 弱测量对DQCP的临界行为产生了显著的非对称影响，可能导致相变性质的改变。研究还讨论了与弱测量强度和测量后态概率相关的实验观测重要方面，为在量子模拟平台（quantum simulation platforms）上观测测量诱导效应提供了理论指导。

Abstract: In this work, we numerically study the effect of weak measurement on deconfined quantum critical point(DQCP). Particularly, we consider the ground state of an one-dimensional spin $1/2$ system with long range exchange interactions($K$), which shows analogues phase transition to DQCP in the thermodynamic limit. This system is in the ferromagnetic phase below the critical exchange interaction $K_c$ and in the valance bond solid phase above $K_c$. The weak measurement is carried out by coupling a secondary ancilla system to the critical system via unitary interactions and later measuring the ancilla spins projectively. We numerically calculate entanglement entropy,correlation length, and order parameters of leading post-measurement states using uniform matrix product state representation of the quantum many-body state in the thermodynamic limit. We report asymmetric restructuring of entanglement of the post measurement states across the phase boundary under weak measurements. Especially, the trajectory $\left(\downarrow \downarrow\right)$ describing a uniform measurement outcome given the all ancilla spins initiated in the same $\left(\downarrow \right)$ state, shows anomalous entanglement when increasing the strength of weak measurement. The bipartite entanglement entropy strongly increases when $K<K_c$ whereas it weakly decreases when $K>K_c$. We argue with numerical evidences that observed asymmetry in entanglement would lead to a weak first order phase boundary in the thermodynamic limit. We also discuss important aspects in experimental observation of measurement induced effects linked to the strength of weak measurement and probability of post-measurement states.

</details>


### [155] [Universal quantum computation with group surface codes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05502)
*Naren Manjunath,Vieri Mattei,Apoorv Tiwari,Tyler D. Ellison*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出群表面码（group surface codes）作为Z₂表面码的自然推广，展示了如何利用其实现非克利福德门（non-Clifford gates）从而实现通用量子计算，并建立了与拓扑规范理论（topological gauge theories）的明确对应关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于扩展拓扑量子计算的能力，特别是超越Bravyi-König定理对拓扑泡利稳定子模型（topological Pauli stabilizer models）计算能力的限制，实现在无需编织任意子（anyons）的情况下进行通用量子计算。

Method: 方法包括引入群表面码作为Z₂表面码的自然推广，建立与有限群量子双模型（quantum double models）的等价性，并通过一组基本逻辑操作（包括横向逻辑门、信息传输、制备和读出）来构建各种逻辑门。

Result: 结果表明群表面码可用于在Z₂表面码中实现非克利福德门，从而实现通用计算；对于适当选择的群，任意可逆经典门可在群表面码中横向实现；研究还建立了与拓扑规范理论的明确对应关系。

Conclusion: 该工作扩展了无需编织任意子的拓扑序中实现通用量子计算的研究，展示了某些群表面码如何绕过Bravyi-König定理的限制，并为滑动群表面码和制备魔法态（magic states）的近期构造提供了统一视角。

Abstract: We introduce group surface codes, which are a natural generalization of the $\mathbb{Z}_2$ surface code, and equivalent to quantum double models of finite groups with specific boundary conditions. We show that group surface codes can be leveraged to perform non-Clifford gates in $\mathbb{Z}_2$ surface codes, thus enabling universal computation with well-established means of performing logical Clifford gates. Moreover, for suitably chosen groups, we demonstrate that arbitrary reversible classical gates can be implemented transversally in the group surface code. We present the logical operations in terms of a set of elementary logical operations, which include transversal logical gates, a means of transferring encoded information into and out of group surface codes, and preparation and readout. By composing these elementary operations, we implement a wide variety of logical gates and provide a unified perspective on recent constructions in the literature for sliding group surface codes and preparing magic states. We furthermore use tensor networks inspired by ZX-calculus to construct spacetime implementations of the elementary operations. This spacetime perspective also allows us to establish explicit correspondences with topological gauge theories. Our work extends recent efforts in performing universal quantum computation in topological orders without the braiding of anyons, and shows how certain group surface codes allow us to bypass the restrictions set by the Bravyi-K{ö}nig theorem, which limits the computational power of topological Pauli stabilizer models.

</details>

### [156] [Plasmonic Spin Meron Lattices with Height-Sensitive Topology Evolution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.03042)
*Anand Hegde,Komal Gupta,Chen-Bin Huang*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文展示了在圆偏振光照射下，金属方形耦合结构上方的等离子体自旋半子（meron）晶格可通过高度控制实现拓扑切换。近界面处形成Néel型半子晶格，较大高度时转变为Bloch型晶格，中间高度区域呈现丰富的拓扑演化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探索等离子体自旋半子晶格的高度可控拓扑切换机制。通过调控观测高度，实现不同拓扑构型之间的转换，为可调谐拓扑光子结构提供新思路。

Method: 采用解析方法结合数值模拟：在等离子体区域使用表面等离子体激元（surface plasmon polariton, SPP）的线性叠加理论，在衍射区域应用Stratton-Chu模型。通过全波有限差分时域（finite-difference time-domain, FDTD）模拟进行验证。

Result: 近界面处形成具有±½类有效位点电荷的Néel型半子晶格；较大高度时边缘衍射场主导，转变为Bloch型构型。中间高度区域出现丰富的快速拓扑演化，伴随面内自旋相位中边界外涡旋-反涡旋对的成核，产生高度依赖的分数位点电荷。

Conclusion: 成功实现了等离子体自旋半子晶格的高度可控拓扑切换，揭示了近场表面等离子体激元和远场衍射机制之间的竞争与过渡，为可重构拓扑光子器件提供了理论基础。

Abstract: We demonstrate height-controlled topological switching of plasmonic spin meron lattices above a metallic square coupling structure under circularly polarized illumination. Near the interface, an evanescent surface plasmon polariton (SPP) channel yields a Néel-type meron lattice with $\pm\frac{1}{2}$ like effective site charges. At larger heights, diffracted fields from the square edges dominate and convert the lattice into a Bloch-type configuration. Over a range of intermediate heights, crossover between the evanescent SPP and edge diffraction gives rise to rich rapid topology evolutions. The switching is accompanied by nucleation of off-boundary vortex-anti vortex pairs in the in-plane spin phase, producing height-dependent fractional site charges. Our findings are analytically formulated by linear superposition of SPPs in the plasmonic regime and Stratton-Chu model in diffraction regime and confirmed via full-wave finite-difference time-domain simulations.

</details>


### [157] [Realizing anomalous Floquet non-Abelian band topology in photonic scattering networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04489)
*Yuze Hu,Mingyu Tong,Tian Jiang,Shuxing Yang,Ning Han,Fujia Chen,Li Zhang,Rui Zhao,Qiaolu Chen,Hongsheng Chen,F. Nur Ünal,Robert-Jan Slager,Yihao Yang*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 该研究首次在光子散射网络中理论证明并实验实现了二维Floquet非阿贝尔能带拓扑，揭示了远离平衡态的多能隙系统特有的拓扑现象，包括反常多能隙相、Floquet欧拉转移、带隙相中的反常狄拉克弦构型，以及Floquet诱导的能带节点非阿贝尔编织过程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多能隙拓扑（multi-gap topology）概念最近被证明能产生超越传统单能隙分类的新奇相。这些相与非阿贝尔四元数电荷（non-Abelian quaternion charges）的能带节点相关，其动量空间编织过程（momentum-space braiding processes）由欧拉类（Euler class）等新不变量表征。将这些相扩展到非平衡（non-equilibrium）体系有望解锁超越静态设置的更丰富多能隙拓扑，但由于维度、对称性和动力学控制的严格要求，其实验实现一直难以实现。

Method: 研究采用光子散射网络（photonic scattering networks）作为平台，理论证明并首次实验实现了二维Floquet非阿贝尔能带拓扑（2D Floquet non-Abelian band topology）。该平台提供了实现非平衡多能隙系统所需的维度、对称性和动力学控制能力。

Result: 在光子散射网络中发现了二维多能隙系统远离平衡态时特有的拓扑现象序列：包括由能带节点相互连接的反常多能隙相（anomalous multi-gap phases）、Floquet欧拉转移（Floquet Euler transfer）、具有反常狄拉克弦构型（anomalous Dirac string configurations）的带隙相，以及Floquet诱导的能带节点非阿贝尔编织（Floquet-induced non-Abelian braiding of band nodes）。此外，观测到了跨越多个能隙的Floquet周期反常边缘态（Floquet-periodic anomalous edge states），为这些二维多能隙Floquet拓扑相提供了实验特征。

Conclusion: 研究结果确立了光子散射网络作为实现非阿贝尔Floquet系统（non-Abelian Floquet systems）的实用且多功能途径，为具有编织能力和稳健光子功能的动态拓扑物理（dynamical topological physics）开辟了新道路。

Abstract: The concept of multi-gap topology has recently been shown to give rise to uncharted phases beyond conventional single-gap classifications. These phases relate to band nodes with non-Abelian quaternion charges and momentum-space braiding processes characterized by new invariants such as paradigmatic Euler class, phenomena that intrinsically require at least two spatial dimensions. Extending such phases into the non-equilibrium regime is predicted to unlock even richer multi-gap topologies beyond static settings, yet their experimental realization has remained elusive due to the stringent requirements on dimensionality, symmetry, and dynamical control. Here, we theoretically demonstrate and, for the first time, experimentally realize two-dimensional (2D) Floquet non-Abelian band topology in photonic scattering networks. Within this platform, we uncover a sequence of topological phenomena unique to 2D multi-gap systems far from equilibrium, including anomalous multi-gap phases interconnected by band nodes, Floquet Euler transfer, gapped phases with anomalous Dirac string configurations, and Floquet-induced non-Abelian braiding of band nodes. In addition, we observe Floquet-periodic anomalous edge states across multiple gaps, providing experimental signatures of these sought-after 2D multi-gap Floquet topological phases. Our results establish photonic scattering networks as a practical and versatile route to non-Abelian Floquet systems, opening avenues for dynamical topological physics with braiding capability and robust photonic functionalities.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Atomically thin materials exhibit electronic and optical properties distinct from their three-dimensional counterparts. For metals, particularly gold, monolayer studies remain largely unexplored due to fabrication and characterisation challenges. Here we report the first optical study of a stable quasi-freestanding gold monolayer formed by Au intercalation between graphene and SiC. Mid-infrared nanoimaging reveals plasmon-polaritons with wavelengths nearly an order of magnitude shorter than free-space light. Analysis of their dispersion using a Drude model yields a relaxation time of $τ= 18\,$fs, comparable to bulk gold, and a Drude weight of $D = 1.3\,$mS$\cdot$eV, nearly twice the bulk expectation. These results establish monolayer gold as a two-dimensional metal, opening opportunities for nanoscale photonics, plasmonics and ultra-thin electronics.

### [159] [Pulse-duration-sensitive high harmonics and attosecond locally-chiral light from a chiral topological Weyl semimetal](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05346)

Abstract: High harmonic generation (HHG) in solids results from an interplay between intraband acceleration and electron-hole recombination driven by a high-intensity laser pulse. Here, we theoretically reveal that the driving pulse duration can play a major role in extending HHG to higher photon energies by promoting higher conduction band excitations. The effect is present in a conventional semiconductor as Si, restricted in a large-gap insulator as MgO, and most prominent in RhSi, a prototypical chiral Weyl semimetal presenting numerous band crossings. Further, we elucidate the HHG selection rules in RhSi required for the synthesis of attosecond locally chiral light. The chiral crystal structure enables the generation of a local 3D electric field exhibiting an asymmetric instantaneous torsion on attosecond timescales. A pronounced circular dichroism emerges when the driving helicity is either aligned with or opposite to the crystal handedness. Our findings motivate future experiments in chiral Weyl semimetals to track high-energy band crossings and in-situ locally chiral light, paving the way for chiral compact light sources and light-wave driven topological electronics.

Method: 通过推导$so(2r)$李代数在相同和相反手征性旋量表示张量积中的分裂卡西米尔算符特征恒等式，显式构造该算符不变子空间的投影算子（projectors），并计算这些投影算子的迹（traces）。

Result: 获得了$Spin(2r)$规范群规范理论中梯形费曼图（ladder Feynman diagrams）色因子（colour factors）的显式表达式，同时得到了$so(2r)$李代数在旋量表示下杨-巴克斯特方程不变解的新形式。

Conclusion: 本文成功建立了$so(2r)$旋量表示中分裂卡西米尔算符的数学框架，为相关规范理论计算提供了精确工具，并扩展了杨-巴克斯特方程的解空间，具有理论和计算应用价值。

Abstract: In this paper, we derive characteristic identities for the split Casimir operator of the Lie algebra $so(2r)$ in tensor products of spinor representations of the same and opposite chiralities. Using these identities, we explicitly construct projectors onto invariant subspaces of this operator and compute their traces. The results obtained allow us to derive explicit expressions for the colour factors of ladder Feynman diagrams in gauge theories with gauge group $Spin(2r)$. In addition, we obtain a new form of a solution to the Yang-Baxter equation that is invariant under the action of the Lie algebra $so(2r)$ in spinor representations.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: In this article, we establish the Drinfeld correspondence between Poisson Lie groups and their infinitesimal counterparts, Lie bialgebras, in the infinite-dimensional setting. Important examples of interest include the smooth loop group $C^{\infty}(\mathbb{S}^{1}, G)$ and the analytic loop group $C^ω(\mathbb{S}^{1}, G)$ of a 1-connected real Lie group $G$, as well as $\widetilde{\mathrm{Diff}^{\infty}(M)_0}$ and $\widetilde{\mathrm{Diff}^ω(M)_0}$ -- the universal covering groups of the identity components of the groups of smooth and real-analytic diffeomorphisms of a compact manifold $M$.

### [162] [Causal Fermion Systems, Non-Commutative Geometry and Generalized Trace Dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05018)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用理论比较分析方法，系统对比三种理论的结构框架和数学方法，重点关注它们在连续极限下恢复几何结构的方式，特别是时空点之间关系的编码机制。

Conclusion: 三种理论虽然在多方面存在差异，但在连续极限的几何结构恢复上具有一致性。因果费米子系统的主要贡献在于重新定义了时空点之间关系的编码方式，这一创新具有向其他理论框架推广的潜力。

Abstract: We compare the structures and methods in the theory of causal fermion systems with generalized trace dynamics and non-commutative geometry. Although the three theories differ on many aspects, they agree in that the geometric structure to be recovered in the continuum limit is not the bare spacetime but a suitable fiber bundle. Furthermore, the comparison leads us to the conclusion that the key innovation in causal fermion systems lies in the manner in which the relation between different spacetime points is encoded. The role of Synge's classical world function $σ(x,y)$ that encodes the geodesic distance between any two points in the manifold, is taken by a generalized two-point correlator. We show that this idea can be transferred to non-commutative geometry and generalized trace dynamics.

### [164] [The Gibbs phenomenon for the Krawtchouk polynomials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05408)
*John Cullinan,Elisabeth Young*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了使用Krawtchouk多项式对符号函数进行傅里叶逼近时出现的吉布斯现象（Gibbs phenomenon），发现其与经典吉布斯常数不同，且逼近的陡度（steepness）有明确上界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在探究Krawtchouk多项式对符号函数的傅里叶逼近特性，特别关注其吉布斯现象是否与经典情况一致，以及逼近陡度随多项式次数增加的变化规律。

Method: 通过分析Krawtchouk多项式构建的傅里叶逼近$\mathcal{F}_N$，研究符号函数的逼近特性。方法包括数值证据展示和严格的数学证明。

Result: 数值证据表明Krawtchouk多项式逼近的吉布斯现象不同于经典吉布斯常数。严格证明了逼近陡度$\mathcal{F}_N'(0)$的极限为$\log 4$，即$\lim_{N \to \infty} \mathcal{F}_N'(0) = \log 4$。

Conclusion: Krawtchouk多项式对符号函数的傅里叶逼近展现出与经典正交多项式不同的特性：吉布斯现象有别于经典常数，且逼近陡度有明确上界而非无界增长。

Abstract: We study the Fourier approximation $\mathcal{F}_N$ of the sign function by the Krawtchouk polynomials. We give numerical evidence that the Gibbs phenomenon of the approximation differs from the classical Gibbs constant; this is in contrast to other families of orthogonal polynomials. We also show that the steepness $\mathcal{F}_N'(0)$ of the approximation is bounded by explicitly proving $\lim_{N \to \infty} \mathcal{F}_N'(0) = \log 4$. This is also in contrast to approximations by classical orthogonal polynomials, where the steepness has been shown to be unbounded as the degree increases.

# cond-mat.quant-gas [[Back]](#toc)

### [165] [Chiral and pair superfluidity in triangular ladder produced by state-dependent Kronig-Penney lattice](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04498)
*Domantas Burba,Giedrius Žlabys,Dzmitry Viarbitski,Thomas Busch,Gediminas Juzeliūnas*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种用于超冷原子的三角梯子（triangular ladder）实现方案，该系统同时具备几何阻挫（geometric frustration）和可控的双体相互作用，特别是配对隧穿（pair hopping）和密度诱导隧穿（density-induced tunneling）。通过密度矩阵重整化群（DMRG）计算，发现了配对超流（pair superfluid）和手性超流（chiral superfluid）等量子相。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在实现一个同时具备几何阻挫和可控双体相互作用的超冷原子系统，特别是要实现对配对隧穿和密度诱导隧穿的控制。这种系统为研究强关联量子多体物理提供了新的平台。

Method: 通过自旋依赖的Kronig-Penney晶格（spin-dependent Kronig-Penney lattice）实现三角梯子结构，该晶格利用空间依赖的三脚架型（tripod-type）原子-光耦合创建。采用密度矩阵重整化群（DMRG）计算推导量子相图。

Result: 配对隧穿稳定了具有配对关联幂律衰减特征的配对超流（pair superfluid）。由最近邻（NN）和次近邻（NNN）隧穿竞争引起的阻挫导致了手性超流（chiral superfluid）的出现。在高势垒区域，系统可映射到XXZ自旋模型，并找到了精确的相变点。

Conclusion: 该工作提出了一种实现具有几何阻挫和可控相互作用的三角梯子超冷原子系统的具体方案，发现了包括配对超流和手性超流在内的丰富量子相，为探索强关联量子多体物理提供了新平台。

Abstract: We propose a concrete realization of a triangular ladder for ultracold atoms, which simultaneously hosts geometric frustration and unusual two-body interactions, and in particular controllable pair hopping and density-induced tunneling. This is done by means of a spin-dependent Kronig-Penney lattice created using a spatially-dependent tripod-type atom-light coupling. We apply density matrix renormalization group (DMRG) calculations to derive the quantum phase diagram. We find that pair tunneling stabilizes a robust pair superfluid, characterized by power-law decay of pair correlations. Additionally, a chiral superfluid arises from frustration induced by competing nearest neighbor (NN) and next-nearest neighbor (NNN) tunnelings. Finally, in the high barrier regime, we map our system onto the XXZ spin model and find the exact phase transition points.

</details>


### [166] [Layering and superfluidity of soft-core bosons in shallow spherical traps](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04650)
*Fabio Cinti,Matteo Ciardi,Santi Prestipino,Giuseppe Pellicane*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 该研究通过蒙特卡洛模拟分析了球形对称弱囚禁势中软核玻色子的奇特结构，发现粒子在特定参数下会形成具有二十面体对称性的壳层簇结构，随着粒子数增加会形成第二个同心壳层，呈现出十二面体图案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多体物理的基础理论和模型可以通过超冷原子实验进行探测，其中弯曲囚禁系统特别值得关注，因为它们能够产生在平直空间中无法获得的奇异物质态。本研究聚焦于曲率效应更强的相对小样本系统。

Method: 采用蒙特卡洛模拟（Monte Carlo simulations）方法，分析球形对称弱囚禁势中软核玻色子（soft-core bosons）的组装结构，通过适当调节参数研究粒子在弯曲空间中的排列行为。

Result: 约百个粒子在特定参数下会形成具有二十面体对称性（icosahedral symmetry）的壳层簇结构；随着粒子数增加，会逐渐形成第二个同心壳层，与原始壳层部分重叠且完美对应，形成十二面体图案（dodecahedral pattern）。不同参数下观察到其他多面体对称性的簇排列。

Conclusion: 低温下超流密度在径向方向不均匀；加热系统时，超流性在簇结构仍然存在的情况下逐渐消失，这种行为类似于平面上从超固态到正常固态的转变。这些行为原则上可以在装载到气泡阱中的里德伯修饰原子系统中进行测试。

Abstract: Fundamental theories and models of many-body physics can be probed in experiments on ultracold atoms held in place by electromagnetic fields. In particular, of considerable interest are systems under curved confinement, since they can yield exotic states of matter which would be impossible to obtain in flat space. In this study we focus on relatively small samples, where curvature effects are stronger, and analyze by Monte Carlo simulations the peculiar structure arising in an assembly of soft-core bosons subject to a weak trapping potential with spherical symmetry. Upon suitable tuning of the parameters, a hundred particles or so group together in clusters arranged in a shell with icosahedral symmetry. As the number of particles increases, a second shell gradually develops, concentric to (and partly overlapping with) the original one, where clusters are in perfect registry with the first shell, thus forming a dodecahedral pattern. Cluster arrangements with the symmetry of other polyhedra are seen for different sets of parameters. At low temperature the superfluid density is non-uniform in the radial direction; heating the system progressively, superfluidity eventually vanishes while still clusters are present, a behavior resembling the transition from supersolid to normal solid on a plane. Two shells of clusters are also observed in systems of classical or distinguishable quantum particles, but in those cases the shells are more fragile to thermal fluctuations. All these behaviors can in principle be tested in systems of Rydberg-dressed atoms loaded into a bubble trap.

</details>


### [167] [Efficient simulation of Bose-Einstein condensates in nontrivial topologies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05447)
*Abel Beregi,Jean-Baptiste Gerent,Nathan Lundblad*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种针对空心薄壳玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体（BEC）的高效有限差分模拟框架，通过半结构化网格的选择性空间采样，相比传统方法实现了超过一个数量级的计算性能提升，并应用于微重力环境下气泡形BEC形成的可行性评估。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 气泡形玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体（Bose-Einstein condensates, BECs）具有独特的空心薄壳几何结构，支持与紧凑型凝聚体截然不同的多种现象。然而，由于其固有的三维结构和极端纵横比，对此类系统的数值模拟具有特别的挑战性。

Method: 提出了一种高效的有限差分模拟框架，专门用于求解此类非平凡拓扑结构中的偏微分方程。该方法通过在半结构化网格上采用选择性空间采样，显著降低了内存使用，并实现了超过一个数量级的计算性能提升。该算法天然适用于GPU上的高度并行执行。

Result: 将该框架应用于模拟通过受控空心化协议形成气泡BEC的过程，使用了与国际空间站上冷原子实验室相关的从头算（ab initio）囚禁势。从这些模拟中，识别出了实现绝热演化所需的特征时间尺度和参数斜坡。

Conclusion: 通过该模拟框架评估了在微重力环境下实验实现气泡形凝聚体的可行性，为薄壳凝聚体的大规模时间依赖模拟提供了高效的计算工具。

Abstract: Bubble-shaped Bose-Einstein condensates (BECs) constitute a unique class of quantum fluids with a hollow, thin-shell geometry that supports a wide variety of phenomena that are distinct from those of compact condensates. Numerical simulation of such systems is particularly challenging due to their inherently three-dimensional structure and extreme aspect ratios. We present an efficient finite-difference simulation framework designed for solving partial differential equations in such nontrivial topologies with a focus on the static and dynamical modeling of bubble-shaped BECs. By employing selective spatial sampling on a semi-structured grid, our method substantially reduces memory usage and achieves more than an order-of-magnitude improvement in computational performance compared to conventional split-step Fourier solvers. The algorithm is naturally extendable for highly parallel execution on GPUs, enabling large-scale, time-dependent simulations of thin-shell condensates. We apply this framework to simulate the formation of bubble BECs through a controlled hollowing-out protocol using ab initio trapping potentials relevant to the Cold Atom Laboratory aboard the International Space Station. From these simulations, we identify characteristic timescales and parameter ramps required to achieve adiabatic evolution, thereby assessing the feasibility of experimentally realizing bubble-shaped condensates in microgravity environments.

</details>


### [168] [Spin-resolved microscopy of $^{87}$Sr SU($N$) Fermi-Hubbard systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05478)
*Carlos Gas-Ferrer,Antonio Rubio-Abadal,Sandra Buob,Leonardo Bezzo,Jonatan Höschele,Leticia Tarruell*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文报道了基于锶-87原子的量子气体显微镜（quantum-gas microscope）实现，该技术通过窄线宽689 nm跃迁实现自旋分辨单原子探测，能够同时测量10个自旋态，为研究SU(N)费米-哈伯德模型中的奇异磁性提供了关键工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子气体显微镜虽然已能直接观测哈伯德模型的相，但SU(N)量子系统的微观探索仍然难以实现。碱土金属类费米子通过实现更高对称性提供了研究SU(N)哈伯德模型的机会，这些模型具有丰富的相图有待揭示。

Method: 基于锶-87原子，利用689 nm窄线宽跃迁（intercombination line）的冷却和荧光成像方案，实现自旋分辨单原子探测。通过自旋选择性光泵浦协议（spin-selective optical pumping protocol），在单次实验中确定所有10个自旋态的占据情况。

Result: 成功实现了锶-87量子气体显微镜，能够观测单个粒子在整个自旋-9/2基态流形中的拉莫尔进动（Larmor precession），验证了方法的有效性。该技术为探测格点分辨的磁关联提供了关键能力。

Conclusion: 锶-87量子气体显微镜为研究SU(N)费米-哈伯德模型中的奇异磁性提供了强大方法，同时为量子模拟、计算和计量学研究提供了新的探测工具。

Abstract: Quantum-gas microscopes provide direct access to the phases of the Hubbard model, bringing microscopic insight into the complex competition between interactions, SU(2) magnetism, and doping. Alkaline-earth(-like) fermions extend this spin-1/2 paradigm by realizing higher symmetries and giving access to SU(N) Hubbard models, with rich phase diagrams to be unveiled. Despite its fundamental interest, a microscopic exploration of SU(N) quantum systems has remained elusive. Here we report the realization of a quantum-gas microscope for fermionic $^{87}$Sr. Our imaging scheme, based on cooling and fluorescence on the narrow intercombination line at 689 nm, enables spin-resolved single-atom detection. By implementing a spin-selective optical pumping protocol, we determine the occupation of each of the 10 spin states in a single experimental realization, a crucial capability for probing site-resolved magnetic correlations. We benchmark our method by observing single-particle Larmor precession across the full spin-9/2 ground-state manifold. These results establish $^{87}$Sr quantum-gas microscopy as a powerful approach to study exotic magnetism in the SU(N) Fermi-Hubbard model, and provide a new detection tool for studies in quantum simulation, computation, and metrology.

</details>


### [169] [Core-bound waves on a Gross-Pitaevskii vortex](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05505)
*Evan Papoutsis,Nathan Apfel,Nir Navon*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 该研究发现了Gross-Pitaevskii涡旋中两类难以捉摸的核心束缚激发模式——变径波（轴对称）和槽纹波（四极子）的色散关系，揭示了这些涡旋特异性激发在短波长极限下表现为径向束缚粒子，在长波长极限下具有不同的解耦行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在揭示Gross-Pitaevskii涡旋中两类难以捉摸的核心束缚激发模式——变径波（varicose waves）和槽纹波（fluting waves）的色散关系，这些激发模式在涡旋动力学中具有重要意义但尚未被充分理解。

Method: 通过分析Gross-Pitaevskii方程，研究变径波（轴对称）和槽纹波（四极子）这两种涡旋特异性激发的色散关系，并在短波长和长波长极限下进行理论解释，最后通过Gross-Pitaevskii方程的直接数值模拟验证所提出的光谱学方案。

Result: 在愈合长度量级的波长下，变径波、槽纹波以及已知的Kelvin波都拥有无限序列的核心束缚分支，其能量低于Bogoliubov色散关系。短波长极限下这些激发可解释为径向束缚于涡旋的粒子；长波长极限下槽纹波从核心解耦，变径波简化为沿涡旋传播的声子，而基本Kelvin波成为唯一的涡旋特异性核心束缚激发。

Conclusion: 研究成功揭示了Gross-Pitaevskii涡旋中变径波和槽纹波的完整色散关系，提出了创建和探测变径波的现实光谱学方案，并通过数值模拟验证了该方案的有效性，深化了对涡旋特异性激发的理解。

Abstract: We find the dispersion relations of two elusive families of core-bound excitations of the Gross-Pitaevskii (GP) vortex, varicose (axisymmetric) and fluting (quadrupole) waves. For wavelengths of order the healing length, these two families -- and the well-known Kelvin wave -- possess an infinite sequence of core-bound, vortex-specific branches whose energies lie below the Bogoliubov dispersion relation. In the short-wavelength limit, these excitations can be interpreted as particles radially bound to the vortex, which acts as a waveguide. In the long-wavelength limit, the fluting waves unbind from the core, the varicose waves reduce to phonons propagating along the vortex, and the fundamental Kelvin wave is the only core-bound vortex-specific excitation. Finally, we propose a realistic spectroscopic protocol for creating and detecting the varicose wave, which we test by direct numerical simulations of the GP equation.

</details>

### [170] [The Extra Vanishing Structure and Nonlinear Stability of Multi-Dimensional Rarefaction Waves: The Geometric Weighted Energy Estimates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05332)
*Haoran He,Qichen He*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文首次建立了理想气体可压缩欧拉方程中多维稀疏波的非线性稳定性，证明了小扰动初始数据存在收敛于背景稀疏波的全局解，克服了因稀疏波前特征性质导致的导数损失问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究多维气体动力学中不连续奇点通过稀疏波（rarefaction waves）的解析机制。虽然一维情况已得到充分理解，但自Majda提出以来，高维情况的严格构造一直是未解决的开放问题，主要由于稀疏波前的特征性质导致线性化估计中的导数损失。

Method: 采用创新的几何加权能量方法（Geometric Weighted Energy Method, GWEM），该方法能在标准Sobolev空间中实现无导数损失的能量估计。关键是通过声学度量（acoustical metric）对稀疏波前进行详细几何描述，识别出特征速度高阶导数中的隐藏额外消失结构。

Result: 证明了对于$H^s$空间（$s > s_c$）中平面稀疏波的小扰动初始数据，存在唯一的全局解，且该解渐近收敛于背景稀疏波。这是系列论文中的首篇，提供了关键的先验能量界。

Conclusion: 本文首次建立了多维稀疏波的非线性稳定性，克服了先前Nash-Moser方案的局限性。解的存在性及在多维黎曼问题（Riemann problem）中的应用将在后续论文中讨论。

Abstract: We study the resolution of discontinuous singularities in gas dynamics via multi-dimensional rarefaction waves. While the mechanism is well-understood in one spatial dimension, the rigorous construction in higher dimensions has remained a challenging open problem since Majda's proposal, primarily due to the characteristic nature of rarefaction fronts which leads to derivative losses in linearized estimates. In this paper, we establish the nonlinear stability of multi-dimensional rarefaction waves for the compressible Euler equations with ideal gas law. We prove that for initial data being small perturbations of the planar rarefaction wave in $H^s$ ($s > s_c$), there exists a unique global solution that converges asymptotically to the background rarefaction wave as $t \to \infty$. Our proof relies on a novel Geometric Weighted Energy Method (GWEM), which yields stable energy estimates without loss of derivatives in standard Sobolev spaces, overcoming the limitations of previous Nash-Moser schemes. A key ingredient is a detailed geometric description of the rarefaction wave fronts via the acoustical metric, where we identify a hidden extra vanishing structure in the top-order derivatives of the characteristic speed. This is the first paper in a series, providing the crucial a priori energy bounds. The existence of solutions and applications to the multi-dimensional Riemann problem will be addressed in the forthcoming companion paper.

</details>


### [171] [Well-posedness of the heat equation in domains with topological transitions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05403)
*Maxim Olshanskii,Arnold Reusken*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 该研究分析了在可能发生拓扑转变的演化域中的线性抛物方程，通过引入各向异性时空函数空间，建立了弱解的存在性、唯一性和先验估计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于分析拓扑结构可能发生变化的演化域中的线性抛物方程，这类问题在圆柱形域的传统方法中难以处理，特别是当域发生分裂、合并或孔洞生成/消失等拓扑转变时。

Method: 方法包括：将演化域描述为光滑时空水平集函数（smooth space-time level set function）的子水平集；引入各向异性时空函数空间（anisotropic space-time function spaces），扩展了圆柱形域中使用的经典Bochner空间；应用Babuška-Banach定理建立弱解理论。

Result: 主要结果包括：建立了各向异性时空函数空间的关键泛函分析性质，如紧支光滑函数的稠密性；证明了对于由具有孤立非退化临界点的水平集函数生成的域演化，弱解的存在性、唯一性和先验估计。

Conclusion: 该分析框架适用于由水平集函数生成的域演化，这些函数具有孤立非退化临界点，对应于Morse理论在二维和三维空间中对一般拓扑变化的分类，为处理拓扑转变的演化域中的偏微分方程提供了理论基础。

Abstract: We analyze a linear parabolic equation with homogeneous Dirichlet boundary conditions posed in domains whose evolution may involve topological transitions. The domains are described as sublevel sets of a smooth space-time level set function, allowing for transitions such as domain splitting and merging and the creation or vanishing of islands and holes. We introduce anisotropic space-time function spaces that extend the classical Bochner spaces used in cylindrical domains and establish key functional-analytic properties of these spaces, including the density of compactly supported smooth functions. This framework enables the application of the Babuška-Banach theorem, yielding existence, uniqueness, and a priori estimates for weak solutions. The analysis applies to domain evolutions generated by level set functions with isolated nondegenerate critical points, which correspond to the generic topology changes classified by Morse theory in two and three spatial dimensions.

</details>

### [172] [Sensitivity of a closed dielectric haloscope to axion dark matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05006)
*A. Ivanov,D. Leppla-Weber,B. Ary dos Santos Garcia,D. Bergermann,H. Byun,A. Caldwell,V. Dabhi,C. Diaconu,J. Diehl,G. Dvali,B. Döbrich,J. Egge,E. Garutti,S. Heyminck,T. Houdy,F. Hubaut,J. Jochum,A. Kazemipour,Y. Kermaidic,S. Knirck,M. Kramer,D. Kreikemeyer-Lorenzo,C. Krieger,C. Lee,X. Li,A. Lindner,B. Majorovits,J. Maldonado,A. Martini,A. Miyazaki,E. Öz,P. Pralavorio,G. Raffelt,J. Redondo,A. Ringwald,J. Schaffran,A. Schmidt,L. Stankewitz,F. Steffen,C. Strandhagen,I. Usherov,H. Wang,G. Wieching*

Main category: astro-ph.IM

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种确定封闭式介电晕镜（dielectric haloscope）对轴子暗物质（axion dark matter）灵敏度的简化模型，该模型能够以最小计算资源描述实验灵敏度，并应用于MADMAX原型实验数据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 介电晕镜旨在探测理论上备受关注的轴子质量范围（~26 μeV至~500 μeV），但大规模设计导致模拟计算成本高昂且耗时。因此需要开发一种简化模型来高效确定实验灵敏度。

Method: 提出一个能够描述封闭式介电晕镜电磁响应的简单模型，该模型考虑了实际几何缺陷以及接收系统引入的噪声，并应用于CERN的1.6 T Morpurgo磁体中MADMAX原型实验所采集的数据。

Result: 该模型能够以最小计算资源确定实验灵敏度，支撑了首次使用介电晕镜进行的轴子暗物质搜索，并为未来MADMAX暗物质搜索奠定了基础。

Conclusion: 该简化模型为介电晕镜实验的灵敏度分析提供了高效的计算工具，成功应用于MADMAX原型实验，标志着介电晕镜技术在轴子暗物质探测领域的首次应用实践。

Abstract: We present a method to determine the sensitivity of a closed dielectric haloscope to axion dark matter. Dielectric haloscopes aim to probe the theoretically well-motivated axion mass range of ~26 $\mathrmμ$eV to ~500 $\mathrmμ$eV by utilizing a stack of dielectric disks and a mirror to enhance the axion-photon conversion within an external magnetic field. Their conversion volume is nearly axion-mass independent, thereby favoring large-scale designs to increase sensitivity. The large volume causes simulations to be computationally expensive and time-consuming. This paper presents a simple model that can be used to determine the sensitivity of the experiment with minimal computational resources. The model is able to describe the electromagnetic response of a closed dielectric haloscope, accounting for realistic geometric imperfections, as well as the noise introduced by the receiver system. It is applied to data taken with a MAgnetized Disk and Mirror Axion Experiment (MADMAX) prototype within the 1.6 T Morpurgo magnet at CERN. This work underpins the first axion dark matter search using a dielectric haloscope and provides the foundation for future dark matter searches with MADMAX.

</details>


### [173] [Parameter estimation of eccentric massive black hole binaries with LISA and its cosmological implications](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04462)
*Jia-Hao Zhong,Jin-Zhao Yang,Tao Yang,Xu-Heng Ding,Xi-Long Fan,Kai Liao,Bei You*

Main category: astro-ph.IM

TL;DR: 该研究分析了轨道偏心率（eccentricity）对LISA探测大质量黑洞双星（MBHBs）参数估计和宇宙学约束的影响，发现偏心率能显著提升定位精度和距离推断，从而增加明亮标准汽笛（bright sirens）数量并改善宇宙学参数测量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 未来空间引力波（GW）观测站如LISA将探测大质量黑洞双星（MBHBs），这些源通常伴随电磁对应体，可作为明亮标准汽笛（bright sirens）用于宇宙学研究。轨道偏心率（eccentricity）能显著改善引力波参数估计，因为偏心率诱导的多重谐波提供额外信息并有助于打破波形参数间的简并性。

Method: 使用EccentricFD波形模型，在三种群体模型（popIII、Q3d和Q3nod）下构建LISA的5年引力波事件目录。分析初始偏心率e₀=0.4在10⁻⁴ Hz频率下对参数估计的影响。

Result: 偏心率显著改善天空定位和距离推断，最佳情况下提升约10倍。明亮标准汽笛数量大幅增加：popIII模型从8增至11，Q3d从6增至12，Q3nod从13增至24。在ΛCDM模型中，Q3d模型的H₀相对不确定度从8.17%降至4.35%，改善约47%。结合最新宇宙微波背景数据，对暗能量状态方程和修正引力波传播的约束也得到改善。

Conclusion: 偏心率是引力波探测和参数估计中极为重要的特征，能够使未来空间观测站实现更精确的宇宙测量。该研究证明了考虑轨道偏心率对提升宇宙学约束能力的关键作用。

Abstract: Future space-based gravitational wave (GW) observatories such as LISA will detect massive black hole binaries (MBHBs), which are expected to be accompanied by electromagnetic counterparts, thereby providing bright standard sirens for cosmology. The orbital eccentricity of MBHBs can significantly improve the parameter estimation of GWs because the multiple harmonics induced by eccentricity provide additional information and help break down the degeneracies among waveform parameters. In this paper, we use the EccentricFD waveform and construct 5-year GW event catalogs for LISA under three population models (popIII, Q3d and Q3nod). For the three models, we find that an initial eccentricity of $e_0=0.4$ at $10^{-4}$ Hz yields improvements in sky localization and distance inference by a factor of $\mathcal{O}(10)$ in the best cases. As a consequence, the average number of bright sirens increases substantially: from 8 to 11 (PopIII), 6 to 12 (Q3d) and 13 to 24 (Q3nod). This increase in event number, together with enhanced localization and distance inference, leads to tighter cosmological constraints. In the $Λ$CDM model, for instance, the relative uncertainty on $H_0$ is reduced from $8.17\%$ to $4.35\%$ for the Q3d model, corresponding to an improvement of approximately $47\%$. We also investigate the improvement in constraints on the dark energy equation of state and modified GW propagation when combining bright sirens with the latest cosmic microwave background data. These results demonstrate that eccentricity is a remarkably significant feature in GW detection and parameter estimation, enabling more accurate measurements of the Universe with future space-based observatories.

</details>
