### [174] [Crunching, Bouncing, and Cyclical Cosmologies from Dark Sector Interactions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02332)
*Marcel van der Westhuizen,Amare Abebe*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文提出在广义相对论框架下，通过暗物质（DM）与暗能量（DE）之间的非引力相互作用，可在平坦FLRW宇宙学中产生未来大坍缩（Big Crunch）或过去非奇异反弹（non-singular bounce）的新机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索相互作用暗能量（IDE）模型中未被充分研究的参数区域，特别是强相互作用区域，这些区域可能产生奇异的宇宙学行为，如宇宙转折点（turnarounds）。

Method: 采用基于线性核（linear kernels）$Q = 3H(δ_{\rm dm}ρ_{\rm dm} + δ_{\rm de}ρ_{\rm de})$的唯象相互作用暗能量（IDE）模型，重点研究暗能量向暗物质强能量转移的参数机制，其中相互作用在某一组分密度为零时不消失。

Result: 在强相互作用机制下，暗区（dark-sector）密度可变为负值，导致平坦宇宙中宇宙学转折点所需能量条件被违反，从而产生最大尺度因子（maximum scale factor）后坍缩为大坍缩，或最小非零尺度因子（minimum non-zero scale factor）对应的反弹；在闭合宇宙中，同一IDE框架的特殊情况可调谐为循环场景（cyclic scenario）。

Conclusion: 虽然这些强相互作用场景不太可能描述观测到的宇宙，但它们具体证明了在熟悉的IDE模型参数空间中未被充分探索的区域可以自然地产生奇异的宇宙学行为。

Abstract: We present new mechanisms that produce either a future Big Crunch turnaround or a past non-singular bounce in flat FLRW cosmologies within general relativity at the background level, driven solely by non-gravitational interactions between dark matter (DM) and dark energy (DE). We study phenomenological interacting dark energy (IDE) models based on linear kernels of the form $Q = 3H(δ_{\rm dm}ρ_{\rm dm} + δ_{\rm de}ρ_{\rm de})$, focusing on parameter regimes with strong energy transfer from dark energy to dark matter. In this strong interacting regime, the interaction does not vanish when one component crosses zero density, allowing one of the dark-sector densities to become negative. The resulting sign changes can violate the energy conditions required for cosmological turnarounds in a flat universe, thereby enabling either (i) a maximum scale factor followed by recollapse into a big crunch, or (ii) a minimum non-zero scale factor corresponding to a bounce. We derive analytic conditions for these turnarounds and obtain closed-form expressions for the associated maximum or minimum scale factor. We also show that, in a closed universe, a special case of the same IDE framework can be tuned to yield a cyclic scenario. Although these strong interaction scenarios are unlikely to describe the observed Universe, they provide a concrete demonstration that exotic cosmological behaviour can arise naturally in underexplored regions of the parameter space of familiar IDE models.

</details>


### [175] [Probing Dark Energy on the Moon](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04841)
*Alfredo Gurrola,Robert J. Scherrer,Oem Trivedi*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 该研究提出利用月球激光干涉仪测量视界尺度度规涨落，直接探测暗能量有效场论（EFT）的动力学部分，为暗能量和修改引力模型提供新的观测约束手段。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 暗能量有效场论（effective field theory, EFT）为描述宇宙加速膨胀提供了模型无关的框架，但其许多定义算符受现有观测的约束较弱。需要新的观测手段来直接探测暗能量EFT的动力学部分，而不仅仅是背景膨胀历史。

Method: 通过月球激光干涉仪（lunar laser interferometer）测量视界尺度（horizon-scale）的度规涨落（metric fluctuations），直接探测暗能量EFT的动力学部分。该方法特别关注EFT动力学系数M₂⁴和相关的暗能量声速（sound speed）c_s²。

Result: 该方法能够敏感地探测EFT动力学系数M₂⁴和暗能量声速c_s²，为晚期加速膨胀模型的微观物理一致性条件提供了全新的观测手段。这允许对EFT参数空间的广泛区域进行探测、约束或潜在发现。

Conclusion: 月球激光干涉仪测量视界尺度度规涨落的方法，为暗能量有效场论动力学部分的直接探测建立了定性上全新的观测手段，能够约束标量扰动动力学算符，超越仅依赖背景膨胀历史的传统约束方法。

Abstract: The effective field theory (EFT) of cosmic acceleration provides a model-independent framework for describing dark energy and modified gravity, yet many of its defining operators remain weakly constrained by existing observations. We show that measurements of horizon-scale metric fluctuations with a lunar laser interferometer can directly probe the kinetic sector of the EFT of dark energy, enabling constraints on operators governing scalar perturbation dynamics rather than only the background expansion history. In particular, we demonstrate sensitivity to the EFT kinetic coefficient $M_2^4$ and the associated sound speed of dark energy, $c_s^2$. This establishes a qualitatively new observational handle on the microphysical consistency conditions of late-time acceleration models, allowing broad regions of EFT parameter space to be probed, constrained, or potentially discovered.

</details>


### [176] [STOchastic LAttice Simulation of hybrid inflation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04850)
*Tomoaki Murata,Yuichiro Tada*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 该研究通过晶格模拟分析多瀑布场混合暴胀模型中曲率扰动的空间分布特征，发现拓扑缺陷在暴胀期间被随机噪声重新连接成更精细结构，且曲率扰动的全局结构为早期宇宙物理提供了新的探测手段。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在分析多瀑布场混合暴胀模型（multi-waterfall hybrid inflation models）中产生的曲率扰动的空间分布特征，这些模型已知会产生各种拓扑缺陷（topological defects）。

Method: 使用基于暴胀随机形式（stochastic formalism of inflation）的晶格模拟代码STOLAS，通过改变瀑布场数量n和暴胀子势能函数形式（"二次型"和"三次型"）来分析六个案例，并采用欧拉特征（Euler characteristic）作为拓扑诊断工具。

Result: 概率密度函数和功率谱与随机-δN算法基本一致；"三次型"案例在PDF中存在特征性上界，抑制原初黑洞形成但可能影响晕形成；拓扑缺陷在暴胀期间被随机噪声重新连接成更精细结构，使其关联长度远小于瀑布相变临界点处的哈勃尺度；曲率扰动在n=1时表现出全局结构。

Conclusion: 曲率扰动的全局结构为早期宇宙物理提供了新颖的探测手段，尽管对于n=1的情况，尚不能确定这些结构是否完全由畴壁引起，因为弦和单极子并未留下类似结构。

Abstract: We investigate the spatial profile of the curvature perturbation generated in multi-waterfall hybrid inflation models, which are known to produce various topological defects. Using the lattice simulation code \acl{STOLAS}, based on the stochastic formalism of inflation, we analyse six cases by varying the number of waterfall fields $n$ and the functional form of the inflaton potential (``Quadratic'' and ``Cubic'' cases). Our statistical analysis shows that the \acp{PDF} and power spectra are broadly consistent with the so-called stochastic-$δN$ algorithm. The ``Cubic'' case also exhibits a characteristic upper bound in the \ac{PDF}, as discovered in our previous work, that suppresses \acl{PBH} formation while potentially affecting halo formation. Furthermore, we employ the Euler characteristic as a topological diagnostic tool to identify the structures of the waterfall fields as well as the curvature perturbation. We find that the topological defects, such as domain walls ($n=1$), cosmic strings ($n=2$), and monopoles ($n=3$), are reconnected during inflation into finer structures by the stochastic noise, making their correlation lengths much smaller than the Hubble scale at the critical point of the waterfall phase transition counterintuitively. The Euler characteristic also implies global structures of the curvature perturbation for $n=1$, though we do not conclude if they are due to the domain wall, because neither the strings ($n=2$) nor monopoles ($n=3$) leave such structures. The global structures of the curvature perturbation will provide a novel probe for the physics of the early universe.

</details>


### [177] [Reassessing the SIGW Interpretation of PTA Signal: The Role of Third-Order Gravitational Waves and Implications for the PBH Overproduction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05191)
*Zhi-Chao Zhao,Sai Wang,Qing-Hua Zhu,Xin Zhang*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 该研究通过将标量诱导引力波（SIGW）框架扩展至三阶引力波，增强了SIGW的谱振幅，从而缓解了脉冲星计时阵列（PTA）信号解释中存在的原初黑洞（PBH）过量产生问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近期将脉冲星计时阵列（PTA）信号解释为早期宇宙线性宇宙学曲率扰动诱导的二阶引力波，这导致了原初黑洞（PBH）的过量产生问题，形成了理论上的张力。本研究旨在通过扩展标量诱导引力波（SIGW）框架来解决这一矛盾。

Method: 研究将标量诱导引力波（SIGW）框架扩展至包含三阶引力波，从而显著增强SIGW的谱振幅。方法上结合了宇宙微波背景（CMB）和重子声学振荡（BAO）的联合数据集，推导了宇宙学引力波物理能量密度分数的约束，并进一步纳入PTA数据来约束SIGW的谱振幅和峰值频率。

Result: 分析结果表明，数据组合偏好的参数区域能在一定程度上缓解原初黑洞（PBH）过量产生问题，从而支持了该模型的理论一致性。此外，通过将分析扩展至包含超大质量黑洞双星产生的引力波背景，研究证实了SIGW对PTA信号解释的稳健性。

Conclusion: 该研究通过引入三阶引力波增强了标量诱导引力波（SIGW）框架，为解决PTA信号解释中的PBH过量产生问题提供了理论途径。这些发现有望通过未来高精度观测得到进一步验证。

Abstract: In light of recent interpretations attributing pulsar timing array (PTA) signal to second-order gravitational waves induced by linear cosmological curvature perturbations in the early universe, the overproduction of primordial black holes (PBHs) poses a theoretical tension. In this work, we address this issue through extending such a scalar-induced gravitational wave (SIGW) framework to include third-order gravitational waves, which allow for a substantial enhancement in the spectral amplitude of SIGWs. Analyzing a combined dataset from cosmic microwave background and baryon acoustic oscillations, we derive cosmological constraints on the physical energy-density fraction of cosmological gravitational waves. Further incorporating PTA data, we obtain constraints on the spectral amplitude and peak frequency of SIGWs. Our results indicate that the parameter region favored by the data combination can to some extent alleviate the PBH overproduction problem, thereby supporting the theoretical consistency of our model. Furthermore, we demonstrate the robustness of our SIGW interpretation for the PTA signal by extending the analysis to include a gravitational wave background from supermassive black hole binaries. These findings are poised for further scrutiny with future high-precision observations.

</details>
